Making	sure	you	have	great	body	language	when	you	approach	is	also	key.
You	 want	 to	 keep	 your	 head	 up,	 shoulders	 back	 (not	 slouched),	 chest	 out,	 and
eyes	 ahead.	 This	 demonstrates	 a	 confident	 personality,	 and	 speaks	 volumes
before	 any	 word	 is	 even	 uttered.	 In	 fact,	 great	 body	 language	 alone	 can	 easily
attract	 a	 woman	 and	 be	 the	 deciding	 factor	 for	 a	 successful	 approach.	 It’s
imperative	that	you	do	not	exhibit	weak	body	language.	Even	if	you	feel	like	a
complete	loser,	and	at	your	very	worst,	try	your	best	to	keep	good	posture.	After
all,	this	sub-communication	is	a	great	majority	of	your	overall	presentation.

Eye	contact	goes	hand-in-hand	with	body	language.	After	you	stop	her	and
lock	 eyes	 on	 her,	 you	 want	 to	 keep	 a	 good,	 solid,	 steady	 gaze.	 Looking	 away
when	she	stares	at	you	shows	a	lot	of	weakness	on	your	part,	so	don’t	do	it.	By
staring	 back	 at	 her	 consistently,	 right	 into	 her	 eyes,	 you	 tell	 her	 unconsciously
that	you	are	a	powerful	man.	You	tell	her	you	can	take	control	of	situations,	and
that	 you	 stand	 by	 what	 you	 are	 saying	 (and	 doing).	 If	 you	 say	 something	 and
then	look	away	right	after	saying	it	(perhaps	it	was	something	edgy	you	wanted
to	try	telling	her),	you	clearly	demonstrate	that	you	don’t	stand	by	your	words.

It’s	 like	 an	 obvious	 poker	 bluff,	 where	 you	 boldly	 push	 all	 your	 chips	 into
the	center	in	an	attempt	to	display	a	strong	hand,	but	then	look	down	and	guard
your	cards	very	closely	the	second	your	fingers	let	go	of	those	chips.	You	protect
those	 cards,	 fearing	 that	 someone	 might	 accidentally	 see	 the	 truth	 behind	 your
play:	that	dud	hand	you've	so	brashly	bet	all	your	money	on.

The	same	thing	goes	here.	By	looking	away	from	the	woman,	you	fear	that
she	 might	 actually	 look	 right	 through	 you,	 even	 to	 your	 soul,	 and	 see	 the	 fake
confidence	that	you've	displayed	to	her.	Then	she	might	see	the	truth	and	realize
that	you’re	not	really	this	cool,	confident	guy	you	pretend	to	be.

Just	by	keeping	your	eyes	on	hers,	looking	right	at	her	and	not	away	when
you	 say	 something,	 you	 demonstrate	 a	 tremendous	 amount	 of	 confidence	 and
value.	Again,	even	if	you’re	not	feeling	spectacular,	and	you	want	to	look	away,
do	your	best	not	to.	It	pays	off	to	suck	it	up	and	stay	in	there.

By	 having	 good	 eye	 contact,	 I	 do	 mean	 to	 keep	 a	 good	 eye	 gaze	 on	 her.
However,	don’t	take	this	to	mean	your	eyes	must	be	locked	on	hers,	throughout
every	word	of	your	conversation.	If	you	do	this,	she	will	run!

Do	 however	 look	 at	 her	 eyes	 for	 a	 few	 seconds	 while	 either	 you	 or	 she
speaks,	look	away	for	a	second	or	two,	and	then	come	back	to	her.	Having	this
natural	break	in	eye	contact	is	good.	Two	people,	even	if	madly	in	love,	do	not
stare	into	one	another’s	eyes	for	their	entire	discussions.	Trying	to	do	something
like	this	just	makes	you	look	awkward	as	shit!

Instead,	a	good	rule	of	thumb	is	a	few	seconds	on,	maybe	3-to-8,	and	then	a
second	or	two	off.	Sticking	to	this	rough	guideline	should	serve	you	well	at	first
while	you're	trying	to	get	the	timing	down	for	when	to	look	away	and	break	eye
contact.

Okay,	so	you've	gone	up	to	her,	stopped	her,	and	made	eye	contact	with	her;
now	you	want	to	deliver	the	infamous	opening	line.	If	you're	going	direct,	this
should	 obviously	 be	 something	 that	 states	 your	 intentions	 pretty	 clearly.	 It
doesn’t	 have	 to	 be	 off-the-wall	 bold,	 like	 “You	 are	 the	 sexiest	 woman	 I	 have
ever	seen!”	It	can	be	something	subtle	and	not	so	daring,	something	like,	“Hey,	I
saw	 you	 over	 here	 and	 I	 just	 wanted	 to	 come	 over	 and	 introduce	 myself.”
Something	 like	 this	 is	 direct	 (no	 games	 or	 trickery	 here)	 and	 honest.	 You're
simply	telling	a	woman	that	you've	seen	her	and	wanted	to	meet	her.	Which	is
exactly	the	truth.

I	 don’t	 want	 to	 give	 too	 many	 examples	 right	 now.	 The	 upcoming	 chapter
will	 be	 filled	 with	 examples	 of	 indirect,	 direct	 and	 observational	 openers.	 For
now,	let’s	move	on	to	the	phase	following	the	initial	line.

Once	you've	delivered	your	line,	whether	direct	or	indirect,	you'll	naturally
want	to	transition	away	from	it.	After	all,	who	wants	the	whole	conversation	to
be	 about	 the	 opener?	 Openers	 are	 just	 that,	 openings	 for	 other	 things	 to	 talk
about.	 After	 you	 finish	 with	 your	 opener,	 you	 want	 to	 begin	 talking	 about
something	 else.	 You	 can	 either	 introduce	 yourself	 (that's	 already	 a	 different
topic)	or	ask	her	a	question	to	find	out	a	little	more	about	her.

Perhaps	 you	 could	 go	 with	 something	 like	 “What	 are	 you	 doing	 in	 Boston
today?”	 That	 will	 do	 just	 fine.	 From	 there	 she	 can	 answer	 and	 give	 you	 more
information	to	work	with.	(Obviously,	if	you're	not	in	Boston,	you	wouldn’t	say
that;	in	fact,	you	can	substitute	anything	for	Boston	here:	“this	coffee	shop,”	“the
park,”	“this	bar,”	etc.)

The	 next	 thing	 you	 want	 to	 make	 sure	 to	 do,	 if	 you	 haven’t	 done	 it	 yet,	 is
reach	out	to	shake	her	hand	and	introduce	yourself.	Doing	this	shows	her	you're
being	 friendly,	 and	 also	 subconsciously	 empowers	 her.	 (By	 offering	 your	 hand
up	 for	 her	 to	 shake,	 you	 are	 giving	 her	 the	 power	 to	 turn	 you	 down	 and	 reject
you.	 This	 may	 not	 seem	 like	 a	 good	 thing,	 but	 to	 a	 woman	 who's	 just	 been
approached	by	a	strange	man,	it’s	a	very	helpful	measure	to	take	in	relaxing	her.)
She	feels	slightly	safer	when	you	put	yourself	out	on	the	line	like	this.	You	also
get	 to	 touch	 her,	 which	 is	 literally	 the	 first	 step	 of	 physical	 escalation.	 Just	 by
taking	 this	 tiny	 step,	 you	 open	 the	 door	 for	 further	 escalation,	 and	 gradual
moves,	albeit	baby	steps,	into	more	intimate	contact.

When	you	introduce	yourself,	you	can	just	keep	it	simple.	You	don’t	need	to

come	 up	 with	 anything	 fancy	 or	 funny	 or	 over-the-top,	 in	 an	 attempt	 to	 be
extraordinary.	 Just	 simply	 say,	 “Oh,	 by	 the	 way,	 my	 name	 is	 Justin	 ;	 what’s
yours?”	extending	your	hand	as	you	speak.	That’s	it.	She	will	most	likely	return
with	her	hand,	and	reciprocate	the	introduction.	(Please	don’t	make	the	mistake
of	 trying	 to	 be	 Mr.	 Suave	 when	 you	 introduce	 yourself,	 because	 of	 some	 lame
PUA	video	on	YouTube	 that	you	may	 have	seen.	This	doesn’t	 work.	Just	be	a
gentleman	here	and	introduce	yourself	like	one.)

After	 this,	 you	 want	 to	 build	 rapport	 with	 her,	 a	 bond	 between	 two	 human
beings.	To	build	rapport	with	a	woman	you	want	to	make	her	comfortable.	You
make	 her	 comfortable	 by	 being	 genuine	 and	 showing	 her	 your	 confidence	 in
what	 you're	 doing.	 By	 being	 relaxed	 and	 showing	 her	 that	 you	 yourself	 are
comfortable,	 even	 in	 that	 typically	 stressful	 moment	 of	 approaching	 a	 woman,
you	make	her	comfortable	in	return.	You	also	make	her	comfortable	by	smiling
at	her,	having	good	body	language,	and	keeping	steady	eye	contact.	All	of	these
things	work	synergistically	to	relax	her.

Another	great	technique	you	can	try	using	is	called	“mirroring.”	It’s	an	NLP
technique	whereby	you	subtly	mimic	her	body	language	and	movements,	which
makes	her	see	more	of	herself	in	you.	The	science	behind	this	procedure	is	that
we	as	humans	tend	to	feel	most	comfortable	around	things	that	look,	act,	or	feel
like	ourselves.	So	by	imitating	her	actions,	we	allow	her	to	feel	like	she's	looking
at	someone	similar	to	herself,	which	in	turn	makes	her	more	comfortable.

Some	things	you	can	do	to	mirror	her	could	be	crossing	your	arms	if	she	has
her	arms	crossed,	leaning	back	if	she's	leaning	back,	slowing	your	speech	down
to	 her	 speed	 if	 she	 talks	 slower	 than	 you,	 or	 even	 holding	 something	 in	 your
hand	if	she	has	something	in	hers.	Basically,	you	want	to	try	your	best	to	be	her
“mirror	image.”

To	 build	 rapport	 with	 a	 woman,	 you	 want	 to	 do	 your	 best	 to	 find	 things
between	 the	 two	 of	 you	 that	 are	 similar.	 Again	 this	 goes	 right	 along	 with
mirroring	 and	 feeling	 comfortable.	 Human	 beings	 like	 others	 with	 whom	 they
have	something	in	common.	It’s	true	that	opposites	attract	in	some	cases,	but	for
the	 most	 part,	 it’s	 been	 scientifically	 proven	 that	 most	 people	 are	 attracted	 to
others	 who	 are	 similar	 to	 them.	 By	 finding	 commonalities	 between	 you	 and	 a
woman,	you	actually	increase	your	attractiveness	to	her,	as	well	as	your	bond.

Finding	 things	 you	 share	 with	 a	 woman	 can	 be	 really	 easy	 once	 you're	 in

conversation.	Women	love	to	talk	and	they	will	give	you	all	sorts	of	information
to	work	with.	Even	the	quiet	woman	you’ve	just	met	will	still	usually	give	you
enough	to	build	a	bond	around	if	there's	something	there.	You	just	take	notice	of
little	things	about	what	a	woman	is	talking	about,	and	then	relate	them	back	to
your	 own	 experience,	 or	 (if	 you	 can’t	 relate	 to	 what	 she’s	 saying)	 you	 ask	 her
more	 questions,	 so	 you	 can	 get	 a	 better	 understanding	 about	 a	 subject;	 from
there,	you	can	relate	it	back	to	your	own	awareness.

For	example,	if	you	ask,	“Where	are	you	from?”	and	she	says	“California,”
but	 you've	 never	 been	 there	 before	 in	 your	 life,	 should	 this	 be	 the	 end	 of	 the
conversation?	Should	you	just	walk	away,	flustered,	because	she	doesn't	live	in
Boston,	like	you?	Of	course	not!	Work	with	what	she	gives	you,	and,	believe	it
or	not,	she's	actually	given	you	a	ton	of	material	with	which	to	work.

The	 possibilities	 for	 a	 response	 to	 something	 like	 this	 are	 quite	 literally
endless.	 You	 could	 respond	 with,	 “California,	 huh?	 That’s	 the	 opposite	 end	 of
the	country.	What	brings	you	all	the	way	out	here?”	Or	perhaps,	“California!	I've
always	 wanted	 to	 go	 there.	 What's	 it	 really	 like?”	 Or	 even	 this:	 “Ya'	 know,	 I
sometimes	wish	I	lived	there.	It’s	so	warm	there	all	year	round,	isn’t	it?	Unlike
here,	where	it’s	freezing	half	of	the	year!”	Or	how	about	this?	“Wow,	it’s	nice	to
finally	meet	someone	who	doesn’t	have	my	New	England	accent!”

As	 you	 can	 see,	 there	 are	 many	 different	 ways	 you	 could	 continue	 the
conversation	from	here.	If	you	get	stuck	in	the	beginning	and	run	out	of	things	to
say,	just	ask	her	where	she’s	from,	what	she	likes	to	do	for	fun,	and	what	she's
doing	 that	 day.	 These	 are	 some	 of	 the	 easier	 topics	 to	 liven	 up	 a	 conversation.
Asking	 her	 these	 things	 will	 usually	 work	 to	 keep	 building	 rapport	 and	 a
connection	between	the	two	of	you.

After	you	build	a	connection	with	her	you	want	to	go	for	the	number	close.
This	could	be	one	minute	after	the	opener,	or	an	hour	later,	depending	on	how
much	 of	 a	 connection	 you	 want	 to	 build	 and	 how	 much	 time	 you	 actually
surmise	 you	 have	 with	 her.	 However,	 getting	 her	 number	 is	 quite	 honestly	 the
easiest	part	of	the	entire	approach.	If	you	have	built	any	type	of	connection	with
the	woman	at	all,	she	will	have	no	aversion	to	handing	over	her	digits.

If	 you’ve	 been	 talking	 to	 her	 for	 a	 while,	 and	 have	 built	 up	 a	 good
connection,	most	likely	you've	touched	upon	some	of	the	things	you	both	like	to
do.	If	this	is	the	case,	you	can	bring	one	of	those	things	back	up,	and	suggest	you

two	should	get	together	and	share	that	activity.	Say	for	instance	you	were	talking
about	how	much	you	like	to	ice-skate;	you	could	say	“Hey,	I	have	to	get	going
soon,	I’m	running	a	little	behind	schedule	now.	It	was	great	to	meet	you,	though;
we	definitely	have	to	go	ice-skating	together	soon.	What's	your	number,	so	we
can	set	this	up?”	With	a	set-up	like	this,	she	will	almost	certainly	give	you	her
number.

If	 you	 weren’t	 necessarily	 talking	 about	 any	 activity,	 and	 you	 don’t	 really
have	 anything	 to	 bring	 back	 into	 the	 conversation	 that	 you	 could	 both	 do,	 fall
back	 on	 something	 simpler:	 going	 to	 the	 bar	 with	 her	 for	 a	 drink,	 or	 simply
planning	to	meeting	 up	 soon	 to	“hang	 out.”	Say	something	 like,	“I	 have	to	 get
running,	but	it	was	really	great	to	meet	you,	Suzie	.	We	should	definitely	grab	a
drink	together	soon.	Do	you	have	a	number?”	Or	“I	have	to	get	running	now.	It
was	really	nice	meeting	you,	Julie	.	We	definitely	need	to	hangout	soon!	What’s
your	number,	so	we	can	plan	something	out?”	With	either	of	these,	she'll	surely
give	you	her	number.

After	that,	you	can	text	to	set	up	your	date	to	hang	out	together.	Voila!

"Believe	you	can	and	you're	halfway	there."

-	Theodore	Roosevelt

	Chapter	Eight

How	I	Approach,	Continued

In	the	previous	chapter	we	talked	about	how	to	handle	the	direct	approach.
Like	 I	 said,	 I	 don’t	 necessarily	 have	 a	 strict	 formula	 or	 system	 for	 how	 I	 open
with	a	woman.	It’s	more	of	a	permeable	guideline	to	what	I	do.	With	that	said,
I'd	now	like	to	give	you	the	other	half	of	my	flexible	guideline,	and	tell	you	what
else	 I	 like	 to	 do	 when	 I'm	 not	 going	 direct.	 Let’s	 begin	 now	 by	 discussing	 the
ever-important	indirect	approach.

After	 reading	 about	 the	 direct	 approach,	 by	 now	 you	 inadvertently	 have	 a
good	idea	about	what	the	indirect	approach	is	like.	It's	not	because	I	accidentally
gave	 away	 any	 clues	 earlier,	 but	 because	 the	 indirect	 approach	 and	 the	 direct
approach	involve	similar	steps.	In	fact,	aside	from	the	beginning,	the	indirect	and
direct	 approaches	 are	 actually	 one	 and	 the	 same.	 Just	 as	 when	 you're	 going
direct,	 in	 the	 indirect	 approach	 you	 must	 also	 remember	 to:	 stop	 the	 woman,
smile,	make	eye	contact,	deliver	your	opener,	shake	her	hand/introduce	yourself,
transition	away	from	your	opener	and,	finally,	get	her	digits.

Most	 of	 the	 time,	 I	 begin	 my	 day	 (one	 where	 I	 intend	 to	 do	 a	 number	 of
approaches)	with	approaching	indirectly.	I	do	this	because	it’s	so	much	easier	to
start	talking	to	a	woman	this	way,	as	opposed	to	being	direct	and	telling	them	my
true	feelings	right	off	the	bat.

I’m	not	sure	about	you,	but	I	(like	most	guys	I	know	or	work	with),	need	to
get	warmed	up	before	I	start	getting	into	that	confident,	outgoing,	flirtatious,	fun
zone.	 I	 can’t	 just	 snap	 my	 fingers	 and	 magically	 be	 “on”	 when	 it	 comes	 to
meeting	women.	I	can	try	going	direct	when	I	first	start,	but	I	usually	won’t	have
the	 necessary	 energy	 to	 pull	 this	 off.	 (Like	 I	 said,	 maybe	 you	 can	 do	 this,	 as
some	guys	can,	but	I’m	not	one	of	them.)

Instead,	I	use	the	more	down-to-earth,	realistic	approach,	which	is	circuitous
in	nature.	This	allows	me	to	get	socially	warmed	up	so	I	can	quickly	get	into	my
“zone.”	In	the	meantime,	it	allows	me	to	successfully	approach	a	woman,	even
when	my	energy	(along	with	everything	else)	may	still	not	be	quite	ready.

Getting	 back	 to	 the	 steps,	 it’s	 imperative	 that	 you	 stop	 a	 woman	 who's
walking.	As	Newton’s	Law	of	Motion	states:	All	objects	in	motion	will	remain	in
motion,	 unless	 acted	 upon	 by	 an	 outside	 force.	 You	 must	 be	 that	 outside	 force
whenever	approaching	a	woman,	and	you	must	stop	her	movement,	or	else	she’ll
just	keep	walking	away	forever.

If	she's	sitting	or	standing	still,	you	obviously	don't	need	to	stop	her,	and	this
makes	 things	 even	 easier.	 But	 remember	 that	 you	 want	 to	 mimic	 her	 body
language,	so	if	she's	sitting	down	at	a	coffee	shop	or	on	the	grass	in	a	park,	you
should	bend	down	and	speak	to	her	on	her	own	“level.”	After	a	few	seconds,	you
can	maybe	sit	down	next	to	her,	or	just	crouch	down.	Do	not	stand	over	her	and
try	 to	 open	 her	 from	 this	 position.	 She	 will	 not	 be	 receptive	 at	 all.	 You	 are
making	her	very	uncomfortable	by	doing	this!

After	you	stop	her	(or	just	go	up	to	her,	if	she	needn’t	be	stopped)	you	want
to	 make	 sure	 you	 smile	 again,	 and	 then	 make	 and	 maintain	 good	 eye	 contact.
After	 smiling	 and	 making	 eye	 contact,	 deliver	 your	 indirect	 opening	 line.	 The
truly	 great	 thing	 about	 this	 is	 that	 it	 can	 be	 anything	 in	 the	 world.	 You	 could
simply	 ask	 her	 for	 the	 time,	 for	 directions,	 for	 her	 opinion	 on	 something,
anything	at	all,	really.

The	most	important	thing	about	the	indirect	approach	is	the	transition	away
from	that	indirect	opener.	This	transition	is	99%	of	the	approach.	It	either	makes
or	breaks	the	entire	process.

Going	up	to	a	woman	indirectly	is	easy;	any	average,	frustrated,	chump-of-a-
man	can	do	this.	However,	what	separates	the	guys	who	routinely	date	and	sleep
with	 high-quality	 women	 from	 the	 ones	 who	 can’t	 is	 their	 ability	 to	 transition
from	that	initial	circuitous	line	into	attraction-building	mode.

Most	 guys	 will	 stop	 a	 woman,	 ask	 her	 a	 question,	 and	 then	 when	 she
answers	the	question	have	no	idea	what	to	do	next.	They	freeze,	managing	only
to	utter	a	reluctantly	awkward	“Thank	you,”	as	the	woman	walks	away,	shaking
her	 head.	 Don’t	 be	 the	 guy	 who	 doesn’t	 know	 what	 to	 say	 after	 opening
indirectly!

It’s	such	a	simple	way	to	open	a	woman.	You	complicate	things	when	you
start	to	think	of	how	perfect	everything	has	to	be	in	the	approach.	Don’t	stress
about	 trying	 to	 think	 of	 funny	 and	 witty	 things	 to	 say	 following	 your	 opening
line.	Instead,	just	have	a	few	go-to	ways	of	transitioning	away	from	it.

A	 great	 transition	 after	 an	 indirect	 opener	 (actually	 my	 favorite)	 is	 to	 go
immediately	direct.	That’s	right,	go	right	into	telling	her	the	real	reason	why	you
stopped	her!	Tell	her	something	like,	“Wow!	I	just	realized	how	sexy	you	look.
What's	your	name?”	Or	maybe	a	little	less	risky:	“Hey,	you’re	really	cute	!	I’m
Justin	,	what’s	your	name?”	You	can	do	this	even	without	explaining	anything
and	you	might	even	cut	her	off	in	the	middle	of	what	she	was	saying,	assuming
she	was	answering	your	indirect	question.	You	could	just	take	over	the	situation
and	 take	 charge	 of	 the	 interaction,	 completely	 forgetting	 about	 the	 indirect
question	you	asked	her.

Another	great	transition	 is	commenting	 on	something	about	 her	that	 stands
out.	This	could	be	anything	at	all	you've	noticed:	her	appearance,	her	speech,	her
vibe,	 her	 energy,	 some	 accessory	 she's	 wearing	 .	 .	 .	 you	 get	 the	 point.	 After
indirectly	opening	her,	you	could	say,	“I	just	noticed	your	accent.	You	can’t	be
from	Boston	!	Where	are	you	from?”	Or	maybe	“Hey,	I	really	like	your	energy!
You	seem	like	a	fun	and	outgoing	person.	What’s	your	name?”	A	few	lines	like
these	 are	 great	 for	 getting	 the	 conversation	 going.	 They	 are	 unassuming,	 non-
threatening,	and	rather	effective.

You	want	to	build	rapport	as	soon	as	possible	after	you	approach.	Asking	her
a	 rapport-building	 question	 after	 the	 initial	 opener	 is	 a	 great	 way	 to	 transition.
Say	 any	 one	 of	 the	 rapport-building	 questions	 we	 discussed	 in	 the	 previous
chapter:	 Where	 are	 you	 from?	 What	 do	 you	 like	 to	 do	 for	 fun?	 What	 have	 you
been	 doing	 today?	 You	 can	 also	 combine	 that	 with	 something	 else:	 “So	 what
were	you	up	to	on	this	fine	day	before	I	stumbled	across	you?”	From	there	you
could	start	freely	talking	about	each	other’s	days.	(Notice	how	fine	is	italicized
above,	because	it	denotes	a	sarcastic	and	rather	funny	way	of	saying	that	word	in
that	sentence.	Sarcasm	can	often	be	a	great	tool	for	humor,	if	used	sparingly.)

A	final,	easy-to-do	but	less-effective	way	to	transition	away	from	the	opener
is	 to	 just	 either	 thank	 her	 for	 answering	 your	 question	 and	 then	 introduce
yourself,	or	thank	her	and	offer	a	“high-five”	as	a	sort	of	reward	for	helping	you
out.	 (This	 is	 really	 a	 last-ditch	 move,	 though!)	 You	 could	 say	 something	 like,
“Thanks.	 I’m	 Justin,	 by	 the	 way	 (offering	 your	 hand	 to	 shake).	 What’s	 your
name?”	Or	you	could	say,	“Thanks	so	much	for	the	help,	you’re	awesome,	high-
five?”

I	know	the	high-five	seems	a	little	lame,	but	it	does	work	at	times.	It	works
because	it’s	playful	and	innocent.	Who	doesn’t	want	to	high-five	a	guy	who	puts

up	his	hand?	Nobody	wants	to	leave	a	high-fiver	hanging.	After	getting	the	high-
five,	 you	 can	 then	 get	 her	 name	 and	 give	 her	 yours	 in	 return,	 and	 proceed
onward.

When	going	direct,	it’s	usually	good	to	introduce	yourself	directly	after	your
opening,	straightforward	line.	It’s	good	to	get	the	name-exchange	part	out	of	the
way	and	begin	to	really	build	rapport	this	way.	It	works	this	way	because	using
the	 direct	 line	 is	 very	 bold	 and	 warrants	 an	 introduction	 from	 the	 person	 (you)
who's	saying	it.

On	the	other	hand,	using	a	weak,	indirect	line,	and	then	saying	“My	name	is
Justin	by	the	way.	What’s	your	name?”	doesn’t	really	fit	the	equation.	In	other
words,	if	you	try	to	use	the	hand-shake/name	exchange	as	the	transition,	it	won’t
work	well.	It’s	really	forcing	something	that	isn’t	there	yet.	(You	could	try	it,	of
course.	 It	 might	 work	 once	 in	 a	 while,	 but	 I	 don’t	 recommend	 it.)	 Instead,	 use
one	of	the	transitions	first,	then	introduce	yourself	and	shake	her	hand.	After	a
smooth	transition,	the	introduction	is	much	easier	and,	more	importantly,	natural.
She	will	feel	like	she's	having	a	normal	conversation,	rather	than	being	hit	on	by
some	random	guy.

After	 shaking	 her	 hand	 and	 introducing	 yourself,	 you	 want	 to	 proceed	 to
building	 more	 rapport,	 and	 then	 finally	 getting	 her	 number.	 Again,	 the	 rapport
comes	down	to	how	much	time	you	can	and	want	to	invest.	If	you	only	have	a
minute	 or	 a	 couple	 of	 seconds	 to	 talk	 to	 her,	 obviously	 you	 can’t	 build	 a	 huge
amount	of	rapport.	Even	still,	you	can	bring	up	the	fact	that	she	seems	nice	and
that	you'd	like	to	get	to	know	her	further.

You	can	use	a	standard	line	like,	“It	 was	really	nice	to	meet	you,	Erika	.	I
have	to	get	going,	but	we	should	grab	a	drink	soon.	What’s	your	number?”	Or	“I
have	to	get	back	to	work,	and	you	probably	have	to	get	going,	but	we	definitely
need	to	hang	out	soon.	What’s	your	number	so	we	can	set	something	up?”	Either
one	of	these	works	great.

If	time	is	on	your	side	and	you	have	much	more	opportunity	to	build	rapport,
then	go	ahead	and	do	it.	Talk	about	shared	interests.	Talk	about	things	you	love
doing	 and	 places	 you	 like	 to	 go.	 Hopefully,	 you	 can	 connect	 on	 one	 of	 these
topics	and	when	the	time	comes	when	you	decide	to	get	her	number,	you'll	bring
one	of	these	shared	interests	back	up.	Maybe	you	both	like	to	walk	your	dogs	in
the	park,	and	you	say	“I	have	to	get	running	now,	but	we	absolutely	have	to	get

our	dogs	together	and	take	them	to	the	park.	What’s	your	cell,	so	I	can	text	you
mine	and	we	can	set	this	up!”

Anything	will	work	here.	Just	bring	back	up	whatever	you	were	connecting
on,	and	say	that	you	“definitely”	or	“absolutely”	have	to	get	together	again	to	do
that	thing.	Women	love	this.	If	she	has	even	the	tiniest	bit	of	attraction	or	rapport
with	you,	she	will	give	you	her	number.	It’s	actually	much	easier	than	you	think
to	 get	 a	 woman’s	 number.	 And	 it’s	 much	 easier	 than	 you	 think	 to	 get	 good	 at
approaching	indirectly.

"Keep	your	face	always	toward	the	sunshine,
And	shadows	will	fall	behind	you."

-	Walt	Whitman

	Chapter	Nine

Everyday	Openers

As	promised,	I	have	delivered	an	opener	for	just	about	every	situation	you
could	 think	 of	 for	 meeting	 a	 woman.	 These	 openers	 have	 all	 been	 tried	 and
tested,	 so	 I	 know	 they	 work.	 If	 they	 don’t	 work	 for	 you,	 for	 whatever	 reason,
don't	blame	me!	It’s	not	the	words	you	say,	it’s	how	you	say	them.	This	section
should	not	be	used	as	a	way	to	take	opening	pick-up	lines	and	then	repeat	them
verbatim,	word-for-word,	in	an	attempt	to	pick	up	girls.	That’s	not	going	to	work
well	for	you.

Instead,	use	this	as	a	general	guide	for	things	you	could	potentially	say	when
it	 comes	 to	 different	 scenarios	 and	 different	 approaches.	 The	 possibilities	 are
pretty	much	infinite,	but	I	want	to	give	you	an	idea	and	perhaps	give	you	the	key
to	generating	your	own	ideas.	Originality	is	the	father	of	genius	.

Why	 won’t	 these	 openers	 work	 and	 why	 is	 being	 original	 so	 important?
They	 won’t	 work	 because	 using	 someone	 else’s	 opener	 is	 like	 repeating	 the
punchline	of	a	joke	after	everyone’s	already	laughed.	Have	you	ever	tried	this?
What	probably	happened	was	the	person	who	didn’t	get	it	the	first	time,	didn’t
get	 it	 the	 second	 time;	 or	 even	 if	 they	 did,	 they	 didn’t	 find	 it	 funny	 this	 time,
because	 the	 energy	 and	 excitement	 of	 the	 punchline	 was	 gone.	 It’s	 almost
exactly	the	same	with	using	opening	lines.	Opening	lines	used	in	the	spur	of	the
moment	work	great	on	a	woman,	because	they	have	new	excitement	and	energy
in	 them.	 If	 heard	 by	 one	 person,	 and	 copied	 later	 on	 by	 that	 same	 person,	 it
probably	won’t	be	effective.

By	 being	 original,	 you	 create	 natural	 and	 authentic	 energy	 and	 excitement
with	 your	 openers.	 You	 live	 in	 the	 moment	 with	 the	 woman	 and	 create	 real
magic.	Even	if	you	don’t	succeed,	you	use	that	creative	and	imaginative	part	of
your	brain	that	makes	things	happen.	Next	time	you	try	approaching,	you	will	be
more	in	tune.

Without	further	ado,	here	is	a	list	of	my	openers	for	just	about	any	situation:

Street	(Daytime)

Direct:	“Hey,	I	saw	you	standing	over	here	and	I	had	to	come	say	hi.	You're

really	cute.	What’s	your	name?”

Indirect:	“Excuse	me,	can	you	tell	me	how	to	get	to	Panera	from	here?”

Observational:	(to	a	woman	sitting	on	a	bench	listening	to	her	MP3	Player)

“Hey,	what’s	up?	What	you	listening	to?	Anything	good?”

Recommendation:	 Opening	 a	 woman	 on	 the	 street	 is	 probably	 the	 hardest
situation;	 but	 it	 can	 be	 the	 most	 rewarding	 place	 to	 meet	 women.	 When	 just
starting	 out,	 stick	 to	 going	 indirect	 for	 the	 majority	 of	 your	 approaches.	 It	 is
much	easier	to	succeed	this	way	because	it	is	less	stressful.

Bar/Lounge

Direct:	 “Hey	 sweetheart,	 what’s	 your	 name?	 You	 look	 absolutely	 beautiful

tonight,	I’m	Justin	.”

Indirect:	“Hey,	do	you	know	what	time	this	place	closes?”

Observational:	 “Hey,	 that	 drink	 looks	 really	 good.	 What	 is	 it,	 Vodka	 or

Rum?”

Recommendation:	Bar/Lounge	openers	are	usually	done	best	by	going	direct.
Women	at	a	bar	or	lounge	know	right	away	when	you	approach	them	that	you're
hitting	on	them.	Therefore,	being	straightforward	tends	to	work	best,	as	long	as
you're	straightforward	and	confident.	Without	the	latter,	you're	doomed	to	fail.

Supermarket

Direct:	“Hey,	I	know	this	is	random	but	I	just	saw	you	picking	out	veggies’

over	here	and	I	had	to	come	introduce	myself.	You’re	really	cute!”

Indirect:	“Excuse	me,	do	you	know	where	the	cereal	aisle	is	in	here?”

Observational:	 (looking	 at	 her	 basket/carriage)	 “Hey,	 is	 that	 organic	 stuff
any	good?	I	know	it’s	supposed	to	be	much	healthier,	but	I’m	a	little	hesitant	to
try	it	(smile	).”

Recommendation:	Supermarkets	can	be	tough	for	going	direct,	because	most
women	are	not	usually	thinking	about	getting	hit	on	in	a	supermarket.	They	are
also	 often	 crowded	 and	 you're	 “enclosed.”	 If	 you	 are	 actually	 there	 shopping,
and	 it	 backfires,	 it	 might	 be	 a	 very	 awkward	 experience,	 for	 both	 you	 and	 the

woman	you	approach.	Therefore,	indirect	approaches	(in	particular	observational
ones)	 are	 best	 here.	 They	 are	 safe	 and	 under	 the	 radar,	 yet	 they	 can	 still	 be
effective.

Coffee	Shop

Direct:	“Hey,	do	you	mind	if	I	sit	next	to	you?	I	love	having	a	chat	with	my

coffee.”

Indirect:	“Excuse	me,	is	this	seat	right	next	to	you	taken?”

Observational:	 “What	 is	 that	 you’re	 drinking?	 It	 looks	 amazing	 .	 .	 .	 Ten

times	better	than	what	I	got!”

Recommendation:	Coffee	shops	are	great	places	to	meet	women;	they're	sort
of	like	daytime	bars.	Women	are	usually	more	open	to	talking	to	guys	here	than
in	 a	 place	 like	 a	 supermarket.	 However,	 it’s	 still	 usually	 best	 to	 use	 a	 solid
observational	 opener,	 or	 a	 fairly	 modest	 direct	 line	 like	 the	 one	 above,	 rather
than	 being	 so	 straightforward.	 Women	 are	 more	 open	 here,	 but	 they	 still	 aren't
necessarily	anticipating	direct	approaches	and	compliments.

Nightclub

Direct:	 “Hey,	 sweetheart!	 You	 look	 absolutely	 sexy	 tonight!	 What’s	 your

name?”

Indirect:	“Hey,	what	kind	of	music	do	they	play	here?	It’s	my	first	time	in

this	place.”

Observational:	“Was	that	you	tearing	it	up	on	the	dance-floor	a	minute	ago?
You	definitely	have	some	good	moves	(smile	).	I	guess	I’m	gonna	have	to	show
you	mine	in	a	few	(smile	).”

Recommendation:	 Direct	 is	 definitely	 the	 best	 approach	 in	 this	 arena.
Women	are	here	to	have	fun	and	meet	guys.	More	often	than	not,	they're	looking
to	 hook	 up	 and	 have	 sex,	 too.	 Be	 confident	 with	 your	 sexual	 desires	 and	 she'll
reciprocate	 with	 hers.	 (However,	 beware	 of	 coming	 off	 cheesy	 or	 making
yourself	look	desperate	for	sex.)

Gym

Direct:	 “Hey,	 what’s	 up?	 I’ve	 seen	 you	 in	 here	 a	 few	 times,	 what’s	 your

name?”

Indirect:	 “Hey,	 do	 you	 know	 any	 other	 good	 biceps	 exercises?	 I’m	 getting
sick	of	doing	curls	every	week,	and	you	seem	like	you	know	all	kinds	of	crazy
exercises?”

Observational:	“Wow,	you	train	pretty	hard!	I	thought	I	was	a	nut	(smile	).

What,	do	you	have	the	Olympics	coming	up	soon?”

Recommendation:	Indirect	openers	are	best	at	a	gym.	You	want	to	spark	up	a
conversation	with	a	woman	here	in	as	subtle	a	way	as	possible.	Women	are	on
guard	 at	 the	 gym.	 (They	 are	 very	 self-conscious	 and	 expecting	 to	 be	 talked	 to
because	 of	 the	 way	 they	 are	 dressed,	 but	 that	 doesn’t	 necessarily	 mean	 they
welcome	 it.)	 Come	 in	 indirectly,	 get	 into	 a	 conversation	 about	 something
random	or	innocent,	then	slowly	go	for	the	kill	.	.	.	I	mean,	prize.

Street	(Nighttime)

Direct:	“Hey,	sweetheart!	You	look	absolutely	sexy	tonight!	Where	are	you

heading?	You	should	come	to	the	bar	with	me	and	my	friends.”

Indirect:	 “Excuse	 me,	 do	 you	 know	 where	 there's	 a	 good	 bar	 around	 here?
I’m	 meeting	 up	 with	 my	 friend	 in	 a	 little	 while,	 and	 I	 want	 to	 go	 somewhere
good.”

Observational:	 “Hey,	 where	 are	 you	 heading	 to	 all	 dolled	 up	 like	 that?	 Is

there	a	good	lounge	or	club	around	here	I	don’t	know	about?”

Recommendation:	These	nighttime	openers	are	more	applicable	to	scenarios
very	late	in	the	evening,	if	not	the	early	morning	(10	p.m.-to-3	a.m.	range).	They
are	much	more	bold	and	blunt	than	any	of	the	other	openers	on	this	list.	Most	of
the	time,	at	this	point	in	the	night,	women	are	either	heading	to	a	bar	or	club	to
drink	 and	 have	 fun,	 or	 coming	 back	 from	 one	 after	 drinking	 and	 having	 fun.
Therefore,	they	are	much	blunter	themselves	and	may	be	open	to	these	types	of
approaches.	 I	 recommend	 going	 direct	 and	 being	 bold	 if	 you're	 approaching	 a
woman	on	the	street	at	night.	(Just	to	be	clear,	these	are	all	approaches	in	public
settings,	 mainly	 in	 bar	 or	 club	 areas	 with	 lots	 of	 people.	 You	 don’t	 want	 to	 be
saying	these	things	when	she	is	by	herself	and	nobody	is	around!	If	you	do	you
will	surely	look	like	a	creep	or	diddler	or	worse!)

Mall

Direct:	“Hi,	I	don’t	mean	to	bug	you,	but	I	just	saw	you	walking	by	and	had

to	come	tell	you	how	cute	you	are!	What’s	your	name?”

Indirect:	“Excuse	me,	do	you	know	where	the	food	court	is?”

Observational:	(smiling	at	a	woman	walking	toward	you)	“Hey,	how	do	you
do	it?	(She	looks	at	you	and	asks,	‘What?’)	How	do	you	carry	so	many	bags	all
at	once?	You're	probably	getting	a	better	workout	than	when	I	go	to	the	gym!”

Recommendation:	The	mall	has	been	famous	as	a	pick-up	hotspot	for	many
decades.	 Because	 of	 this	 infamy,	 it	 can	 be	 easy	 for	 women	 to	 scope	 out	 a
potential	 approacher	 from	 miles	 away.	 This	 leaves	 them	 cautious	 and	 often
disinterested	 in	 meeting	 men	 in	 that	 setting.	 However,	 coming	 in	 with	 a	 good
indirect	 opener	 can	 often	 negate	 this	 self-defense	 mechanism	 and	 allow	 you	 to
covertly	swoop	in	under	the	radar.	Asking	a	simple	question	to	get	them	to	stop

Beach

Direct:	 “What’s	 up,	 sweetheart?	 You	 look	 absolutely	 sexy!	 What’s	 your

name?	I’m	Justin	(smile!	).”

Indirect:	“Hey,	have	you	been	in	the	water	yet?	I’m	wondering	if	it’s	cold	or

not?”

Observational:	 (holding	 up	 your	 chick-magnet,	 aka	 football)	 “Hey,	 do	 you
want	to	pass	with	me?”	(You	can	say	this	to	a	woman	sitting	or	lying	next	to	you
or	in	your	area.)

Recommendation:	An	observational	opener	is	best	at	the	beach.	Going	direct
isn’t	 really	 ideal;	 it’s	 similar	 to	 the	 gym,	 where	 a	 girl	 might	 feel	 like	 you're
coming	on	too	strong	for	her.	She	might	be	a	little	self-conscious,	even	if	she's
absolutely	 beautiful.	 Instead,	 scope	 out	 the	 environment,	 bring	 a	 football,
Frisbee,	or	some	other	accessory.	If	nothing	else,	invite	her	to	“play”	with	you.
Typically,	this	will	work,	as	girls	want	to	do	something	other	than	just	lie	down
the	entire	day.

Park

Direct:	 “Excuse	 me.	 I	 know	 this	 is	 random,	 but	 I	 just	 had	 to	 come	 say	 hi.

You	are	really	beautiful!	What’s	your	name?”

Indirect:	“Hey,	that’s	a	really	cool	dog.	What	kind	is	he,	and	is	he	friendly?”

Observational:	(to	a	girl	sitting	on	a	bench	with	her	MP3	player	on)	“Hey,

what	are	you	listening	to?”

Recommendation:	Depending	on	your	energy	level	and	your	experience,	the
park	can	vary.	If	you’re	just	starting	out	in	the	day,	and	you	really	don’t	have	the
energy	to	do	bold,	direct	approaching,	your	best	bet	is	to	go	indirect.	However,	if
you	 have	 good	 energy	 and	 are	 flowing,	 going	 direct	 is	 probably	 a	 little	 easier.
This	one's	literally	a	tossup,	depending	on	your	particular	mood	(Okay,	maybe	I
lean	 a	 little	 more	 toward	 indirect,	 just	 because	 it’s	 a	 little	 easier	 to	 pull	 off,	 as
girls	are	not	expecting	to	be	talked	to	by	a	random	guy	at	the	park	(unlike	at	a
nightclub	 or	 bar).	 But	 I	 don’t	 want	 to	 discredit	 the	 effectiveness	 of	 a	 strong
direct	game.)

Sporting	Event	(Pre-game)

Direct:	“Hey,	are	you	rooting	for	the	Patriots	?	You	look	way	too	sexy	to	be

a	Jets	fan!”

Indirect:	“Hey,	are	we	allowed	to	drink	out	in	the	open?	Or	do	the	cops	come

around	and	check	people?”

Observational:	“Hey,	do	you	mind	if	me	and	my	buddies	come	hang	out	with
you	and	your	girls?	You	look	like	you're	 going	to	be	having	a	blast	 over	here,
and	my	buddies	and	I	are	definitely	a	fun	time,	too!”

Recommendation:	 A	 pre-game	 at	 a	 sporting	 event	 is	 definitely	 a	 fun,
sometimes	crazy	environment.	Women	are	usually	partying	and	open	to	having	a
good	 time.	 It’s	 best,	 however,	 to	 not	 be	 so	 direct	 unless	 you're	 approaching
women	who	are	very	loud	and	obviously	drinking.	These	women	will	be	more
readily	 accepting	 of	 a	 direct	 approach.	 For	 most	 others,	 a	 good	 observational
opener	 will	 suit	 you	 best.	 After	 you	 open	 the	 door,	 you	 can	 create	 that	 fun,
oftentimes	crazy	environment	with	her	and	her	friends.	.	.	.	God,	do	I	love	pre-
games!

School

Direct:	 “Hey,	 what’s	 up?	 You’re	 in	 my	 English	 class,	 right?	 What’s	 your

name	again?	I’m	Justin.”

Indirect:	“Hey,	excuse	me,	do	you	know	where	the	Fine	Arts	building	is?”

Observational:	“Hey,	I	just	saw	your	books.	Do	you	major	in	Psych	.?	I’m

taking	two	courses	this	semester.	It’s	really	interesting.”

Recommendation:	 Going	 super	 direct	 on	 a	 college	 campus	 (or	 any	 type	 of
school	 environment)	 is	 not	 really	 recommended.	 In	 fact,	 it’s	 almost	 asking	 for
trouble.	Unless	you	want	to	be	investigated	by	the	school’s	police	force,	I	would
not	propose	going	up	to	young	women	and	telling	them	how	good	they	look.	In
fact,	this	happened	recently	on	a	college	campus	in	Massachusetts,	and	a	young
man	ended	up	getting	arrested.

Go	figure.	The	“party-girl	“college	girls	don’t	like	being	approached	during
the	 day	 and	 told	 how	 sexy	 they	 look.	 They	 only	 like	 being	 approached	 when
they're	drinking	at	night.	Instead,	go	indirect,	or	even	observational	here,	or	use
another	modest	direct	line,	like	the	one	above.	Lines	like	this	are	actually	really
effective.	Keeping	it	simple	and	asking	for	directions	to	a	building	on	campus	is
also	 very	 effective,	 and	 may	 be	 your	 best	 bet	 (if	 you	 don’t	 happen	 to	 share	 a
class	with	a	hottie).

Party

Direct:	“What’s	up,	sexy?	What’s	your	name?	I’m	Justin!”

Indirect:	“Hey,	do	you	know	whose	party	this	is?	I’m	friends	with	Joe	,	but

I’m	not	sure	whose	house	this	is.”

Observational:	 “You	 definitely	 seem	 like	 a	 lot	 of	 fun!	 What’s	 your	 name?

We	have	to	go	dance.	I	can	already	tell	you’re	a	blast!”

Recommendation:	 Party	 environments	 are	 perhaps	 the	 most	 exciting	 of	 all.
Women	here	are	very	outgoing	and	bold.	They	tend	to	let	their	guard	down	the
most,	as	they're	surrounded	by	friends	and	have	been	drinking	alcohol	to	let	go
of	 their	 societal	 inhibitions.	 Going	 direct	 when	 you	 see	 a	 woman	 you	 want	 to
talk	to	at	a	party	is	pretty	smart.	It	can	usually	work	when	done	confidently.

However,	observational	openers	can	work	slightly	better,	as	in	the	example
above.	 You	 can	 go	 direct,	 but	 instead	 of	 a	 generic	 direct	 opener,	 where	 you'd
probably	talk	about	her	looks,	try	opening	her	through	observation,	talking	more
about	her	energy	or	excitement.

For	 some	 of	 these	 examples	 I	 made	 a	 particular	 note	 to	 smile.	 It’s	 mostly
common	 sense	 that	 a	 good	 approach—whether	 direct,	 indirect	 or	 observational
—should	 be	 done	 in	 a	 fun,	 flirty	 way,	 so	 you	 should	 probably	 be	 smiling

anyways.	 However,	 I	 just	 needed	 to	 leave	 an	 additional	 reminder	 for	 some	 of
those	particular	situations	that	warrant	it	as	a	necessity.	Without	a	smile	for	most
of	these	openers,	you'll	come	off	as	being	too	serious.	Remember	to	show	your
pearly	whites!

That’s	all	the	examples	I	can	think	of	for	most	situations.	For	every	example
I	 gave,	 you	 could	 easily	 substitute	 a	 name	 or	 activity,	 even	 a	 place.	 I'm	 just
giving	you	rough	ideas	in	hopes	of	getting	your	own	minds	cranking,	so	you	can
generate	 some	 original	 openers	 of	 your	 own.	 Remember,	 coming	 up	 with	 your
own,	unique,	spur-of-the-moment	openers	is	100	times	more	effective	than	using
the	ones	listed	above!

"I	hated	every	minute	of	training,
But	I	said,	'Don't	quit.
Suffer	now	and	live	the	rest	of	your	life	as	a	champion'."

-	Muhammad	Ali

	Chapter	Ten

Dealing	With	Rejection

When	you	approach	women	on	the	street,	your	ass	is	naturally	going	to	get
rejected	most	of	the	time.	I’ve	said	this	before	and	I’ll	say	it	again:	“Successfully
approaching	a	woman	on	the	street	is	like	hitting	a	90	mph	fastball	from	a	Major
League	pitcher.”	It’s	hard	as	hell	to	have	continual	success	in	this	field.	In	fact,
maintaining	 an	 average	 of	 about	 30	 percent	 success	 is	 a	 great	 and	 optimal
number	to	shoot	for.

With	that	said,	you	must	get	used	to	being	rejected.

It	sucks	to	think	that,	believe	me,	and	it	sucks	even	more	to	type	that	out	on
the	pages	of	a	book,	but	it’s	true.	It’s	a	tough	world,	and	you	have	to	be	tough	to
survive.	 Guys	 who	 can’t	 handle	 being	 rejected	 are	 guys	 who	 never	 push
themselves	into	trying.

These	 are	 the	 same	 guys	 who	 become	 complacent	 in	 life	 and	 settle	 for
mediocrity	 and	 indifference.	 They	 work	 40+	 hours	 every	 week	 for	 40	 years
straight	 at	 the	 same	 boring	 job,	 because	 they	 don’t	 want	 to	 risk	 not	 finding
something	 else.	 They	 marry	 women	 they	 don’t	 really	 love	 because	 they're	 too
afraid	to	be	alone.	They	go	about	life	with	what-ifs	.	.	.	and	many	regrets.	And
they	live	an	unfulfilled	and	unhappy	life,	because	they've	never	had	the	courage
to	face	their	fears.

Don’t	be	one	of	these	people.	Don’t	live	your	life	out	of	fear.	Take	hold	of
your	fears	and	worries,	and	be	brave	enough	to	challenge	them	and	put	yourself
out	there.	That	beautiful	woman	walking	by	who	you’re	scared	as	hell	to	go	talk
to	could	actually	be	the	woman	you	end	up	marrying	and	creating	a	family	with.
She	could	be	your	one	and	only	true	love,	your	soul	mate	.	But	if	you	let	your
anxiety	decide	your	next	move,	she	can,	and	will,	keep	walking	right	on	by	and
out	of	your	life	forever!

Here’s	 some	 advice:	 If	 you	 get	 rejected	 by	 a	 woman,	 move	 on	 to	 the	 next
one!	“There	are	a	million	fish	in	the	sea”	as	they	say,	and	that	woman	is	but	one
tiny	little	fry.	(In	fact,	there	are	more	like	3.5	billion	women	in	the	sea,	and	this

one	 woman	 is	 absolutely	 meaningless	 in	 the	 overall	 picture.)	 If	 you	 fail,	 just
literally	walk	over	to	the	very	next	attractive	woman	you	see	and	approach	her.
Don’t	 dwell	 on	 the	 last	 one,	 or	 let	 her	 affect	 your	 mood	 or	 disposition	 in	 any
way!

On	that	note,	when	you	get	rejected	by	a	woman,	try	your	very	best	to	play	it
off	as	if	she’s	not	rejecting	you.	For	instance,	if	you	stop	a	woman	on	the	street
and	tell	her	she	looks	beautiful,	and	you	just	had	to	say	hi,	and	she	says	“You’re
weird,	 get	 the	 hell	 away	 from	 me,”	 what	 do	 you	 think	 a	 good	 reaction	 to	 this
would	 be?	 Would	 getting	 mad	 at	 her	 be	 wise?	 Would	 cowering	 down	 and
walking	away	with	your	tail	between	your	legs	be	smart?	Would	saying	you’re
sorry	 and	 apologizing	 and	 feeling	 embarrassed	 be	 okay?	 Absolutely	 not!	 None
of	these	options	are	any	good.	In	fact,	they're	all	terrible.	However,	some	guys
feel	 that	 when	 they	 get	 rejected	 in	 a	 way	 like	 this,	 they	 have	 to	 react	 in	 an
equally	 strange	 fashion,	 whether	 it	 be	 a	 timid	 reaction	 or	 an	 angry,	 aggressive
one.

Choose	 none	 of	 these.	 Instead,	 be	 cool	 about	 it.	 Play	 it	 off	 with	 a	 smile,	 a
laugh,	or	a	friendly	gesture.	Don’t	let	her	dump	her	shitty	mood	onto	you.	Keep
your	 fun,	 optimistic	 and	 playful	 mood,	 regardless	 of	 her	 reaction	 to	 your
approach.	 This	 way	 you	 can	 continue	 on	 with	 your	 approaches	 in	 a	 positive
mood,	not	a	negative	one	because	you	let	the	woman	who	rejected	you	take	over
your	emotions.	Also,	by	being	cool,	other	women	around	who	might	potentially
be	 watching	 or	 listening	 to	 you	 don’t	 see	you	 getting	 rejected.	If	 they	 see	 this,
your	 chance	 of	 picking	 them	 up	 is	 like	 hitting	 that	 90	 mph	 fastball	 .	 .	 .
blindfolded	and	with	a	toothpick	in	your	hands.	Perception	is	reality,	and	in	this
case	it	really	does	matter	how	women	perceive	you.	Even	if	a	woman	tells	you	to
“Go	to	hell!”	you	can	still	smile.	Other	women	will	just	notice	you	smiling	and
think	you’re	having	a	good	time.

We	have	to	learn	to	embrace	rejection	in	order	to	succeed	in	life.	Rejection
is	actually	a	positive	tool	that	we	can	use	to	better	ourselves.	Without	rejection
life	would	be	easy	and	without	challenge.	It	would	be	like	playing	and	beating
the	same	level	of	the	same	video	game	every	single	day	of	your	life!	It	would	not
only	get	boring	very	soon,	but	become	miserable	after	a	while.

Rejection	teaches	us	what	we	can	improve	on.	It’s	a	way	to	self-reflect	and
an	experience	that	enlightens	us	a	bit	more	into	our	approach—whether	it	be	in
how	to	actually	approach	a	woman	or	in	some	other	aspect	of	our	everyday	lives.

It’s	merely	an	experience	that	most	consider	bad,	but	which	allows	us	feedback
and	a	chance	to	learn.

It’s	 also	 a	 way	 to	 motivate	 us.	 Nobody	 likes	 that	 feeling	 of	 being	 turned
down.	So	what	do	successful	people	do	when	they	get	this	feeling?	They	make
sure	 they	 do	 everything	 in	 their	 power	 to	 never	 get	 it	 again!	 They	 work	 their
asses	off,	and	this	rejection	is	the	fuel	they	burn.	It’s	fuel	for	the	fire	inside	and
fuel	for	the	success	that	awaits.

Dating	 coaches	 happen	 to	 be	 masters	 of	 rejection.	 These	 guys	 are	 not
professional	 dating	 coaches	 because	 they	 have	 thin	 skin.	 No,	 they	 have	 very
thick	skin	and	are	able	to	deal	with	rejection	and	overcome	it.	Nobody	wakes	up
one	 day	 and	 just	 decides	 he's	 going	 to	 be	 great	 at	 approaching	 women	 and
talking	 to	 girls.	 It	 takes	 years	 of	 miserably	 failing	 before	 actually	 becoming
somewhat	 proficient.	 If,	 however,	 these	 dating	 coaches	 had	 just	 given	 up	 after
the	 first	 day	 or	 first	 few	 months,	 they	 never	 would’ve	 been	 able	 to	 learn	 and
truly	get	good	at	what	they	do.

The	secret	is	that	they	kept	plugging	away	at	it.	Just	like	anything	in	life	it
takes	 time	 and	 effort.	 The	 more	 you	 keep	 at	 something,	 the	 better	 you	 will
become	over	time.	I	have	been	blown	off,	yelled	at,	threatened,	ignored,	cursed
at,	 stiff-armed,	 and	 just	 about	 everything	 short	 of	 being	 punched	 in	 the	 face
when	it	comes	to	approaching	women.	Trust	me,	it’s	not	easy.

What	 I’ve	 learned	 to	 do	 is	 detach	 my	 emotions	 from	 a	 woman’s.	 I	 keep
myself	clear-headed,	even	during	the	worst	reactions	from	women,	and	I	keep	a
smile	on,	so	to	speak,	in	just	about	every	instance.	I	am	at	the	point	now	where	I
know	that	if	a	woman	“rejects”	me,	I	know,	truly	know	,	that	it’s	her	loss	and	not
mine.	And	this	makes	me	okay	with	it.

One	final,	very	important	thing	to	keep	in	mind	when	approaching	women	is
that	nine	times	out	of	ten,	a	woman	isn’t	actually	rejecting	you	.	She	might	just
be	having	an	awful	day;	she	might	be	thinking	about	something	important,	and
doesn’t	 want	 to	 be	 bothered	 (by	 anyone);	 she	 might	 just	 have	 to	 go	 to	 the
bathroom;	 she	 might	 be	 in	 a	 serious	 rush;	 she	 could	 be	 a	 lesbian,	 or	 already
taken;	 it	 might	 be	 her	 time	 of	 the	 month;	 you	 might	 look	 like	 someone	 she
absolutely	 hates;	 she	 might	 not	 be	 attracted	 whatsoever	 to	 guys	 that	 look	 like
you;	or	she	might	just	be	rejecting	your	approach.	(These	are	all	things	that	are
completely	outside	of	your	control.)	And	for	the	latter	situation,	it’s	still	not	you,

but	your	approach	that’s	making	her	say	“no.”

By	this	I	mean	to	remind	you	of	this	fact:	she	doesn’t	really	know	you.	How
could	 she?	 You’ve	 only	 said	 a	 few	 words	 to	 her,	 so	 she’s	 not	 really	 rejecting
you,	 but	 instead	 the	 situation,	 including	 the	 way	 you’ve	 gone	 up	 to	 her	 and
started	talking	to	her.	If	you	think	about	it,	there’s	really	nothing	to	feel	rejected
about.	She	doesn’t	know	you.	She	doesn’t	know	your	personality,	your	beliefs,
your	 career,	 your	 ambitions—or	 anything	 about	 you	 for	 that	 matter!	 Instead	 of
feeling	 rejection,	 you	 should	 feel	 happy	 knowing	 you’re	 one	 step	 closer	 to
finding	someone	who	will	know	all	of	these	things	about	you,	and	love	what	she
knows.

Rejection	will	always	hurt	no	matter	what	it	is.	Even	for	the	most	seasoned
approach-coach,	who's	a	master	of	rejection.	He	has	mastered	his	way	of	dealing
with	it	and	has	allowed	it	not	to	affect	his	life,	or	his	livelihood	for	that	matter;
on	 a	 basic	 level,	 though,	 that	 sour	 feeling	 of	 being	 passed	 over	 will	 always	 be
there.	It’s	a	sad	but	honest	truth	about	life:	Being	rejected	will	always	hurt.

The	worst	sorts	of	rejection	are	typically	those	we	experience	from	those	we
love	 or	 are	 attracted	 to.	 This	 seems	 to	 be	 the	 harshest	 form.	 A	 break-up,	 an
unanswered	 message,	 a	 no-show	 on	 a	 date,	 an	 uninterested	 response,	 these	 all
sting	 the	 soul.	 It	 makes	 us	 more	 mature	 as	 we	 grow	 older	 and	 overcome	 these
hurts,	but	no	matter	what	they	will	always	be	there.

The	 best	 way	 to	 deal	 with	 rejections	 like	 the	 examples	 above	 is	 to	 talk	 to
someone	 about	 it.	 Humans,	 being	 the	 social	 creatures	 we	 are,	 love	 to	 talk	 to
others	about	our	lives	and	especially	about	the	problems	within	them.	We	love,
no	need	,	to	figure	out	the	problems	that	confront	us	throughout	the	day;	talking
about	 a	 major	 rejection,	 perhaps	 the	 biggest	 problem	 we	 face	 (or	 at	 least	 our
biggest	perceived	problem),	is	definitely	a	need	we	have.	Finding	someone	to	fill
this	need	is	definitely	wise.

Having	 friends	 to	 talk	 to	 about	 your	 rejection	 is	 maybe	 the	 greatest	 help.
Letting	 go	 of	 your	 negative	 emotions	 and	 getting	 all	 the	 crazy	 thoughts	 out	 of
your	head	 is	very	 helpful.	 Telling	them	 to	 someone	who	 will	 be	there	 for	 you,
someone	 who	 can	 console	 and	 support	 you	 is	 even	 better.	 A	 true	 friend	 will
always	listen	and	want	to	help	you	in	your	time	of	grief.	Rather	than	replaying	in
your	head	what	went	wrong	and	why	it	didn’t	work	out,	you	can	actually	release
these	thoughts	onto	someone	else	and	get	honest	feedback.	It’s	such	a	liberating

action.

Not	only	this,	but	having	a	friend,	or	friends,	who	you	can	then	spend	time
with	and	take	your	mind	off	things	is	great	too.	Especially	if	it’s	a	break-up,	and
you’re	 used	 to	 spending	 so	 much	 time	 with	 the	 person	 who	 rejected	 you;
transferring	 that	 time	 over	 to	 your	 friend	 is	 very	 helpful.	 It	 eases	 the	 pain	 and
lessens	the	thoughts	and	emotions	you	have	for	that	other	person.	Keeping	busy
is	very	important,	and	it	allows	you	to	have	fun	again.	It	also	allows	you	to	work
on	 yourself	 and	 focus	 on	 things	 you	 probably	 weren’t	 able	 to	 focus	 on	 before.
Oftentimes,	rejection	can	be	a	true	blessing	in	disguise.

Another	 thing	 I	 know	 that	 works	 when	 dealing	 with	 rejection	 is	 seeing	 a
psychologist.	Especially	if	the	rejection	was	very	serious,	like	a	break-up.	If	you
feel	a	true	and	powerful	hurt	or	if	you	feel	scared	or	uncertain	about	where	to	go
from	here,	seeing	a	psychologist	can	really	help.

You	 don’t	 have	 to	 be	 crazy	 to	 see	 a	 psychologist	 either!	 In	 fact	 I	 believe
seeing	a	psychologist	is	one	of	the	most	proactive	and	healthy	things	you	can	do,
whether	 you're	 facing	 a	 break-up	 or	 some	 other	 form	 of	 rejection,	 or	 even	 if
you're	not.	I	really	believe	that	most	people	would	benefit	from	regularly	going
to	one	of	these	doctors.	Every	now	and	then	I	see	one,	and	I’ve	been	doing	this
for	years.

Psychologists	 are	 professionals	 at	 listening	 and	 helping	 you	 see	 things	 that
may	not	be	clear	to	you	right	away.	They're	almost	like	brain	detectives	and	they
help	you	put	the	pieces	together	on	questions	you	might	be	having	in	your	life.
Something	minor	or	something	major,	it	doesn’t	matter.

Good	psychologists	won’t	judge	you	or	put	you	down	or	try	to	criticize	you
in	any	way.	They	are	literally	there	to	help	you	and	simply	listen	and	give	their
best	input	when	needed.	They’re	great.	(On	a	side	note,	I	am	not	recommending
psychiatrists	 here,	 just	 psychologists.	 Psychiatrists	 are	 usually	 the	 doctors	 who
prescribe	medication,	whereas	psychologists	are	the	doctors	who	do	talk-therapy
and	 never	 prescribe	 any	 meds.	 I	 am	 not	 putting	 down	 psychiatrists	 here,	 but	 I
have	never	personally	been	to	one,	nor	have	I	taken	any	medication,	so	I	cannot
attest	for	going	to	them.)

The	great	Ray	Charles	once	sang	that	“time	heals	a	broken	heart”	and	I	agree
with	this	statement.	There	is	no	pill	or	potion	or	trick	or	gimmick	you	can	use	to
fix	 the	 ultimate	 form	 of	 rejection:	 a	 broken	 heart.	 But	 keeping	 busy,	 keeping

positive	 and	 talking	 to	 friends	 or	 a	 professional	 is	 the	 best	 and	 most	 effective
way	of	helping	yourself.	Ultimately	time	will	heal	you,	and	it	gets	easier	as	each
day	 passes.	 Soon	 enough,	 when	 the	 right	 amount	 of	 time	 has	 passed,	 you'll
notice	that	the	pain	has	been	gone	for	some	time,	and	that	you	didn't	even	notice
when	it	left.

"What	lies	behind	you	and	what	lies	in	front	of	you,
Pales	in	comparison	to	what	lies	inside	of	you."

-	Ralph	Waldo	Emerson

	Chapter	Eleven

Getting	In	"The	Zone"

There	 is	 a	 place	 in	 time	 when	 athletes,	 performers,	 or	 artists	 of	 some	 sort
claim	 to	 be	 in	 “The	 Zone.”	 They	 do	 everything	 perfectly	 and	 with	 precise
execution.	 Their	 work	 comes	 easily	 to	 them.	 Everything	 just	 clicks	 and	 they
assume	roles	of	excellence.	It	almost	seems	magical	to	watch	someone	who	is	in
this	 place:	 A	 perfect	 game	 from	 a	 pitcher.	 A	 high,	 emotionally	 gripping,	 note
from	a	musician	that	tingles	the	hair	on	your	neck.	A	mesmerizing	and	beautiful
painting,	hand-drawn	in	front	of	you.	These	all	embody	the	work	of	someone	in
“Their	Zone.”

I’m	sure	you’ve	come	across	this	before	in	your	own	life.	Maybe	you	get	in
“The	Zone”	all	the	time.	I	know,	for	example,	when	I	lift	weights	(when	I’m	by
myself,	 anyway),	 I	 think	 of	 nothing	 but	 the	 weights	 and	 my	 muscles.	 I	 am	 so
focused	 and	 tuned	 in	 to	 what	 I'm	 doing	 that	 I	 completely	 black	 out	 everything
else	 around	 me.	 A	 naked,	 1990’s	 Baywatch	 -era,	 Pamela	 Anderson-lookalike
could	sit	down	on	the	machine	next	to	me	and	start	flexing,	and	I	wouldn’t	even
notice	her!

Well,	maybe	I	would	,	but	you	get	the	point!

All	 I	 consider	 during	 my	 45	 minutes	 to	 an	 hour	 of	 pumping	 iron	 is	 what
weights	I'm	lifting	now	and	what	weights	I'll	be	lifting	next.	My	iPod	is	usually
on	in	the	background,	which	helps	me	focus	even	more.	This	is	my	zone	.

Have	you	ever	had	that	moment	when	you're	socially	on	?	Your	charisma	is
through	the	roof,	you’re	telling	jokes	and	making	people	laugh,	and	you’re	the
center	of	attention!	You	feel	like	you’re	saying	the	wittiest	and	smartest	things
ever	conceived,	and	people	are	loving	you	for	it!	You	have	all	kinds	of	energy
and	you	feel	unbelievably	great	about	yourself.	This	is	the	feeling	of	being	in	the
Zone.	It’s	the	social	zone,	where	you’re	just	socially	“ON.”	It’s	probably	the	best
feeling	you	can	have	in	the	entire	world.	It’s	even	better	than	popping	ecstasy!
(Just	kidding;	drugs	are	for	morons	and	I’ve	never	done	ecstasy,	so	I	can’t	say
for	sure,	but	it	probably	is!)	It’s	such	a	great	and	magical	feeling	when	you	feel
like	this	.	.	.	I	can’t	imagine	anything	topping	it!

This	 feeling	 of	 being	 ON	 is	 where	 you	 want	 to	 be	 when	 talking	 to	 a	 new
woman.	It’s	like	having	a	giant	magnet	under	your	shirt	that	sucks	her	in.	She	is
often	helpless	when	it	comes	to	wanting	you.	But	it’s	not	that	easy	to	cultivate
this	energy,	or	to	find,	and	be	in	this	Zone.

For	 some	 guys	 it’s	 much	 easier	 to	 get	 warmed	 up	 and	 start	 meeting	 and
attracting	 women	 than	 it	 is	 for	 others—especially	 the	 natural	 extroverts,	 or	 the
ones	who've	been	approaching	women	and	perfecting	the	craft	for	years.	These
guys	know	what	it	takes	to	get	themselves	in	the	social	mood	quickly,	and	start
manifesting	this	feeling	of	being	 ON.	Warming	up	 and	getting	ready	to	talk	to
women	comes	fairly	easy	to	them.

For	others,	myself	included,	it's	another	story.	Even	though	I	no	longer	need
much	time	to	get	myself	warmed	up	and	ready	to	go,	I	still	need	some	practice.	I
am	 a	 natural	introvert	 and	 shy	 guy.	 I	 don’t	 naturally	 love	 being	 loud,	 social	 or
outgoing,	 but	 it’s	 a	 switch	 that	 I’ve	 developed	 through	 the	 years.	 Now	 when	 I
want	these	things,	and	when	I	want	to	meet	women,	I	simply	turn	on	the	switch
and	get	myself	warmed	up.

If	 you’re	 just	 starting	 off,	 I	 definitely	 recommend	 getting	 yourself	 warmed
up	 before	 attempting	 to	 approach	 women.	 If	 not,	 the	 women	 you	 talk	 to	 are
going	to	eat	you	up—not	in	that	fun,	sexual	sort	of	way,	but	more	like	a	Jaws,
tearing	you	into	a	million	pieces	sort	of	way!

If	 you’ve	 ever	 tried	 self-hypnosis,	 you	 know	 it	 can	 be	 very	 effective	 for
implementing	positive	changes	in	your	life.	If	you	haven’t	done	or	heard	of	it,	let
me	explain	it	briefly:	Self-hypnosis	is	the	act	of	hypnotizing	your	own	mind	into
being	 more	 suggestible.	 Normally	 our	 minds	 operate	 on	 a	 conscious	 level.	 We
consciously	 think	 about	 everything	 we	 do,	 meaning	 we	 control	 our	 actions,
thoughts,	ideas,	etc.	However,	there's	another	part	of	our	brains	that	we	do	not
control,	and	this	is	called	the	subconscious.	The	subconscious	is	the	part	of	our
brain	that	automatically	does	things	for	us:	breathing,	sleeping,	feeling	emotions
(we	 can	 consciously	 do	 something	 to	 affect	 our	 emotions,	 but	 we	 can’t
consciously	 make	 ourselves	 feel	 an	 emotion,	 this	 comes	 automatically),
regulating	bodily	processes,	and	much	more.

They	say	that	the	subconscious	is	actually	something	like	97	percent	of	our
entire	 mind,	 leaving	 our	 conscious,	 or	 what	 we	 actually	 control,	 at	 only	 3
percent.	It's	pretty	crazy	if	you	think	about	it.

With	 that	 said,	 getting	 a	 hold	 of	 this	 powerful	 and	 dominant	 part	 of	 our
brains	 would	 seem	 very	 important.	 One	 great	 tool	 for	 taking	 over	 our
subconscious	minds	is	hypnosis,	which	allows	the	subconscious	to	enter	a	state
of	susceptibility,	where	we	can	tap	into	it,	and	actually	make	changes	to	it.	By
doing	this,	we	can	take	over	and	make	positive	suggestions	to	it	that	may	benefit
our	conscious	minds,	and	our	lives.

It	takes	a	little	practice	to	get	good	at	self-hypnosis,	but	it	can	be	used	for	a
broad	 range	 of	 applications.	 Sleeping	 better,	 releasing	 anxiety,	 releasing
depression,	 lowering	 your	 blood	 pressure,	 becoming	 more	 charismatic,	 gaining
more	confidence,	feeling	more	energetic,	concentrating	better	.	.	.	these	have	all
been	 affected	 by	 hypnosis.	 There	 are	 even	 self-hypnosis	 CDs	 containing	 all	 of
these	 topics	 and	 more.	 I’m	 sure	 you	 can	 see	 just	 how	 powerful	 this	 could
potentially	 be	 for	 a	 reserved	 guy	 looking	 to	 get	 in	 the	 right	 mindset	 before
talking	to	women!	So	I	recommend	trying	it	out	for	yourself.

There	 are	 even	 some	 recordings	 out	 there	 specifically	 designed	 for
approaching	women	and	for	becoming	more	confident	in	conversation.	The	two
hypnotists	 I	 often	 recommend	 are	 Andrew	 Dobson	 and	 Paul	 McKenna.	 They
both	 frequently	 deal	 with	 the	 issue	 of	 men	 looking	 to	 meet	 and	 socialize	 with
women.	I’ve	personally	used	products	from	both	of	these	guys	and	found	much
success.

Before	 I	 move	 on,	 I	 do	 want	 to	 say	 that	 self-hypnosis	 is	 not	 a	 cure-all.	 It
won’t	make	you	grow	wings	or	hair,	or	make	your	penis	bigger.	It	does	have	its
limits.	 However,	 it	 can	 be,	 as	 mentioned	 above,	 a	 great	 technique	 for	 planting
positive	suggestions	in	your	subconscious	mind,	which	in	turn	can	be	great	for
affecting	your	conscious	mind,	your	mood	and	your	emotions.

Along	 with	 hypnosis,	 I'd	 also	 recommend	 setting	 goals	 for	 the	 day,	 just
before	 you	 go	 out—and	 then	 sticking	 to	 them!	 Don’t	 make	 them	 too	 hard,	 or
you'll	 never	 accomplish	 them.	 Make	 them	 slightly	 challenging,	 but	 absolutely
achievable.	 Then	 push	 yourself	 to	 achieve	 those	 goals	 (again,	 not	 too	 hard,	 or
you	won’t	end	up	doing	them	at	all)!

For	example	a	good	goal	might	be,	“I	will	approach	10	women	today.”	then
go	out	and	approach	10	women.	If	you	can,	when	you	start	off,	stay	away	from
results-oriented	goals;	these	can	be	overwhelming	and	hard	to	achieve.	Don’t	tell
yourself,	“I	have	to	get	five	numbers	today!”	This	type	of	goal,	although	well-

intended,	can	often	do	the	opposite	and	block	your	progress.

Probably	the	best	thing	you	can	do	to	get	into	your	Zone	is	to	start	talking	to
everyone	once	you	get	out	of	your	house,	and	I	do	mean	everyone.	You	want	to
chat	up	that	ugly	girl	walking	down	the	street.	You	want	to	say	“Hi”	to	the	old
couple	 near	 you.	 You	 want	 to	 smile	 and	 say	 “How	 are	 ya’?”	 to	 the	 guy	 at	 the
hot-dog	stand.

It’s	very	important	to	get	out	of	your	head	and	assume	the	role	of	being	an
outgoing	 person.	 You	 don’t	 need	 to	 be	 over-the-top	 with	 this,	 but	 you	 should
definitely	be	pushing	yourself	out	of	your	shell.	Introverted	as	you	may	be,	for
the	next	few	hours	you	must	assume	the	role	of	being	social.

This	 social	 warming-up	 really	 helps	 when	 that	 incredibly	 sexy	 lady	 walks
by,	 and	 you	 can	 now	 stop	 her	 easily	 and	 say	 “Hi”—just	 as	 you’ve	 been	 doing
with	 everyone	 else.	 If	 you	 hadn’t	 been	 doing	 this,	 you’d	 probably	 feel	 a	 little
awkward	going	up	to	her	and	trying	to	talk	casually.

With	 that	 said,	 you	 should	 not	 do	 what	 many	 guys	 I’ve	 seen	 do:	 use	 not
being	warmed-up	as	an	excuse	not	to	approach	a	woman.	They’ll	say,	“No,	I’m
not	ready	yet!”	or	“I	have	to	get	a	little	more	warmed-up	first.”	These	statements
are	stupid!	You	should	go	and	approach	that	woman	.	.	.	and	use	her	to	warm	up!
If	you	fail	it’s	okay;	you’re	just	warming	up,	you're	supposed	to	fail!	Meanwhile,
if	 you	 succeed,	 you'll	 feel	 awesome.	 You'll	 have	 done	 what	 you	 went	 out	 that
day	to	do,	even	without	being	in	The	Zone.

When	that	time	comes	when	you	are	in	The	Zone,	you'll	know	it.	You'll	feel
great,	your	words	will	flow	smoothly,	your	mind	will	be	focused	and	you'll	be
saying	and	doing	all	kinds	of	clever	and	witty	things.	It’s	amazing.	Oh	yeah,	and
women	will	be	all	over	you!	They	won’t	be	able	to	help	it.	Being	in	The	Zone	is
like	being	a	giant	black	hole	of	fun.	Women	get	pulled	toward	you	and	sucked
into	the	depths	of	your	soul	to	feel	the	magic	of	who	you	are!

"If	a	man	does	not	keep	pace	with	his	companions,
Perhaps	it	is	because	he	hears	a	different	drummer.
Let	him	step	to	the	music	which	he	hears,
However	measured	or	far	away."

-	Henry	David	Thoreau

	Chapter	Twelve

Figuring	Out	Your	Goals

It’s	important	in	dating,	and	in	life	for	that	matter,	to	determine	exactly	what
it	is	you	want	to	achieve.	If	you	go	blindly	through	life	without	a	plan,	you'll	end
up	going	somewhere	you	don’t	want	to	be.	The	same	applies	to	dating.

Before	 you	 start	 meeting	 women,	 and	 then	 dating	 and	 sleeping	 with	 them,
you	must	first	decide	what	it	is	you	really	want.	A	good	way	to	do	this	is	to	write
out	on	a	piece	of	paper	where	you	want	to	be	in	your	dating	life	after	the	next
few	months.

Goal-setting	is	great,	and	there	has	been	much	written	on	the	subject.	I	agree
with	it	wholeheartedly	and	actually	dedicated	a	chapter	to	this	topic	in	my	last
book,	Giving	Shy	Guys	Game	(not	to	mention	the	brief	reference	to	goal-setting
in	the	last	chapter.)	However,	I	don’t	necessarily	want	to	dedicate	another	highly
detailed	 section	 to	 the	 topic.	 Instead,	 I'd	 rather	 give	 you	 a	 brief	 and	 concise
overview	of	goal-setting,	hoping	that	if	you	have	any	further	questions	you	can
read	my	previous	book.	I	simply	want	to	get	across	the	importance	of	having	a
good	idea	of	what	you’re	looking	for.

When	 setting	 goals	 about	 where	 you	 want	 to	 be,	 or	 what	 you	 want	 to
achieve,	make	sure	you	set	goals	that	are	challenging	at	the	moment.	They	can
always	 change	 as	 time	 goes	 on,	 however,	 just	 as	 we	 change	 and	 evolve	 over
time.	Sometimes	we	feel	strongly	about	something,	only	to	find	out	a	short	while
later	we	really	don’t	care	or	necessarily	want	that	same	thing	anymore;	instead,
there's	something	else	on	the	agenda.

This	is	okay.	If	you	set	a	goal	and	realize	after	six	months	you	don’t	have	the
motivation	 to	 achieve	 that	 goal,	 make	 a	 new	 one.	 You	 might	 find	 that	 you’ve
moved	 in	 the	 right	 direction	 while	 trying	 to	 reach	 that	 goal	 and	 are	 already
satisfied	with	the	results.	Again,	this	is	entirely	okay.

The	whole	point	of	setting	a	goal	is	to	improve	at	whatever	it	is	you	want	to
improve	 on.	 Making	 goals	 that	 push	 you	 and	 challenge	 the	 obstacles	 you	 have
set	for	yourself	is	all	you	need,	no	matter	what	the	endeavor	is.	Coming	up	a	bit

short	or	changing	your	mind	about	something	is	all	part	of	the	game.	Remember,
though,	that	figuring	out	where	you	want	to	be	is	very	important,	and	coming	up
with	a	plan	to	get	there	is	the	way	to	do	it!

By	 writing	 down	 your	 ideas	 about	 your	 dating	 life,	 you	 can	 concretely	 see
what	it	is	you	want.	You	can	take	all	the	ideas	in	your	head	(yes,	even	the	crazy
ones!)	 about	 your	 aspirations	 for	 approaching,	 dating,	 going-out	 with	 women,
and	 having	 sex	 with	 them,	 and	 organize	 them	 into	 one	 place.	 Think	 about
everything	 it	 is	 you	 want	 to	 accomplish,	 as	 well	 as	 everything	 you	 want	 (and
don’t	want)	in	a	woman.	Figure	out	how	much	time	you’re	willing	to	dedicate	to
the	 pursuit,	 the	 women	 you	 want	 to	 meet,	 the	 sex	 you	 want	 to	 have,	 and
everything	else	you	can	possibly	think	of	pertaining	to	being	with	women.	Then
take	this	information,	every	last	bit	of	it,	and	come	up	with	a	plan	for	your	entire
dating	life.

Call	it	“My	Dating	Life	Plan”	or	something	else	perhaps	a	little	more	unique.
By	doing	this	you'll	learn,	truly	learn,	what	it	is	you’re	looking	for.	This	will	be
unique	 from	 any	 other	 guy	 on	 the	 planet.	 Everyone	 has	 his	 own	 little	 wants,
needs,	and	desires.	These	will	be	yours.

Maybe	you	want	to	sleep	with	over	100	women.	Maybe	you	want	to	find	a
girlfriend	as	soon	as	possible.	Maybe	you	want	to	sleep	with	a	few	women	and
have	 fun,	 then	 eventually	 find	 and	 have	 a	 great	 girlfriend.	 Maybe	 you	 want	 to
find	a	wife.	Maybe	you	want	to	find	multiple	girlfriends,	or	even	multiple	wives
(maybe	you’re	a	Mormon).	Whatever	it	is,	figure	it	out.	This	information	is	very
important.	It	will	determine	your	plan	for	success.

For	example,	if	your	goal	is	to	sleep	with	as	many	women	as	possible,	you're
not	going	to	be	so	picky	about	who	you	bring	to	bed.	It	will	be	easy	to	go	out
and	 start	 approaching	 every	 woman	 with	 a	 pulse.	 (In	 fact,	 drop	 this	 book	 right
now	and	get	started!)

If,	 however,	 you	 want	 to	 be	 a	 little	 more	 reserved	 about	 the	 women	 you
sleep	with,	you'll	want	to	start	making	a	sort	of	checklist,	of	the	things	that	you
love	in	women	and	things	that	you	hate.	This	might	seem	a	bit	crude	to	some,
but	it’s	actually	very	honest	and	effective.	Why	waste	your	time,	or	a	woman’s
time,	when	you’re	not	really	into	her,	if	there	are	things	about	her	you	can’t	get
past.	By	being	pickier,	you	can	eliminate	a	lot	of	the	women	to	whom	you're	not
so	attracted	(physically,	mentally,	or	in	any	other	way),	right	off	the	bat.	If	this	is

you,	come	up	with	a	more	detailed	plan	about	what	you	want	in	a	woman.

After	you	come	up	with	this	plan,	stick	to	it!	It	might	be	easy	to	forget	what
you’re	 looking	 for,	 or	 to	 give	 in	 to	 someone	 you’re	 not	 really	 interested	 in
(especially	if	you’re	not	on	the	hottest	streak	of	having	sex	lately),	but	please,	do
your	best	and	stay	strong.	If	you	stick	to	your	guns,	I	promise	you,	it	will	work
itself	out.	A	woman	to	whom	you’re	really	attracted	is	just	around	the	corner.

Now	I’m	not	saying	to	be	picky	about	the	women	you	talk	to,	or	use	the	last
two	paragraphs	as	an	excuse	to	be	anti-social—especially	when	you’re	trying	to
get	good	at	the	art	of	approaching	women!	No,	that’s	not	at	all	what	I	mean	here.
What	 I	 am	 saying	 is,	 don't	 just	 sleep	 with	 a	 woman,	 or	 otherwise	 waste	 each
other’s	time	(asking	for	her	number,	texting/calling,	taking	her	on	a	date,	having
sex	with	her,	etc.),	if	you’re	not	really	into	her.	This	is	probably	the	worst	thing
you	can	do.	You're	not	only	hurting	the	woman	by	leading	her	on,	you’re	hurting
yourself,	 at	 the	 very	 core:	 you’re	 hurting	 your	 soul	 by	 lying	 to	 it	 and	 trying	 to
force	it	to	do	something	it	doesn’t	want	to.

Decide	what	you	want,	and	stick	with	it.	Maybe	you	want	to	start	sleeping
with	everything	that	owns	a	vagina.	That’s	great,	go	for	it.	Or	maybe	you	want	to
be	a	lot	pickier,	and	actually	find	your	next	wife.	Again,	that’s	great,	go	for	it!
(You	should	actually	be	meeting	more	women	in	this	case,	since	you're	going	to
be	 more	 particular	 until	 you	 find	 the	 right	 one.)	 Whatever	 the	 case	 may	 be,
whether	 you're	 more	 like	 the	 former	 example	 or	 the	 latter,	 settle	 on	 precisely
what	it	is	you	want.	Make	a	plan	for	meeting	women,	and	make	goals	for	your
dating	 life	 so	 you	 can	 succeed	 in	 this	 area.	 Then	 go	 out	 and	 actually	 push
yourself	 and	 grab	 ahold	 of	 success	 .	 .	 .	 At	 the	 very	 least,	 grab	 ahold	 of	 a
woman’s	digits!

"In	a	gentle	way,	you	can	shake	the	world."

-	Mahatma	Gandhi

	Chapter	Thirteen

The	Types	Of	Women	Out	There

Along	 with	 figuring	 out	 your	 goals,	 comes	 figuring	 out	 your	 girls.	 This
completes	 the	 total	 game	 plan.	 It’s	 important,	 as	 we	 touched	 upon	 in	 the	 last
chapter,	to	really	decide	what	you	like	and	don’t	like	in	a	woman.	And	to	take
this	awareness	and	come	up	with	a	good	idea	about	what	you	want	to	get	out	of
your	dating	life.	This	knowledge	will	really	tighten	up	your	approach	to	meeting
and	dating	women,	and	hopefully	leave	you	with	the	right	idea	about	where	to
go.

I	 want	 to	 give	 you	 the	 list	 of	 a	 few	 different	 types	 of	 women	 and	 the
characteristics	that	they	often	have,	so	you	can	decide	which	types	most	closely
resemble	the	ones	you	desire.	Perhaps	you're	not	looking	for	one	single	category
of	 womanhood,	 but	 instead	 seek	 a	 combination	 of	 two	 or	 even	 three	 of	 these
characteristics.	 That’s	 fine,	 just	 the	 fact	 that	 you	 realize	 you’re	 doing	 this	 will
enlighten	you	even	more	about	what	kind	of	woman	you	want.

Also,	this	list	is	very	general	and	arbitrary.	Not	all	women	will	fit	into	these
molds,	 and	 most	 are	 far	 more	 complex	 than	 any	 labeled	 grouping.	 This	 is
obviously	for	purposes	of	generalization,	so	please	do	not	take	this	section	word-
for-word,	or	get	offended	if	you’re	a	woman	reading	this	who	happens	to	be	one
of	the	not-so-appealing	types!

The	Party	Girl

The	 Party	 Girl	 is	 probably	 the	 funnest	 woman	 out	 there.	 She's	 usually	 the
center	of	attention,	as	she’s	often	doing	something	either	sexual	or	embarrassing.
She	is	definitely	full	of	life	and	entertainment	though,	and	does	not	have	a	dull
moment	 in	 her—unless	 it's	 while	 she's	 hung-over	 or	 passed	 out	 in	 the	 corner.
Cute,	sexy	and	young,	the	party	girl	will	never	be	one	you	become	bored	with.
She'll	know	where	all	the	fun	parties	are	and	will	have	a	lot	of	cool,	cute	young
friends	to	hang	out	with.	She'll	be	very	down	for	sex,	and	should	be	pretty	easy
to	 have	 it	 with.	 In	 fact,	 sex	 is	 basically	 her	 M.O.,	 along	 with	 alcohol	 and
recreational	drugs.	The	party	girl	loves	party	guys	and	having	a	good	time.	She
may	long	for	a	serious	boyfriend	deep	down	inside,	but	she's	just	not	anywhere

near	(Nowhere	in	hell!)	ready	for	one	at	this	point.

Beware:	Falling	for	the	party	girl	may	be	tempting—very,	very	tempting	to
some—but	 you	 must	 look	 to	 these	 types	 only	 for	 fun	 and	 sex.	 Party	 girls	 will
remain	party	girls	at	heart,	and	won't	want	to	settle	down	or	be	serious	anytime
soon.	 Unfortunately	 they	 are	 among	 the	 least	 trustworthy	 and	 loyal	 of	 all	 the
types	 of	 girls	 out	 there.	 Don't	 think	 of	 the	 party	 girl	 as	 anything	 more	 than	 a
pretty	good,	one-time	deal.

The	Dream	Girl

The	Dream	Girl	is	the	one	we	all	want,	the	woman	we	literally	dream	about
at	 times.	 She	 is	 the	 hottest	 lady	 in	 the	 room,	 and	 she	 carries	 herself	 with	 an
almost	 unattainable	 mystique.	 She	 has	 a	 beautiful	 smile	 and	 your	 heart	 pounds
every	time	she	inches	closer	to	you.	She’s	always	either	taken	(in	a	relationship),
or	 seemingly	 talking	 to	 someone	 else	 .	 .	 .	 just	 out	 of	 our	 reach.	 She’s	 called	 a
“dream	girl”	for	a	reason,	and	that	reason	is	she	will	only	be	had	in	our	wildest
dreams.	 Unfortunately	 dream	 girls	 rarely,	 if	 ever,	 become	 a	 reality.	 It’s	 not
impossible,	but	it’s	usually	more	of	a	fantasy	when	it	comes	to	them.	This	is	not
to	say	that	these	women	are	without	their	flaws;	we	just	don’t	see	them,	or	we
pretend	they	don’t	exist,	which	makes	the	fantasy	even	better!

Beware:	The	dream	girl	is	usually	a	woman	who's	unattainable	for	whatever
reason.	She	may	be	seemingly	flawless	in	every	way	(looks,	personality,	charm,
etc.),	 and	 for	 whatever	 reason	 (she’s	 married,	 in	 a	 relationship,	 not	 interested,
not	available,	etc.)	we	just	can’t	manage	to	get	her.	These	women	are	great	for
motivating	us	to	better	ourselves	and	make	ourselves	strive	to	have	someone	as
special	as	a	dream	girl,	but	they	really	should	not	be	looked	upon	as	someone	to
have	 a	 serious	 relationship	 with.	 Dream	 girls	 are	 such	 because	 as	 humans	 we
always	 desire	 what	 we	 can’t	 have.	 Just	 by	 the	 mere	 fact	 of	 being	 unattainable,
these	women	become	dream	girls.	Try	your	best	not	to	seriously	pursue	a	dream
girl,	or	you	risk	pursuing	a	potential	nightmare!

The	Bitchy	Girl

The	Bitchy	Girl	is	usually	a	total	bitch.	She's	always	bossy	and	negative,	and
usually	not	much	fun	to	be	with	at	all.	When	she's	not	getting	enough	attention,
in	 certain	 social	 situations,	 the	 bitchy	 girl	 may	 also	 morph	 into	 an	 even	 less-
appealing	character:	“The	Cock-Block.”	She	might	be	one	of	the	most	physically
attractive	women	in	the	world,	but	once	she	starts	talking	and	gets	going,	she	can

be	terrible	to	be	around.	(Her	issues	are	probably	long	and	complex,	and	could
most-likely	 cover	 the	 course	 of	 an	 entire	 novel	 itself,	 so	 I'll	 refrain	 from
hypothesizing	about	them.)

However,	as	much	as	it	sucks	being	around	a	bitchy	girl	at	times,	if	you	do
somehow	manage	to	befriend	and	actually	take	a	liking	to	one,	you	could	be	in
for	 a	 surprising	 treat.	 Bitchy	 girls	 can	 sometimes	 be	 great	 in	 bed,	 and	 can	 get
very	sexual	when	it	comes	down	to	it.	For	various	reasons	(they	don’t	get	laid
enough,	they	hate	a	lot	of	guys,	they're	so	negative	to	be	around,	etc.),	they	can
actually	make	for	a	great	sexual	partner	and	a	unique	and	fun	experience.

Have	 you	 ever	 heard	 the	 fun,	 old	 children’s	 saying	 “I’d	 love	 to	 fuck	 the
bitchiness	 out	 of	 her!”?	 Well,	 that	 wise	 proverb	 came	 from	 someone	 dealing
with	one	of	these	lovely	ladies.

Beware:	 These	 women	 can	 be	 a	 real	 pain-in-the-ass,	 in	 all	 sorts	 of	 ways.
Usually	the	Debbie-Downer	and	Negative-Nancy	of	the	group,	the	bitchy	girl	is
not	one	to	seek	out.	She	often	carries	a	lot	of	psychological	baggage	as	well,	and
is	 usually	 not	 worth	 the	 trouble	 and	 effort	 involved	 in	 dating	 her—or	 for	 that
matter,	even	just	sleeping	with	her.	My	advice:	look	elsewhere	fast!

The	Career	Girl

The	Career	Girl	is	always	focused	on	her	career.	She	works	hard	and	studies
even	 harder.	 She's	 very	 smart	 and	 highly-sophisticated.	 The	 career	 girl	 is	 very
motivated	 and	 doesn't	 spend	 her	 time	 fruitlessly.	 She	 likes	 to	 keep	 busy,	 and
often	 has	 a	 hard	 time	 sitting	 still.	 Career	 girls	 make	 very	 good	 wives,	 because
they	 like	 to	 take	 care	 of	 a	 lot	 of	 things	 and	 make	 sure	 everything	 is	 in	 place
(making	 dinner,	 taking	 care	 of	 the	 kids,	 doing	 house-hold	 chores,	 etc.).	 Long
before	becoming	a	family	woman,	however,	the	career	girl	is	a	hardworking	and
relentless	career-focused	young	lady.	She	often	has	little	extra	time	on	her	hands,
and	can	be	a	bit	too	serious	about	life.

Though	very	bright	and	well-meaning,	career	girls	often	lack	interpersonal-
relationship	skills,	because	they've	focused	too	much	on	work	and	school.	Their
friendships	often	suffer	and	they	don't	like	to	go	out	much.	The	career	girl	might
be	perfect	for	the	career	guy	with	the	same	ambitions,	who	understands	that	her
work	will	usually	come	before	he	does.	Most	other	guys	will	have	a	hard	time
adjusting	to	this	work-first	mentality.

Beware:	The	career	girl	in	her	never-ending	quest	to	succeed	professionally
may	suffer	personally.	She	has	only	a	few	friends	and	little	spare	time	to	enjoy
life.	She's	very	intelligent,	but	almost	too	intelligent	for	her	own	good.	It	would
behoove	 her	 to	 take	 a	 break	 more	 often	 and	 enjoy	 the	 subtleties	 of	 life.	 Most
guys	 are	 turned	 off	 by	 her	 tunnel-vision	 focus	 on	 career	 success.	 Guys	 should
only	seek	a	career	girl	if	they	can	handle	the	little	time	she'll	have	for	them	and
the	fact	that	her	career	always	comes	first.

The	Shy	Girl

The	 Shy	 Girl	 is	 always	 very	 hard	 to	 figure	 out.	 Does	 she	 like	 me?	 Is	 she
feeling	me?	Is	she	bored	out	of	her	mind?	Does	she	think	I’m	a	weirdo?	These
are	all	questions	that	might	pop	into	your	head	when	dealing	with	the	shy	girl.
She’s	always	quite	reserved,	and	keeps	her	emotions	in	check.	It’s	hard	to	figure
out	 what	 she’s	 thinking.	 She’s	 shy,	 but	 you	 know	 that	 deep	 beneath	 that	 hard
shell	of	hers	lies	an	extrovert	ready	to	explode--she	just	has	to	feel	comfortable
with	 you	 first.	 She	 may	 let	 slip	 a	 hint	 from	 time	 to	 time	 giving	 you	 a	 brief,
fleeting	indicator	of	interest	in	the	form	of	a	smile	or	a	quick	chuckle.	Then	she'll
revert	back	to	being	shy	and	tough	to	read.

Many	times	shy	girls	can	be	the	best	lovers.	They	have	this	pent-up	bottle	of
emotions	within,	and	when	the	time	comes	to	let	loose,	boy	do	they	ever!	In	the
bedroom,	 once	 they're	 comfortable	 with	 you,	 they	 make	 great	 sexual	 partners.
They	 let	 themselves	 go	 and	 enjoy	 themselves,	 but	 only	 when	 they	 completely
trust	and	are	very	much	into	you.

Beware:	 Shy	 Girls	 are	 usually	 among	 the	 hardest	 women	 to	 figure	 out.
Though	they're	not	bad,	they	can	be	very	frustrating.	One	minute	you	think	she’s
digging	 you;	 the	 next,	 you	 think	 your	 attempts	 to	 woo	 her	 are	 completely	 in
vain!	 Beware	 giving	 up	 too	 soon	 on	 the	 shy	 girl	 during	 one	 of	 these	 times	 of
doubt.	 Often,	 with	 persistence	 and	 good	 game,	 shy	 girls	 will	 eventually	 come
around	 and	 end	 up	 giving	 you	 enough	 to	 work	 with.	 Though	 not	 easy,	 these
ladies	are	usually	worth	the	work	and	the	time.

The	Outgoing	Girl

The	Outgoing	Girl	is	always	easy	to	read.	She	wears	her	heart	on	her	sleeve
and	is	fun	to	be	around.	Games	are	not	typically	played	by	outgoing	girls,	unless
of	 course	 they	 find	 them	 being	 played	 by	 you.	 (Everyone	 plays	 the	 game	 in
general,	but	these	girls	tend	to	not	really	care	too	much	about	it.	It's	almost	as	if

they're	 above	 it	 all!)	 In	 which	 case	 these	 outgoing	 girls	 can	 definitely	 play	 all
kinds	of	games,	and	are	usually	quite	adept	at	it.

However,	most	of	the	time	the	outgoing	girl	is	very	confident	in	herself	and
just	fun	to	be	around.	She	loves	talking,	chatting,	laughing,	playing,	and	having	a
good	time	wherever	she	is.	She	usually	loves	dancing	and	singing	and	being	the
center	 of	 attention.	 Unlike	 the	 party	 girl,	 the	 outgoing	 girl	 doesn’t	 have	 to	 be
drunk	or	under	the	influence	of	any	kind	of	drug	to	be	loud	and	charismatic.	The
confidence	and	energy	that	emanates	from	the	outgoing	girl	is	very	attractive	and
much	desired	by	all	men.

Beware:	The	outgoing	girl	is	usually	very	opinionated	and	can	sometimes	be
controlling.	 She	 is	 very	 confident	 and	 knows	 it.	 However,	 she	 can	 border	 on
wanting	always	to	be	right	and	trying	to	control	all	situations,	all	the	time.	She
can	 be	 very	 annoying	 to	 a	 lot	 of	 guys,	 and	 is	 often	 too	 tough	 to	 handle.	 She
needs	a	very	strong,	dominant	man	to	handle	her,	or	a	man	who's	easygoing	and
willing	to	put	up	with	her	being	in	control	a	lot	of	the	time.	For	most	guys,	she	is
not	for	them.

The	Playing-Hard-To-Get	Girl

The	Playing-Hard-To-Get	Girl	is	always	very	sexy	and	attractive.	She	uses
the	 “dream	 girl”	 principle	 to	 elicit	 unbelievable	 amounts	 of	 attraction	 from	 the
guys	 who	 pursue	 her.	 She	 knows	 the	 concept	 of	 guys	 wanting	 what	 they	 can’t
have,	 and	 she	 uses	 this	 to	 her	 advantage.	 She	 often	 enjoys	 seeing	 guys	 jump
through	hoops	to	try	to	get	to	her,	which	may	even	turn	her	on.	Maybe	not	the
most	physically	attractive	of	the	types,	the	playing-hard-to-get	girl	makes	up	for
this	by	playing	the	game	so	well.	She	knows	exactly	what	to	say	and	what	to	do
to	push	the	attraction	switches	in	guys,	and	make	them	want	her	more	and	more.

Guys	 often	 fall	 for	 the	 mistake	 of	 trying	 to	 be	 the	 playing-hard-to-get	 guy
