with	this	kind	of	woman,	and	end	up	being	the	never-hear-from-her-again	guy.
They	can’t	play	this	girl’s	game	better	than	she	can.	She	is	a	master	at	it.	Instead,
they	 can	 play	 their	 own	 game,	 and	 allow	 her	 to	 unknowingly	 partake.	 This	 is
actually	the	only	true	way	to	get	these	types	of	girls.	All	other	attempts	will	only
end	in	disappointment.

Beware:	Though	sexy	and	enticing,	the	playing-hard-to-get	girl	can	often	be
very	 tough	 to	 get.	 She	 is	 very	 physically	 and	 emotionally	 draining.	 She	 loves
playing	games	and	doing	things	to	throw	you	off.	It’s	in	her	nature.	Sometimes

even	 the	 most	 seasoned	 seducers	 cannot	 figure	 these	 women	 out.	 That’s	 okay,
though.	 Sometimes	 they're	 just	 not	 meant	 to	 be	 figured	 out.	 (They	 may	 just	 be
playing	games,	and	not	actually	interested	at	all.	Who	knows,	some	girls	are	just
plain	crazy,	and	if	there	is	any	type	on	this	list	who	might	be	legitimately	crazy,
it’s	 the	 playing-hard-to-get	 girl.)	 Many	 a	 great	 man	 has	 fallen	 for	 the	 trap	 of
trying	to	get	a	hold	of	one	of	these	ladies,	only	to	figure	out	later	on	that	they
were	 just	 grasping	 at	 straws.	 The	 playing-hard-to-get	 girl	 is	 often	 the	 most
frustrating	type	of	girl	there	is,	so	you	must	always	remember	to	look	out	for	this
type.	If	you	find	yourself	grasping	at	straws	at	any	point,	move	on!

The	Perfect	Girl

The	 Perfect	 Girl	 is	 perfect	 in	 every	 way.	 She	 makes	 you	 feel	 unbelievable
when	you’re	around	her.	She	brings	a	smile	to	your	face	every	time	you	see	her.
Your	heart	jumps	every	time	she’s	near	you.	You	miss	her	when	you’re	away.
You	 think	 about	 her	 when	 you	 haven’t	 seen	 her	 for	 a	 while.	 She’s	 beautiful
inside	 and	 out,	 and	 invigorates	 you	 with	 every	 breath	 she	 draws.	 You	 can’t
imagine	your	life	without	her,	because	she	completes	everything	about	you.	She
compliments	you	in	every	way	and	brings	out	the	absolute	best	in	you.

You’re	funnier,	wittier,	kinder,	nicer,	more	charming,	more	outgoing,	more
charismatic,	and	more	alive	when	you’re	with	her.	She	is	the	absolute	best	that
every	other	type	of	woman	has	to	offer,	all	rolled	into	one.	You	can’t	think	about
any	 other	 woman	 when	 you’re	 with	 her;	 you	 can	 only	 think	 of	 why	 it	 took	 so
long	for	you	to	meet	her.	You	do	all	this	because	you	love	her	and	truly	care	for
her	 like	 no	 other.	 She	 is	 your	 one-and-only	 true	 soul	 mate	 in	 life,	 and	 she	 is
absolutely	perfect!

Beware:	 The	 perfect	 girl	 is	 hard	 to	 find.	 She's	 out	 there	 somewhere—
everyone	has	his	perfect	girl.	But	she	is	hard	to	find.	It	may	take	years	or	even
multiple	lifetimes	(if	you	believe	in	souls	and	reincarnation)	to	find	that	perfect
girl,	but	rest-assured	she's	out	there.	Just	keep	looking.

"Tomorrow	is	the	most	important	thing	in	life.
Comes	into	us	at	midnight	very	clean.
It's	perfect	when	it	arrives	and	it	puts	itself	in	our	hands.
It	hopes	we've	learned	something	from	yesterday."

-	John	Wayne

	Chapter	Fourteen

A	Woman's	Perspective	On	Meeting	Men

Back	when	I	was	writing	my	first	book,	I	wanted	to	figure	out	the	best	time
of	 day	 to	 approach	 women.	 I	 knew	 at	 the	 time,	 from	 my	 own	 experience,	 that
women	often	loved	being	stopped	during	the	day	and	chatted	up.	It	was	common
when	I	first	began	approaching	women	to	get	blown	out	when	I	approached	at
night,	but	pretty	rare	to	get	blown	out	during	the	day.	Of	course,	I	wasn’t	very
successful	 when	 I	 first	 started	 off—nobody	 really	 is—but	 the	 times	 were	 few
and	far	between	when	I	got	horribly	shut	down	during	the	day.	I	knew	there	was
something	to	this.

Women	 are	 expecting	 to	 be	 approached	 at	 night,	 and	 so	 they	 have	 their
guards	 up	 very	 high.	 It’s	 almost	 like	 they	 put	 their	 state-of-the-art	 security
systems	on	high-alert,	and	they	shut	you	down	as	soon	as	you	get	close.	It’s	sort
of	 contradictory	 in	 a	 way,	 because	 women	 are	 going	 out	 to	 meet	 and	 interact
with	men	and	have	a	good	time,	but	they	also	turn	away	a	lot	of	good	men	and
don’t	give	themselves	a	chance	to	have	it.

Yes,	quite	the	paradox	indeed.

During	 the	 writing	 of	 my	 first	 book,	 I	 created	 a	 fairly	 simple	 but	 effective
study	to	get	some	real-world	statistics	on	what	time	of	day	women	prefer	to	be
approached.	The	results	were	pretty	one-sided.	Approximately	70	percent	of	the
women	I	talked	to	preferred	meeting	men	during	the	day.	Yes,	that’s	right,	of	the
130	women	I	asked,	“What	time	of	day	do	your	prefer	to	meet	guys,	daytime	or
nighttime?”	91	of	them	said	they	preferred	the	daytime.

This	 is	 actually	 quite	 astonishing	 if	 you	 think	 about	 it.	 It’s	 almost	 like	 an
untapped	and	secret	way	of	meeting	women;	most	guys	never	approach	women
during	 the	 day!	 And	 women	 actually	 prefer	 that	 you	 approach	 them	 this	 way.
How	funny!	It’s	crazy,	but	true.

Now,	I	admit	that	the	survey	I	made	is	not	100	percent	reliable	and	true	for
every	woman,	but	it’s	still	a	pretty	good	sample-size,	and	the	fact	that	so	many
women	chose	the	daytime	does	reveal	a	lot	about	what	they	think.

I	had	some	follow-up	questions	for	these	women,	and	a	lot	of	them	told	me
the	reasons	why	they	don’t	like	meeting	men	at	night.	Some	of	the	answers	were
pretty	 obvious,	 while	 others	 were	 rather	 funny.	 Their	 reasons	 included:	 men
being	 too	 pushy,	 men	 being	 too	 drunk,	 not	 being	 able	 to	 have	 a	 good
conversation,	 men	 thinking	 the	 women	 wanted	 to	 hook	 up	 just	 because	 they
were	out	at	night,	men	treating	women	like	pieces	of	meat,	and	men	just	being
plain	sloppy.	These	are	all	major	turn-offs	for	women	and	a	lot	of	women	have
decided	that	meeting	sober	men	during	the	day	is	a	much	better	option.

For	the	guy	who	thinks	women	are	harder	to	meet	during	the	day,	I	urge	him
to	look	at	the	scientific	data	behind	this.	I'm	a	numbers	guy,	and	the	numbers	in
this	 case	 do	 not	 lie.	 If	 you’re	 not	 having	 success	 during	 the	 day,	 you	 may	 just
need	 to	 work	 on	 your	 approach	 and	 perfect	 the	 skill.	 There's	 obviously
something	throwing	your	chances	off,	so	a	bit	of	reflection	on	what	you’re	doing
right	or	wrong	would	be	best.

With	that	said,	however,	it	is	very	hard	to	be	successful	in	meeting	women
during	 the	 day.	 Just	 because	 women	 prefer	 a	 sober	 guy	 when	 the	 sun’s	 out,
doesn’t	 necessarily	 mean	 she'll	 prefer	 your	 sorry	 ass!	 Just	 kidding,	 she	 might
indeed	find	you	of	interest,	but	she	does	have	to	be	approached	the	right	way	in
order	to	feel	attraction	for	you.	(Continue	reading	this	book,	and	applying	what
you	learn!)

With	that	said,	I	do	love	going	out	at	night,	and	I	recommend	it	to	my	clients
all	the	time.	There's	nowhere	near	the	quantity	of	women	during	the	day	as	there
is	 at	 night,	 and	 the	 best	 way	 to	 learn	 game	 fast	 is	 to	 put	 yourself	 in	 situations
where	women	are	abundant.	Women	happen	to	be	most	abundant	after	the	sun
sets.

I	 like	 to	 say	 “Carpe	 Noctem”	 (“Seize	 the	 Night”)	 when	 it	 comes	 to	 going
out.	 Start	 approaching	 and	 having	 a	 great	 time	 when	 you	 go	 out	 at	 night.	 It’s
more	of	a	party	vibe	then,	and	you	can	easily	get	away	with	a	lot	more	in	this
kind	 of	 environment.	 Even	 if	 you	 do	 get	 rejected	 more	 or	 blown	 out	 more,	 it
doesn’t	matter	as	much;	you'll	be	learning	with	every	experience.

The	nighttime	is	also	best	for	working	on	your	direct	approach.	You	can	be	a
lot	more	edgy	and	outgoing,	because	women	are	a	lot	more	accustomed	to	this
type	of	approach.	(That	doesn’t	mean	be	a	dick!)	You	can	be	loud	and	bold	and
cocky,	and	get	away	with	saying	a	lot	of	risqué	things	at	night,	whereas	if	you

tried	these	things	during	the	day,	you'd	probably	just	get	your	ass	arrested!	It’s
more	accepted	at	night,	and	encouraged	by	the	party	atmosphere.

If	 you’re	 just	 starting	 off	 in	 “game”	 and	 trying	 to	 get	 better	 at
communicating	with	women,	definitely	go	out	both	times,	during	the	day	and	at
night.	Don’t	just	choose	one	or	the	other.	Work	on	your	indirect,	natural	game
during	the	day,	and	then	switch	on	your	outgoing	and	direct	game	at	night.

Both	day	game	and	night	game	are	equally	challenging	 in	their	own	 ways.
Day	 game	 presents	 the	 obstacles	 of	 starting	 completely	 random	 conversations,
with	women	who	are	typically	not	ready	to	meet	you.	Night	game	presents	the
major	obstacle	of	getting	past	the	high-tech	security	systems	most	women	have
in	place.	It	takes	time	to	see	results	in	either	setting,	but	much	less	time	if	you
practice	with	both.	What	you	learn	during	the	day	will	improve	your	night	game,
and	vice	versa.

Women	prefer	meeting	guys	during	the	day,	but	they'd	just	as	easily	enjoy
meeting	 a	 great	 guy	 at	 night.	 If	 you	 approach	 her,	 that	 guy	 could	 definitely	 be
you!

"To	the	mind	that	is	still,	the	whole	universe	surrenders."

-	Lao	Tzu

	Chapter	Fifteen

What	Not	To	Do

There	 are	 plenty	 of	 things	 to	 consider	 when	 you	 approach	 a	 woman.	 It’s
tough	as	it	is	to	remember	all	these	little	details,	not	to	mention	perfect	them.	But
as	 it	 turns	 out,	 following	 a	 list	 of	 what	 not	 to	 do	 when	 you	 approach	 might
actually	be	the	best	way	to	remember	what	you	should	do!

I	 wanted	 to	 compile	 a	 list	 of	 things	 to	 avoid	 when	 approaching	 women	 in
everyday	situations.	There	are	a	million	mistakes	I	see	guys	making	all	the	time,
but	 here's	 a	 list	 of	 some	 of	 the	 more	 common	 ones.	 By	 following	 this	 list	 of
things	to	avoid,	I	hope	I	can	give	you	some	insight	into	improving	your	approach
and	give	you	a	greater	chance	at	success.

So	without	further	ado,	I'd	like	to	give	you	the	“What	Not	to	Do”	checklist

of	things	to	avoid	when	you	approach	a	woman.

Coming	On	Too	Strong

This	could	 be	 applied	to	 guys	 approaching	at	 night	 just	as	 easily	 as	during
the	 day.	 Remember,	 a	 lot	 of	 the	 time	 guys	 at	 night	 can	 become	 offensive,	 and
feel	entitled	and	okay	with	saying	whatever	rude	or	repugnant	thing	that	pops	in
their	 heads.	 However,	 these	 guys	 are	 usually	 drunk	 and	 I’m	 not	 really	 talking
about	them	here.

No,	 I	 mean	 coming	 on	 too	 strong	 during	 the	 day,	 when	 you	 see	 a	 cute
woman	 walking	 on	 the	 street	 by	 herself,	 and	 you’ve	 been	 approaching	 women
all	day.

Women	want	a	guy	who	can	communicate	in	their	language.	If	you	are	way
too	 excited	 or	 way	 too	 loud	 (i.e.	 obnoxious),	 you're	 not	 going	 to	 be	 on	 her
current	emotional	level.	That’s	not	to	say	that	if	she	seems	down	you	can’t	bring
her	 up,	 but	 I	 think	 you	 get	 the	 point.	 If	 possible,	 you	 want	 to	 be	 slightly	 more
energetic	than	her.	Not	too	much,	or	you’ll	scare	her	off	or	creep	her	out,	but	just
enough.	Brighten	her	day	with	your	radiance,	don’t	blind	her	with	it.

Women,	 although	 preferring	 to	 meet	 guys	 during	 the	 day,	 are	 far	 from

expecting	 it.	 The	 act	 of	 you,	 a	 complete	 stranger,	 coming	 up	 and	 stopping	 her
can	be	slightly	intimidating	to	say	the	least	(especially	if	you’re	a	big	guy).	What
you	want	to	do	to	avoid	coming	on	too	strong	is	make	sure	you	never	sneak	up
behind	any	woman.	This	never	fails	to	completely	ruin	your	chances	with	them.

If	you’re	a	big	dude,	and	you	stop	a	lady	on	the	street,	that’s	scary	enough
for	her.	If	you	do	the	same	thing,	except	this	time	you	sneak	up	from	behind	her,
you’re	going	to	scare	the	shit	out	of	her!	So	try	to	avoid	this	whenever	possible.
Instead,	come	from	the	front	or	the	side,	and	make	yourself	visible	long	before
you	 get	 close.	 This	 allows	 her	 time	 to	 see	 you	 and	 process	 you	 entering	 her
world.

Avoiding	Eye	Contact

It’s	 easy	 to	 avoid	 eye	 contact	 when	 you’re	 nervous	 or	 unsure	 of	 what	 her
reaction	is	going	to	be	to	your	approach.	But	this	is	where	you	must	do	your	very
best	and	try	your	hardest	to	maintain	good	eye	contact.	Once	you	start	looking
down	 or	 away,	 she's	 going	 to	 subconsciously	 think	 you're	 inferior	 to	 her,	 and
subconsciously	 reject	 you,	 even	 before	 she	 consciously	 says,	 “No.”	 It’s	 one	 of
the	easiest	and	deadliest	pitfalls	to	approaching	women.	Avoid	this	at	all	costs.

Women	want	to	know	that	a	man	to	whom	they’re	talking	is	confident	and
sure	of	himself,	and	maintaining	eye	contact	is	one	of	the	easiest	ways	to	show
this.	“The	eyes	are	the	windows	to	the	soul”	as	the	great	proverb	states.

Using	Pick-Up	Lines

Most	 guys	 won’t	 use	 those	 over-the-top-cheesy	 pick-up	 lines	 like	 “How
much	 does	 a	 Polar	 Bear	 Weigh?”	 or	 something	 equally	 awful.	 However,	 guys
will	 use	 other	 pick-up	 lines	 from	 the	 Pick-Up	 Artist	 Community	 that	 are
similarly	ineffective.	They’ll	read	about	the	use	of	some	routine	or	line	from	a
new	 and	 cool	 pick-up	 artist	 and	 then	 decide	 that	 this	 works.	 It	 rarely,	 if	 ever,
does.

For	one	thing,	it	usually	doesn’t	work	because	the	person	who	created	it	was
using	 it	 for	 himself,	 in	 the	 moment;	 it	 applied	 to	 that	 particular	 situation,	 but
none	 other.	 Trying	 to	 transfer	 that	 line	 and	 situation	 into	 what	 you’re	 doing	 is
just	not	a	good	idea.	It	won't	be	in	the	moment,	nor	will	it	be	relevant	to	what
you're	 doing.	 Secondly,	 it	 won't	 be	 genuine,	 since	 it's	 not	 really	 coming	 from
you,	but	from	some	pick-up	guru	on	the	internet.	Women	can	easily	sense	this

spuriousness.

This	 is	 why	 I	 never	 recommend	 using	 lines.	 Instead,	 I	 give	 examples	 of
things	 that	 work	 and	 lines	 that	 I’d	 say;	 never	 do	 I	 recommend	 that	 you	 copy
what	I	say	word-for-word.	It’s	just	not	going	to	be	anywhere	near	as	effective	as
you	coming	up	with	something	on	your	own.

Trying	To	Be	Cool

It’s	hard	to	be	playful	and	goofy	with	someone	you’ve	just	met.	Especially	if
that	 someone	 is	 a	 smoking-hot	 woman.	 However,	 I	 would	 speculate	 that	 being
goofy	is	ten	times	better	than	being	cool	when	meeting	women.	Trying	to	be	too
cool	 for	 school	 and	 being	 the	 bad-ass	 guy	 who	 acts	 like	 he’s	 The	 Man	 is	 not
attractive.	It	shows	women	that	you	aren't	comfortable	being	yourself,	but	must
instead	put	on	a	front	and	pretend	to	be	awesome.

Instead,	 be	 goofy.	 Be	 funny	 and	 playful	 and	 enjoy	 yourself.	 Be	 more
genuine	to	who	you	really	are,	and	stop	pretending	to	be	the	perfect,	cool	guy	in
the	 movies.	 Nobody	 is	 like	 this!	 Women	 would	 be	 much	 more	 comfortable
around	 a	 guy	 who’s	 laughing	 and	 joking	 instead	 of	 a	 serious	 and	 stone-faced
guy.	Be	the	former.

Coming	In	Too	Weak

Coming	 in	 too	 weak	 can	 be	 easy	 to	 do,	 especially	 for	 the	 newbie.	 To
approach	and	effectively	attract	a	beautiful,	random	woman	you	see,	you'll	need
to	come	in	and	open	her	with	a	certain	bravado.	Going	in	half-assed	and	trying	to
be	 cool	 or	attractive	just	isn’t	going	to	 cut	it.	 You	have	to	think	 of	yourself	 as
being	 a	 dominant,	 almost	 cavemanish	 figure	 (if	 you	 seem	 to	 be	 one	 of	 these
weak	approachers,	that	is)	and	come	in	much	stronger.

Bring	 up	 your	 confidence	 and	 bring	 up	 your	 audacity,	 for	 chrissakes!	 Be
bold	and	don’t	be	afraid	to	challenge	her	and	be	in	her	face.	If	you’re	coming	in
too	 weak,	 you	 have	 to	 either	 warm	 up	 better	 because	 you’re	 not	 100	 percent
ready	to	do	approaches,	or	completely	change	your	mindset	(because	you’re	still
shy	and	or	timid	by	nature).

A	mindset	shift	in	the	latter	case	is	a	must	in	order	to	see	success.	It	can	be
done,	however,	so	if	this	seems	like	you,	don't	fret.	In	fact,	when	I	first	started
this	was	definitely	me.	It	took	time,	but	I	was	able	to	stop	coming	in	so	weak,
being	timid	and	shy	about	approaching.	(Now	I	have	to	tone	things	down	a	bit	at

times,	and	guard	against	coming	in	too	strong.)

Having	Low	Energy

Having	 low	 energy	 when	 you're	 talking	 to	 a	 woman	 just	 completely	 kills
your	chances	of	being	successful	with	her.	No	woman,	and	I	mean	absolutely	no
one,	 wants	 to	 be	 with	 a	 boring,	 tired	 and	 unexciting	 man.	 Women	 crave
excitement,	 enthusiasm,	 and	 energy!	 We	 all	 do.	 If	 you	 are	 not	 on	 her	 level,
energy-wise,	she's	going	to	be	turned	off	immediately.

Having	 low	 energy	 goes	 hand-in-hand	 with	 coming	 in	 too	 weak.	 It’s
important	 to	 be	 wary	 of	 this,	 and	 to	 stop	 your	 low	 energy	 approaches	 in	 their
tracks	when	you	get	them.	A	quick	espresso	might	be	in	order,	or	just	a	break	for
a	few	minutes	to	relax	and	refocus.

If	 you	 notice	 that	 after	 a	 while	 (at	 least	 an	 hour,	 more	 likely	 a	 few	 hours)
you’re	 starting	 to	 have	 blander	 approaches,	 you	 should	 probably	 take	 a	 break
and	just	rest	up	for	5-10	minutes.	Approaching	women	can	be	very	tiresome,	and
it	can	eventually	take	a	physical	toll,	whether	you	recognize	it	or	not.	This	break
refreshes	and	recharges	you,	and	gets	rid	of	the	low	energy	you're	emitting.	It’s
like	 charging	 up	 a	 battery	 so	 it	 has	 more	 juice	 to	 perform.	 You	 can	 think	 of
yourself	 as	 this	 battery,	 and	 the	 approaches	 as	 the	 performance	 you	 want	 to
boost.

Caring	Too	Much	About	Other	People

As	a	natural	introvert,	I	typically	live	in	my	head.	I	think	and	re-think	a	lot	of
the	 things	 that	 occur	 in	 my	 life.	 I'm	 also	 very	 aware	 of	 other	 people	 and	 often
consider	their	feelings	and	opinions	ahead	of	my	own.	This	can	be	a	good	thing
when	 it	 comes	 to	 being	 a	 nice	 person;	 most	 introverts	 are	 great	 and	 caring
people.	 But	 it	 can	 also	 be	 a	 huge	 detriment	 if	 you	 care	 too	 much	 about	 what
others	think,	especially	in	something	like	the	dating	field.

When	you	approach	women	you	should	be	thinking	only	about	yourself	and
the	 girl	 you’re	 talking	 to.	 All	 others	 should	 be	 blocked	 out.	 What	 introverts,
myself	included,	tend	to	do	at	times	is	think	too	much	about	what	other	people
are	thinking.	We	tend	to	want	to	please	the	people	around	us,	as	opposed	to	just
pleasing	 ourselves.	 Extroverts	 usually	 don’t	 have	 this	 problem,	 because	 they're
naturally	 attuned	 to	 communicating	 with	 others	 and	 being	 comfortable
expressing	 themselves	 more	 outwardly.	 But	 when	 it	 comes	 to	 the	 introverted

community	 (up	 to	 half	 the	 population,	 by	 some	 estimates),	 the	 community	 of
people	 who	 aren't	 as	 comfortable	 expressing	 themselves	 outwardly,	 this
challenge	of	approaching	a	woman	can	be	very	difficult.

We	don’t	feel	comfortable	being	the	center	of	attention,	especially	when	it’s
something	as	daring	as	hitting	on	a	woman	in	public!	We	think	of	how	to	avoid
this	social	pressure,	how	to	appease	the	crowd	of	potential	onlookers,	and	how	to
talk	to	this	woman	before	us	without	feeling	uncomfortable.	Well,	I’m	here,	as	a
reformed	introvert,	to	tell	you	to	stop	doing	this!

It’s	one	of	the	hardest	things	to	do,	but	it	must	be	done.	Try	to	have	tunnel
vision	 when	 you	 approach	 a	 woman,	 and	 forget	 about	 the	 onlookers	 or	 the
passers-by.	 They	 don’t	 matter	 and	 they	 never	 will.	 All	 that	 matters	 is	 you	 and
your	 life.	 Focus	 on	 your	 desires,	 and	 let	 those	 others	 watch	 you	 make	 your
dreams	come	true.	Let	them	think	about	you	,	don’t	think	about	them!

Waiting	Around	Too	Long

Waiting	around	too	long	before	you	approach	is	like	a	death	sentence.	I	used
to	do	this	all	the	time.	I'd	see	a	beautiful	woman	nearby	and	get	nervous	about
going	up	to	her.	Then	I'd	wait	around	thinking	of	the	perfect	thing	to	say.	I	didn’t
want	to	say	something	stupid,	and	I	didn’t	have	the	courage	to	just	go	in	and	try
something.	 Instead,	 I'd	 wait	 back	 and	 watch	 her	 trying	 to	 think	 of	 something
clever.	.	.

What	always	happened	was	I	never	came	up	with	anything.	Nothing!	Ever!

Instead,	what	would	happen	is	I'd	eventually	force	myself	into	going	up	to
talk	to	her,	after	waiting	around	for	too	many	awkward	moments	(	by	this	point,
she'd	of	course	have	noticed	me,	looking	at	her	not	so	inconspicuously).	But	by
this	time	it	was	far	too	late.	With	each	step	I	took	closer	to	her,	she	was	already
positioning	herself	to	reject	me.

The	closer	I	got,	the	more	I	could	sense	this.	It	was	like	a	Spidey-Sense	that
went	 off	 inside	 me.	 I	 was	 literally	 just	 walking	 into	 a	 death	 trap,	 but	 by	 now
there	was	nothing	I	could	do.	Actually,	I	let	myself	commit	this	social	suicide,	so
that	I	could	learn	from	these	feelings	and	try	to	avoid	them	next	time.	And	I	did.

Now	I	hardly	ever	fall	into	the	trap	of	waiting	too	long.	If	I	see	a	woman	I
might	like,	I	go	for	it	right	away.	The	longer	you	wait,	the	greater	your	chances
of	failing	become!

"I	dwell	in	possibility."

-	Emily	Dickinson

	Chapter	Sixteen

Charisma	Is	King

In	the	internet	blogging	world,	there’s	a	pretty	common	saying:	“Content	is
King.”	I’ve	heard	this	so	many	times	from	so	many	different	people.	It’s	said	so
much	because	it’s	true.	The	more	content	you	have,	the	better	off	your	blog	or
website	 will	 be.	 The	 more	 content,	 i.e.	 the	 more	 information	 you	 bring	 to	 the
table,	the	better	your	website	is	and	therefore	the	better	your	online	presence	is,
thus	making	you	a	king	.

In	the	dating	world,	charisma	is	king.	The	more	charisma	you	bring	to	the
dating	 scene,	 the	 better	 you	 will	 perform	 and	 the	 more	 successful	 you	 will	 be
with	women.	Therefore,	the	more	charisma	you	have,	the	more	of	a	king	you’ll
become	in	this	domain.

Nowhere	in	the	dating	world	is	having	charisma	more	important	than	in	the
approaching	facet.	Having	charisma	when	you	approach	women	is	like	having	a
Shelby	 Cobra	 in	 a	 1960s	 drag	 race.	 You’re	 working	 with	 the	 greatness	 in	 this
case,	and	the	perfect	tool	to	not	only	succeed	but	to	do	incredible	things.

Charisma	 isn’t	 just	 something	 you’re	 born	 with.	 Sure,	 a	 lot	 of	 people	 are
naturally	extroverted	and	tend	to	be	naturally	good	at	expressing	themselves.	But
this	doesn’t	necessarily	mean	they're	charismatic	when	they	do	so.	Just	because
you're	 outgoing	 doesn’t	 mean	 you're	 captivating,	 which	 is	 what	 charismatic
people	are.	Charisma	is	magnetic	and	contagious.	It’s	like	an	addictive	drug	and
people	surrounding	the	charismatic	person	want	more.

Charisma	 sucks	 you	 in	 like	 a	 good	 movie.	 When	 we	 watch	 movies—a
drama,	 where	 the	 main	 characters	 have	 a	 lot	 of	 dialogue—the	 reason	 we're	 so
absorbed	in	what	is	going	on	is	the	actors	are	emanating	so	much	charisma.	They
are	 so	 good	 at	 turning	 on	 that	 charisma	 switch,	 they	 completely	 fool	 us	 into
believing	 wholeheartedly	 that	 what	 they	 are	 doing	 (acting)	 is	 real.	 We	 fool
ourselves	into	believing	that	what	we're	seeing	is	real,	and	that	the	drama	going
on	is	actually	taking	place.	This	allows	us	to	be	immersed	in	and	entertained	by
what's	happening.	It's	all	possible	because	of	the	charisma	and	liveliness	of	the
actors	playing	the	roles.

Imagine	 if	 the	 actors	 in	 your	 favorite	 movies	 didn’t	 have	 so	 much	 raw
emotion,	energy,	and	enthusiasm	when	they	performed.	Go	ahead,	picture	your
favorite	 movies	 right	 now,	 and	 some	 of	 the	 best	 parts	 in	 them.	 (Let’s	 see
Goodfellas,	 when	 Henry	 Hill	 is	 beating	 up	 his	 neighbor.	 Or	 The	 Godfather,
when	 Michael	 Corleone	 goes	 into	 the	 restaurant	 and	 murders	 the	 gangster	 and
crooked	cop.	And	oh	yeah,	Raging	Bull,	when	Jake	La	Motta	fights	Sugar	Ray
Robinson.	 I	 know,	 these	 are	 all	 pretty	 violent	 movies,	 but	 they're	 some	 of	 my
favorites,	and	actually	some	of	the	best	rated	movies	of	all	time!).	Now	picture
these	 scenes	 without	 the	 charismatic	 and	 unbelievably	 talented	 actors	 playing
them.	 Can	 you	 picture	 a	 lifeless	 Pacino,	 a	 boring	 De	 Niro,	 or	 a	 tired-looking
Liotta	in	any	of	these	action-filled	and	high-intensity	scenes?	Of	course	not!	If
that	were	the	case,	all	three	of	these	movies	(and	all	of	the	movies	you	thought
of)	would	have	completely	sucked!

It’s	 all	 about	 the	 allure	 of	 the	 actors	 who	 play	 in	 the	 movie.	 These	 are	 the
people	who	make	or	break	it.	Why	do	you	think	that	studios	pay	millions	upon
millions	of	dollars	to	snag	up	particular	actors	for	their	new	flicks?	Is	it	because
they're	 boring	 and	 lifeless?	 Of	 course	 not!	 It’s	 because	 they	 have	 unbelievable
charisma,	and	can	transform	that	charisma	onto	the	big-screen,	and	in	turn	make
the	 studio-heads	 millions	 of	 dollars	 more	 in	 profit.	 Charisma	 is	 like	 a	 magnet,
and	 it	 literally	 attracts	 people	 and	 convinces	 them	 to	 watch	 those	 movies.
Charisma	is	a	skill	these	actors	have	mastered,	and	it’s	a	skill	that	you	too	can
master.

Great	 public	 speakers	 have	 unbelievable	 amounts	 of	 charisma.	 Think	 of
Jordan	 Belfort	 or	 Tony	 Robbins.	 Like	 the	 great	 actors,	 they've	 harnessed	 this
ability	to	be	magnetic	and	attractive.	When	someone	like	Belfort,	“The	Wolf	of
Wall	Street“(another	great	flick,	by	the	way),	speaks,	he	immediately	grabs	the
attention	of	a	roomful	of	listeners.	Go	on	YouTube	when	you	get	a	chance	and
watch	one	of	his	speaking	seminars.	The	guy	is	amazing.	It’s	easy	to	see	why	he
was	 such	 a	 great	 salesman,	 and	 why	 it	 was	 so	 easy	 for	 him	 to	 fool	 so	 many
people	(actually	stealing	and	defrauding	millions	of	dollars	from	them).

He	quite	honestly	could	have	talked	people	into	walking	off	a	bridge	if	he'd
wanted	to.	All	they	would	have	said	was,	“Where,	and	when	do	I	go?”	I	mean
this	guy	is	influential!	He	has	such	a	great	stage	presence;	when	he	speaks,	he
animates	 his	 words	 and	 captivates	 his	 audience.	 Just	 by	 watching	 him	 perform
you	can	learn	a	lot.	You	could	start	by	imitating	and	copying	some	of	the	things

he	does.	It	helps	to	learn	from	someone	like	this	.	.	.	just	don’t	try	to	imitate	his
criminal	tendencies!	That’ll	land	your	ass	in	the	slammer!

A	 great	 way	 to	 start	 working	 on	 your	 charisma	 is	 to	 practice	 speaking	 in
front	 of	 a	 mirror.	 It	 might	 sound	 crazy,	 and	 you	 might	 look	 crazy	 to	 someone
walking	by	if	they	happen	to	see	you,	but	it	works.	Watching	yourself	and	seeing
how	 you	 communicate	 gives	 you	 great	 feedback	 on	 the	 way	 you	 look	 and
present	yourself.	You	can	also	video-record	yourself,	which	is	what	I	always	do
when	practicing	a	speech.	I	like	to	record	myself,	and	make	sure	to	pick	up	on
what	I’m	doing	right	and	what	I	need	to	work	on.	By	doing	this,	you’ll	see	little
things	you	can	do	to	improve	your	charisma.

Being	 animated	 is	 always	 a	 great	 way	 to	 have	 more	 charisma.	 Expressing
yourself	 by	 using	 your	 hands	 and	 body	 gestures	 is	 great	 for	 powerful
communication.	You	can	work	on	these	gestures	in	front	of	the	mirror,	getting
them	to	fit	you	and	what	you	are	saying.	The	more	you	do	it,	tweaking	the	little
gestures	here	and	there,	the	more	natural	these	gestures	will	become.

Winking	 for	 example,	 can	 help	 improve	 your	 confidence	 and	 charisma.	 If
you	practice	winking	all	the	time	and	practice	your	wink	in	front	of	a	mirror,	you
can	start	to	feel	comfortable	winking	at	a	woman.	I	know	it’s	a	little	cheesy,	but
a	confident	wink	can	actually	go	a	long	way.	A	wink	from	a	guy	(if	done	in	a
funny	manner)	can	be	a	huge	display	of	confidence	to	a	woman.	Not	too	many
guys	 can	 actually	 pull	 off	 a	 good	 wink;	 by	 doing	 so,	 you	 demonstrate	 a	 high
amount	of	value.	Trust	me	on	this	one.	It	may	seem	corny,	but	winking	is	very
useful	in	certain	situations.

It	may	be	hard	to	wink	at	a	very	attractive	woman	at	first,	just	as	it	might	be
hard	getting	that	woman’s	number.	Like	anything	else,	though,	the	more	you	do
it,	 the	 easier	 it	 gets	 and	 the	 more	 comfortable	 you	 become	 with	 it.	 Start	 by
winking	 at	 women	 you	 don't	 find	 so	 attractive,	 when	 you	 tell	 a	 joke	 or
something.	 Then	 gradually	 start	 doing	 it	 to	 cuter	 and	 cuter	 girls	 until	 you
actually	 start	 to	 feel	 more	 comfortable	 doing	 it.	 When	 the	 time	 comes	 that	 a
really	 attractive	 girl	 does	 something	 and	 you	 want	 to	 wink	 at	 her,	 it	 will	 be	 so
much	easier	to	do	so,	and	you	can	deliver	your	new	trademark	move!

But	that’s	enough	on	winking	;).

Your	tone	of	voice	can	also	affect	your	charisma	in	a	major	way.	When	you
express	and	emphasize	different	words,	you	draw	your	audience	in.	It	naturally

grabs	people’s	attention	when	your	voice	shifts	from	one	volume	to	another.	It’s
like	an	internal	alarm	that	goes	off	in	our	ears	when	we	hear	a	change	of	voice
tone.	 Great,	 charismatic	 speakers	 know	 exactly	 how	 to	 alter	 their	 voices	 and
tones	 to	 keep	 their	 audience	 engaged.	 (You	 can	 record	 yourself	 and	 stand	 in
front	of	a	mirror	for	this	one	as	well.)

It	helps	to	hear	yourself	and	look	at	how	you	sound	saying	different	things.
Just	don’t	get	too	caught	up	on	the	way	you	sound.	Most	people	actually	hate	the
way	they	sound,	because	we	hear	ourselves	slightly	different	than	the	rest	of	the
world	does.	If	you	feel	like	you	sound	a	little	bad,	don’t	worry.	We	all	think	we
sound	bad,	when	most	of	the	time	we	actually	don’t	(unless	you're	Paul	Reubens,
he	always	sounds	bad!).

The	hands-down	best	way	to	develop	charisma	when	talking	to	women	is	.	.	.
talking	to	more	women!	The	more	you	talk	to,	the	more	comfortable	you	become
with	them.	This	is	the	best	way	to	get	feedback,	and	observe	what’s	working	and
what’s	 not	 for	 you.	 There	 is	 really	 no	 other	 way	 to	 learn	 than	 to	 talk	 to	 more
women.	Just	by	doing	this,	you'll	develop	an	innate	level	of	charm,	because	your
body	will	come	up	with	its	natural	way	of	communicating	in	the	most	effective
way.	This	effective,	natural,	and	time-tested	technique	is	crafted	in	the	form	of
charisma.	It’s	been	king	since	man	was	born!

"The	best	way	out	is	always	through."

-	Robert	Frost

	Chapter	Seventeen

The	10,000	Hour	Rule

There’s	a	book	by	Malcolm	Gladwell	called	Outliers	that	talks	about	how	it
takes	 10,000	 hours	 of	 practice	 to	 become	 a	 master	 at	 any	 particular	 skill.	 Of
course,	Tim	Ferriss	might	have	you	believe	differently,	since	he’s	able	to	short-
circuit	the	time	it	takes	to	learn	new	skills,	with	all	sorts	of	different	clever	and
innovative	techniques.	He’s	managed	to	save	time	on	things	that	ordinarily	took
years	to	learn—which	in	and	of	itself	is	amazing.	But	even	so,	just	because	he’s
learned	 to	 “cheat”	 the	 normal	 learning	 system	 and	 save	 time	 in	 learning	 new
skills,	 that	 doesn’t	 mean	 Gladwell	 was	 wrong,	 or	 that	 his	 10,000	 hour	 rule	 is
incorrect.

If	 you	 spend	 10,000	 hours	 doing	 something,	 you	 will	 certainly	 master	 it!
(Look	 no	 further	 than	 the	 greatest	 rock	 &	 roll	 band	 in	 history,	 The	 Beatles.)	 I
used	to	think	this	was	complete	B.S.,	until	I	started	approaching	women	.	.	.

Looking	 back,	 this	 theory	 seems	 to	 be	 absolutely	 spot-on.	 There	 are	 a	 few
things	 I'd	 say	 I’m	 a	 “master”	 at,	 or	 at	 the	 very	 least	 proficient	 with,	 in	 life.
Thinking	about	it	now,	I’d	say	I	definitely	spent	at	least	10,000	hours	practicing
each	of	these	skills.	There	are	also	a	lot	of	things	I	wanted	to	pick	up	over	the
years;	however,	looking	back,	I	just	never	dedicated	quite	enough	time.	On	the
contrary,	I’m	not	a	master	at	these	things—I’m	rather	terrible	at	them.	Cooking,
swimming,	and	dancing	all	come	to	mind.

I’m	great	at	baseball.	I	was	one	of	the	best	players	in	the	city	where	I	grew
up.	It’s	no	coincidence	that	I'd	hit	baseballs	for	hours	and	hours	at	a	time	every
day	after	school,	between	the	ages	of	7	and	16.	This	is	why	I	always	made	the
all-star	team	and	consistently	out-performed	many	of	the	kids	my	age,	who	had
equal	if	not	more	athletic	ability	than	I	did.

I’m	also	a	good	writer.	(I	hope	you	can	agree	by	this	point	in	the	book!	If
not,	 it’s	 okay;	 I	 like	 my	 writing.)	 I’ve	 been	 writing	 short	 stories	 and	 reading
books	(a	natural	love	of	mine)	since	I	was	6,	and	I	do	so	now,	nearly	20	years
later.	I’ve	always	had	a	way	with	words,	but	that	was	only	because	I	was	always
reading	and	writing	them,	getting	in	my	practice.	I	mastered	this	skill	and	put	in

my	10,000	hours	.	.	.	many,	many	years	ago.

I’m	 not	 however	 great	 at	 cooking.	 Or	 speaking	 Spanish.	 Or	 juggling.	 Or
playing	 guitar.	 Or	 swimming.	 Or	 many,	 many	 other	 things	 I’ve	 tried	 over	 the
years.	Whether	because	I	lacked	the	patience	or	the	passion,	I	gave	up	on	a	lot	of
these	things	and	came	up	far	too	short	in	the	10,000	hours	of	practice.	In	fact,	the
closest	 I'd	 say	 I’ve	 come	 on	 any	 of	 them,	 if	 I	 had	 to	 make	 an	 educated	 guess,
would	be	playing	guitar;	I'd	say	I’ve	practiced	that	in	the	600-900	hour	range,	or
less	 than	 10	 percent	 of	 where	 I'd	 need	 to	 be	 in	 order	 to	 master	 that	 skill.	 This
would	precisely	explain	why	I	can	only	play	a	few	chords,	and	not	very	well.

When	 it	 comes	 to	 learning	 how	 to	 communicate	 with	 women	 however,	 I'd
say	I’ve	definitely	eclipsed	the	10,000-hour	plateau,	several	years	back.	If	I	had
to	add	up	all	the	hours	I’ve	been	approaching,	dating,	speaking,	communicating,
and	sleeping	with	women,	and	just	being	around	them,	it	would	certainly	add	up
to	 well	 over	 10,000	 hours	 (which	 is	 416	 days,	 by	 the	 way,	 just	 over	 one	 full
year).	 This	 fact	 makes	 me	 an	 expert	 in	 communicating	 with	 them.	 I	 know
exactly	 how	 to	 communicate	 with	 women	 and	 exactly	 how	 to	 attract	 them,
because	I’ve	spent	so	long	perfecting	this	skill.	It’s	not	something	I’m	trying	to
boast	about,	it’s	just	the	truth.	Like	anything	else,	if	you	dedicate	the	time—in
this	case	10,000	hours	of	it—you	too	will	become	a	master.

Admittedly,	 I	 have	 not	 approached	 for	 10,000	 hours.	 Nor	 do	 I	 really	 ever
want	to.	I	also	don’t	think	there	are	that	many	people	who	have	done	this.	If	you
think	about	it,	that	would	be	over	one	full	year	of	continuously	approaching	and
stopping	 women.	 There	 are	 guys	 who	 might	 claim	 they’ve	 done	 this,	 because
they	 can	 claim	 that	 they’ve	 been	 coaching	 for	 years	 and	 years,	 but	 actually
approaching	 women,	 non-stop	 and	 without	 taking	 breaks	 for	 416	 days,	 is	 just
very	hard	to	believe.	It	is	possible.	I	just	don’t	think	too	many	have	done	it.

No	 matter,	 though,	 the	 point	 is	 the	 more	 you	 do	 something	 and	 the	 closer
you	get	to	reaching	this	10,000	hour	threshold,	the	better	you	will	be	in	whatever
skill	you're	trying	to	learn.	It’s	not	like	you	have	to	reach	that	10,000-hour	mark
and	then	you’ll	be	good.	Of	course	not.	You'll	be	getting	good	long	before	that,
maybe	 around	 the	 first	 couple	 thousand	 hours;	 everything	 after	 that	 is	 gravy.
Anything	 above	 nothing	 makes	 you	 closer	 to	 reaching	 your	 goals.	 So	 don’t	 be
discouraged	 if	 you	 feel	 like	 you	 have	 a	 long	 way	 to	 go.	 You	 might,	 but	 it’s
certainly	not	as	long	as	416	days	of	non-stop	training!

The	best	advice	I	can	give	is	to	be	patient	and	keep	that	passion,	unlike	with
some	 of	 the	 things	 I’ve	 given	 up	 over	 the	 years.	 (I	 didn’t	 care	 much	 about
juggling	so	I	gave	it	up.)	I	do	care	about	playing	guitar,	however,	which	is	why
I'm	back	at	it	now.	Keeping	the	patience	is	tough	but	necessary.

It	may	seem	easy	to	just	give	in	and	quit	when	the	going	gets	tough,	but	with
patience,	the	ultimate	virtue,	you	must	keep	on	trying.	Nothing	good	ever	comes
easy,	 and	 getting	 great	 with	 meeting	 and	 attracting	 women	 is	 definitely	 no
exception.	So	keeping	a	positive,	open	mind	is	essential!

As	far	as	keeping	the	passion	for	approaching,	use	your	lack	of	success	with
women	 as	 a	 motivation	 to	 succeed.	 Etch	 a	 picture	 in	 your	 mind	 of	 yourself	 50
years	from	now.	Do	you	want	to	be	alone	and	sad	that	you	missed	out	on	life,	or
do	you	want	to	have	a	big	smile	on	your	face,	with	grandkids	at	your	feet,	and	a
loving	 wife	 by	 your	 side?	 Keep	 this	 image	 in	 your	 mind	 and	 think	 about	 the
future	you	want	to	make	for	yourself.	The	life	you	want	to	live	is	open	to	you,
you	just	have	to	work	for	it.

Keep	a	positive	and	fun	outlook	when	meeting	women	and	the	passion	will
stay	 with	 you.	 The	 rest	 will	 take	 care	 of	 itself.	 You	 might	 never	 reach	 that
10,000	hours	of	approaching	mastery,	and	I	probably	won’t,	either,	but	we	will
learn	plenty	while	trying	to	get	there!

"Once	we	believe	in	ourselves,
We	can	risk	curiosity,	wonder,	spontaneous	delight,
Or	any	experience	that	reveals	the	human	spirit."

-	E.	E.	Cummings

	Chapter	Eighteen

Eliminating	Approach	Anxiety

Many	 years	 back	 when	 I	 was	 my	 former,	 shy,	 lonely,	 and	 even	 depressed
young	 self,	 I	 often	 had	 panic	 attacks	 and	 constant	 anxiety.	 I	 was	 scared	 of
everything	 back	 then.	 I	 was	 anxious	 about	 having	 no	 friends.	 I	 was	 anxious
about	my	looks.	I	was	anxious	about	having	bad	grades	and	getting	into	trouble.
I	 was	 so	 anxious	 and	 afraid	 back	 then,	 my	 own	 shadow	 could	 have	 scared	 the
hell	out	of	me—I’d	probably	have	thought	it	was	a	ghost!

But	being	the	way	I	was,	a	naturally	determined	and	motivated	person,	I	set
out	to	conquer	all	my	fears.	I	began	by	researching	how	to	eliminate	the	worst	of
all	 fears,	 the	 panic	 attack	 .	 There	 were	 a	 few	 methods	 I	 came	 across,	 but	 I
ultimately	 decided	 I	 wanted	 to	 try	 an	 approach	 that	 looked	 the	 safest,	 one	 that
avoided	drugs,	and	one	that	I	could	do	on	my	own.

I	 discovered	 a	 book	 around	 this	 point	 that	 would	 change	 my	 life	 forever.
That	 book	 was	 called	 Panic	 Away	 by	 Joe	 Barry.	 This	 book	 focused	 on	 the
concept	of	eliminating	panic	attacks	completely	(thus	the	name).	It	was	a	short
book,	and	I	read	it	all	very	quickly.

The	 message	 it	 gave	 me	 was	 simple	 but	 unbelievably	 powerful.	 In	 fact,	 it
may	very	well	be	the	most	powerful	idea	I’ve	ever	come	across,	in	all	my	life!
Why	 is	 that?	 How	 could	 one	 simple	 message	 be	 so	 powerful,	 you	 ask?	 Well,
because	this	message	directly	shows	you	how	to	fight	the	most	powerful	emotion
there	is	.	.	.	fear.

It’s	probably	something	you’ve	never	even	considered	doing.	In	fact,	when	I
first	 read	 it,	 I	 thought	 it	 was	 totally	 insane.	 I	 thought	 there	 was	 some	 type	 of
misprint	 in	 the	 book,	 because	 what	 it	 was	 advising	 me	 to	 do	 was	 so	 utterly
counter-intuitive.	 Yet	 the	 more	 I	 thought	 about	 it,	 the	 more	 it	 actually	 made
sense	and	seemed	to	be	quite	plausible.

And	so,	a	few	short	days	later,	I	tried	it	out	when	I	had	my	next	panic	attack,

and	that’s	when	I	knew	for	sure	this	thing	worked.

What	 the	 Panic	 Away	 book	 told	 the	 reader	 to	 do	 was	 .	 .	 .	 challenge	 your

fears	 .	 Not	 be	 afraid	 and	 run	 away	 from	 your	 fears,	 because	 that	 only	 makes
them	worse,	but	actually	call	on	and	ask	for	more	fear.	Yes,	that’s	right,	when
you	are	getting	a	panic	attack,	you	are	to	recognize	the	fears	coming	up,	embrace
the	anxious	feelings,	and	then,	ask	for	more	.

I’m	sorry,	I	don’t	mean	ask	for	more	fear,	but	DEMAND	it!	Demand	more
fear,	 and	 then	 challenge	 it.	 Whatever	 the	 crazy	 thoughts	 rushing	 through	 your
head	 may	 be,	 demand	 that	 you	 have	 more	 of	 them!	 (Of	 course,	 this	 internal
dialogue	is	all	going	on	in	your	head,	between	you	and	your	worst	fears.	That’s
the	source	of	the	anxiety	and	panic	anyway;	it’s	always	internal,	and	it’s	always
coming	from	a	place	within	yourself.)	By	doing	this,	you	empower	yourself	and
cripple	 the	 command	 of	 your	 anxiety.	 It's	 like	 getting	 a	 vintage,	 pre-jail,	 and
drug-free	 Mike	 Tyson	 to	 fight	 for	 you—while	 tying	 up	 the	 hands	 of	 your
opponent!

By	 doing	 this,	 your	 fear,	 anxiety,	 and	 panic	 have	 no	 chance	 to	 take	 over.
Panic	 attacks	 will	 be	 eliminated,	 and	 you	 will	 feel	 much	 better	 about	 yourself.
Soon,	 anytime	 you	 start	 to	 feel	 anxious,	 you	 can	 simply	 implement	 this
technique,	until	none	of	your	anxiety	persists	and	you	can	start	living	your	life
carefree	again.

It	 was	 soon	 after	 this	 that	 I	 encountered	 another	 life-changing	 method	 for
eliminating	 even	 more	 fear	 from	 my	 life.	 It	 had	 to	 do	 with	 doing	 something	 I
absolutely	dreaded,	something	I	don't	completely	enjoy	even	to	this	day,	and	that
is,	riding	roller-coasters.

For	 my	 entire	 life,	 every	 time	 I	 ever	 went	 to	 a	 carnival	 or	 theme	 park,	 I
anxiously	 awaited	 the	 moment	 when	 my	 family	 or	 friends	 inevitably	 stumbled
across	the	roller-coaster	rides.	I	knew	it	was	inescapable	that	I'd	have	to	ride	one,
because	 everyone	 I	 went	 with	 loved	 them.	 Such	 anxiety	 and	 contempt	 coursed
through	 my	 veins	 every	 time	 I	 saw	 one,	 but	 I	 always	 had	 to	 go,	 or	 else	 just
chicken	out	and	look	like	a	complete	wuss—which	was	what	I	started	doing	as	I
got	older	and	older.

I	figured	it	was	better	to	look	like	a	complete	wuss	and	tell	people	that	I'd
get	sick,	rather	than	actually	getting	sick	and	being	a	complete	wuss	after	puking
all	over	myself.	So	I	reverted	to	chickening	out	most	of	the	time.	All	until	one
fateful	day	.	.	.

I	 was	 at	 the	 theme	 park,	 shortly	 after	 I'd	 gotten	 over	 my	 panic	 attacks	 and

generalized	 anxiety.	 I'd	 even	 made	 some	 new	 friends	 and	 begun	 to	 enjoy	 life
again.	 (This	 was	 right	 after	 I'd	 found	 the	 Dating	 Community,	 and	 begun
changing	my	life	for	the	better.)	Well,	one	of	the	friends	I	made	just	so	happened
to	be	a	complete	psychopathic	daredevil!	He	was	the	type	of	guy	who'd	do	back-
flips	into	a	pool	off	a	30	foot	house	roof,	or	ride	180	mph	on	a	street-bike	while
on	one	wheel,	or	jump	out	of	a	plane	while	laughing	his	ass	off!	Yeah,	this	guy
was	nuts.

Well,	anyway,	we	got	to	the	theme	park	one	day	and	sure	enough	he	wanted
to	go	on	all	the	crazy,	terrifying,	and	in	my	opinion,	deadly	roller-coaster	rides.
And	of	course	he	wanted	me	to	go	with	him!

I	protested	and	put	my	foot	down.	”There’s	absolutely	no	way	I’m	going	to

go!”

Well,	 fast	 forward	 about	 20	 minutes,	 and	 there	 I	 was	 sitting	 next	 to	 this
psycho,	 on	 the	 scariest	 ride	 in	 the	 place!	 (He	 also	 happened	 to	 be	 a	 master
persuader,	 and	 he	 was	 great	 at	 making	 things	 sound	 not	 as	 bad	 as	 they	 really
were!)	It	was	the	one	with	all	the	twists	and	turns	and	upside-down	parts,	and	oh
yeah,	that	1,000,000-foot	drop	from	where	you	could	probably	see	all	across	the
country	when	you	were	at	the	top!

So	I	was	sweating	bullets	and	looking	for	a	way	out,	literally	having	a	panic
attack	 and	 trying	 to	 remember	 what	 to	 do.	 All	 of	 a	 sudden	 I	 look	 over	 at	 this
nutcase	and	he's	acting	the	completely	opposite	of	me!	He’s	laughing	and	yelling
and	putting	 his	hands	up	and	shouting	at	the	girls	 next	to	him.	He's	totally	not
worried	at	all	and	loving	life!

“Dude,”	I	asked	him	“what	the	hell	is	wrong	with	you?	Why	are	you	yelling
and	 acting	 like	 a	 jackass?	 We	 are	 about	 to	 die?”	 And	 his	 answer	 completely
changed	my	outlook	from	that	point	forward.	He	said	“That’s	what	you	have	to
do!”	 And	 then	 he	 said	 “You	 have	 to	 get	 pumped	 up	 to	 enjoy	 these	 things.	 Get
into	it	and	yell	with	me;	it’s	way	more	fun	that	way!”

And	 as	 much	 as	 I	 didn’t	 want	 to,	 I	 listened	 to	 the	 crazy	 bastard.	 I	 started
yelling	 and	 shouting	 and	 putting	 my	 hands	 up.	 We	 both	 started	 yelling	 things
like	“We’re	fucked!”	and	“We’re	totally	dead!”	But	by	doing	this	and	embracing
this	fear,	we	put	ourselves	in	the	moment	and	allowed	ourselves	to	enjoy	it!

By	embracing	our	fears	and	accepting	the	fact	that	we	couldn't	change	them

at	that	given	moment,	we	were	able	to	get	ahold	of	ourselves.	We	weakened	the
impact	of	what	was	happening,	along	with	the	panic	that	normally	accompanied
me	while	riding	something	like	a	roller-coaster.

You	 see,	 fear	 is	 really	 just	 a	 mindset.	 If	 you	 go	 along	 with	 your	 fear	 as
opposed	 to	 trying	 to	 fight	 it,	 you'll	 realize	 it	 really	 doesn’t	 have	 an	 impact	 on
you.	It	only	has	an	impact	when	you	try	to	fight	it	or	hide	from	it.	The	minute
you	 recognize	 it	 and	 allow	 it	 to	 run	 its	 course,	 it	 does	 just	 that.	 It	 becomes
nothing	,	which	is	all	it	ever	was.

So	 what	 can	 we	 learn	 from	 these	 two	 stories?	 How	 can	 we	 apply	 this
knowledge	 about	 panic	 attacks	 and	 riding-roller-coasters	 into	 approaching
women?	Simple,	go	with	your	fear	and	disempower	it.

When	you	get	approach	anxiety	just	before	going	up	to	a	woman,	you	can	do
one	of	two	things.	You	can	try	to	fight	it,	letting	it	do	what	it	does	and	getting
into	 your	 head.	 It’ll	 give	 you	 all	 sorts	 of	 negative	 thoughts,	 make	 your	 voice
shake,	your	palms	sweat,	and	throw	your	game	off	in	a	number	of	ways.	Or	you
can	embrace	it,	accepting	the	fact	that	you'll	always	get	a	little	anxious	when	you
approach	 women	 (it’s	 completely	 natural	 to	 feel	 this	 emotion	 in	 life)	 and
acknowledging	that	there’s	no	way	to	completely	rid	yourself	of	this.	Then	you
can	use	this	little	nervous	feeling	to	your	advantage.

Take	the	anxiety	and	turn	it	into	excitement	and	energy!	Allow	this	to	be	the

fuel	for	a	great	approach!

The	best	way	to	get	over	your	fear	of	approaching	is	to	just	go	out	and	do	it.
You	really	can’t	do	anything	else	to	remove	the	fear	completely.	Getting	drunk
may	 help,	 but	 then	 again,	 you’re	 not	 going	 to	 be	 on	 your	 'A'	 game	 when	 you
drink,	 and	 women,	 as	 we	 learned	 earlier,	 don’t	 like	 drunk	 guys,	 anyway!	 This
really	isn’t	an	appealing	alternative.

It’s	best	to	approach	a	woman	the	second	you	feel	the	anxiety	creeping	up.
Do	not	wait	and	let	the	anxiety	build	up.	Don't	take	your	time	trying	to	think	of
something	witty	to	say.	Just	embrace	that	quick	emotional	fear	creeping	up,	and
take	action.	Use	this	fear	to	your	advantage	and	go	in	for	the	kill!

I	remember	watching	Wanderlei	Silva,	the	great	Mixed	Martial	Arts	fighter
from	the	UFC	and	Pride,	giving	an	interview	one	day	about	fear.	Now,	here’s	a
guy	 who's	 made	 a	 living	 by	 fighting	 other	 scary	 dudes	 his	 whole	 life.	 And	 he

hasn’t	 just	 squeaked	 by,	 but	 actually	 dominated	 in	 the	 sport.	 He's	 knocked	 out
most	of	his	competition	with	vicious	punches,	elbows,	and	knees	and	been	one
of	the	most	violent	and	ruthless	fighters	the	MMA	world	has	ever	seen.

In	 the	 interview,	 when	 asked	 about	 whether	 he	 gets	 nervous	 before	 his
fights,	he	surprisingly	said	he	gets	extremely	anxious	before	every	single	fight,
and	 that	 he	 always	 had.	 He’s	 always	 been	 scared	 shitless	 just	 before	 the	 fight
began,	 but	 rather	 than	 cowering	 from	 this	 fear	 and	 letting	 it	 control	 him,	 he's
used	it	to	his	advantage.

He	 said	 he	 enjoyed	 this	 fear	 because	 it	 helped	 him.	 He	 fought	 like	 a	 mad-
man	and	tried	to	go	for	the	kill	every	time	he	fought,	because	the	fear	propelled
him	into	doing	so.	Without	this	fear,	he	wouldn’t	have	had	the	killer	instinct	to
knock	guys	out	and	finish	them.

That	 is	 exactly	 the	 kind	 of	 mindset	 you	 need	 when	 approaching	 women.

(Not	the	knockout	part	of	course!)

You	 need	 that	 killer	 instinct,	 and	 you	 need	 to	 use	 the	 fear	 that	 arises	 just
before	 approaching	 her	 to	 your	 advantage.	 Be	 like	 Wanderlei	 Silva,	 and	 adopt
this	mentality	to	succeed.

You	can	harness	the	power	of	anxiety	and	actually	use	it	as	a	great	tool.	Just
remember,	the	next	time	you	see	a	beautiful	woman	near	you,	don’t	hesitate,	just
go	for	it!

"If	we	did	all	the	things	we	are	capable	of,
We	would	literally	astound	ourselves."

-	Thomas	A.	Edison

	Chapter	Nineteen

Why	Online	Dating	Will	Help	With	Approaching

In	 the	 world	 we	 live	 in	 today,	 everything	 seems	 to	 be	 done	 through	 the
internet:	 online	 banking,	 online	 shopping,	 online	 socializing,	 and	 of	 course,
online	dating.	Over	the	last	5-10	years,	online	dating	in	particular	has	taken	off
and	become	a	staple	in	today’s	singles’	society.

Just	 about	 every	 single	 person	 is	 dating	 online	 today,	 and	 that’s	 good.	 I,
unlike	 a	 lot	 of	 people	 who	 love	 to	 knock	 online	 dating,	 actually	 believe	 it’s	 a
very	good	thing.	In	fact,	it’s	quite	the	revolutionary	concept.

You	see,	online	dating	has	changed	the	very	fabric	of	how	we	meet	women.
Before,	it	was	just	face-to-face	and	we	were	left	talking	only	with	the	women	we
physically	 came	 across	 in	 the	 real	 world.	 Now,	 however,	 with	 the	 advent	 and
expansion	 of	 virtual	 dating,	 people	 can	 connect	 and	 set	 up	 dates	 with	 literally
anyone,	anywhere!

If,	for	instance,	you	live	in	a	small	town,	away	from	large	masses	of	women
and	 potential	 dates,	 no	 longer	 are	 you	 stuck	 with	 having	 to	 snuggle	 up	 next	 to
that	ugly,	morbidly	obese,	and	toothless	lady	down	at	the	local	dive.	Now,	you
can	take	your	exploits	virtual,	and	look	online	for	other	more	appealing	singles.
You	 don’t	 even	 have	 to	 stay	 looking	 in	 your	 town,	 which	 is	 probably	 a	 good
thing;	you	can	pursue	women	in	a	surrounding	town	or	nearby	city.	This	is	what
makes	online	dating	so	powerful:	the	ability	to	connect	to	people	anywhere!

Now	 for	 the	 kicker.	 How	 does	 online	 dating	 help	 your	 in-person	 game,	 or
better	 yet,	 how	 can	 it	 improve	 your	 approaching	 ?	 Simple.	 By	 messaging
women	 you	 are	 “approaching”	 them.	 You	 can	 build	 up	 your	 confidence	 in
“speaking”	to	them,	even	though	it's	only	through	words	on	an	internet	website.
The	point	is,	approaching	a	woman	and	messaging	a	woman	is	nearly	identical.

If	you’ve	ever	messaged	a	woman	online,	on	one	of	these	dating	sites,	you’ll
notice	that	you	get	a	little	nervous	every	time	you	start	to	write	the	message.	And
just	 before	 clicking	 “send”	 you’re	 probably	 most	 anxious.	 Also,	 waiting	 for	 a
reply	 for	 the	 next	 few	 minutes	 is	 also	 a	 little	 nerve-racking,	 especially	 if	 you

really	like	the	profile	of	the	woman.	Those	next	few	moments	you’ll	anxiously
be	awaiting	a	reply	and	hoping	for	a	positive	response.

How	 is	 it	 possible	 we	 can	 generate	 the	 same	 emotions	 from	 a	 computer
screen	and	the	words,	pictures,	and	messages	typed	on	it,	as	we	can	from	a	face-
to-face	 interaction?	 If	 you	 think	 about	 it,	 it’s	 rather	 crazy!	 People	 living	 100
years	 ago	 would	 think	 we	 were	 insane	 if	 we	 tried	 to	 explain	 the	 concept	 of
online	dating	(or	even	just	the	internet)	to	them.	They'd	probably	think	we	were
morons	for	investing	so	much	time	into	a	computer	and	affirm	that	the	only	real
way	 to	 meet	 someone	 was	 by	 talking	 to	 them	 in	 person.	 But	 they	 would	 be
wrong.

Although	 I	 have	 to	 admit	 I	 don’t	 love	 online	 dating,	 I	 do	 really	 like	 the
concept	 of	 it,	 and	 I	 know	 what	 a	 great	 tool	 it	 can	 be.	 It’s	 helped	 many	 guys,
including	myself,	with	communicating	and	actually	meeting	more	women.	It’s	a
great	way	to	get	over	your	fear	of	approaching	a	woman,	and	it’s	a	great	way	to
talk	 to	 a	 great	 number	 of	 women	 at	 once.	 If	 you	 can	 add	 a	 larger	 quantity	 of
women	 into	 your	 communication	 stream,	 the	 chances	 of	 getting	 more	 dates
obviously	 also	 becomes	 that	 much	 greater.	 It’s	 all	 a	 numbers	 game.	 It’s	 like
approaching	50	women	in	one	day	as	opposed	to	five:	you	might	get	rejected	by
40	of	them,	but	if	you	land	numbers	from	the	rest,	that’s	still	10	solid	numbers!
If	 you	 did	 the	 former,	 approached	 five	 women	 and	 got	 the	 same	 percentage	 of
numbers,	you'd	have	just	one!	So	the	more	the	merrier!

Online	 dating	 is	 recommended	 as	 a	 supplement	 to	 your	 in-person	 game.	 If
you	take	sports	supplements,	for	whatever	reason—to	gain	more	muscle,	to	get
ripped,	 to	 lose	 weight,	 to	 have	 more	 energy,	 etc.—you	 know	 that	 supplements
work	 as	 an	 addition	 to	 everything	 else	 you	 do.	 On	 top	 of	 eating	 as	 healthy	 as
possible,	working	out	at	the	gym,	and	sleeping	great	every	night,	a	supplement
can	put	you	into	the	peak	state	of	reaching	your	goals.	But	if	you	take	away	any
of	 these	 three	 main	 things,	 and	 think	 that	 a	 supplement	 will	 make	 up	 for	 what
you’re	lacking,	you're	mistaken.	A	supplement	only	works	a	little,	at	the	micro
level,	 whereas	 these	 other	 actions	 have	 macro	 effects,	 and	 are	 much	 more
important.

Think	 of	 online	 dating	 as	 the	 micro	 level,	 and	 your	 in-person	 game	 as	 the
macro.	It	helps	a	lot	with	meeting	women,	but	everything	else	should	come	first.
Use	it	as	a	supplement	and	not	as	your	main	asset.	You	should	work	on	yourself
and	become	better	with	speaking	to	women	in	person,	and	build	up	your	ability

to	attract	them	in	person	much	more	than	sending	messages	online.	If	you	don’t
have	the	ability	to	attract	a	woman	in	person	then	all	the	dates	you	accumulate
online	 are	 going	 to	 mean	 nothing	 once	 you	 actually	 do	 meet	 face-to-face
(presumably	the	real	intention	in	all	of	this).

Sticking	 with	 this	 macro	 theme	 of	 importance,	 the	 three	 macro	 parts	 to
meeting	 more	 women	 (in	 no	 particular	 order)	 should	 be:	 working	 on	 your
personality	 (everything	 that	 makes	 you	 more	 attractive	 to	 the	 opposite	 sex);
getting	yourself	healthy,	or	maintaining	your	existing	great	health	(working	out,
eating	right,	sleeping	good,	having	good	hygiene,	etc.);	and	actually	approaching
women	 (giving	 yourself	 the	 fastest	 track	 to	 being	 able	 to	 communicate	 with
them).	 Worry	 about	 these	 three	 elements	 above	 all	 else;	 then	 worry	 about	 the
supplement	 that	 is	 online	 dating.	 Get	 these	 macro-parts	 down,	 and	 the	 online
dating	will	just	add	to	the	success	of	what	you're	doing!

Some	guys	get	lost	in	the	online	dating	world	and	seem	to	fall	into	and	get
stuck	 inside	 another	 dimension.	 They	 end	 up	 being	 keyboard	 jockeys,	 caring
only	 about	 potential	 virtual	 dates	 and	 profiles.	 They	 think	 that	 using	 the
supplement	 is	 more	 important	 than	 the	 three	 core	 factors,	 so	 they	 stop
developing	 themselves	 and	 stop	 making	 real-world	 progress.	 Please	 heed	 the
advice	above,	and	do	not	become	one	of	these	guys.	It	will	only	harm	you	in	the
long	run.

I	recommend	most	free	websites	to	try	out	your	online	dating	skills.	Plenty
of	Fish	and	OkCupid	are	two	of	the	more	popular	free	ones.	They	both	are	pretty
decent	 for	 communicating	 with	 women,	 and	 the	 fact	 that	 they	 are	 free	 is	 great
because	 you	 can	 work	 on	 finding	 out	 what	 works	 and	 what	 doesn’t,	 without
having	to	pay	anything.	It's	tougher	to	get	dates	from	the	free	sites,	however,	as	a
lot	of	people	just	go	on	these	sites	to	search	around	and	see	what’s	out	there,	not
necessarily	expecting	to	find	someone.

I	 should	 also	 say	 that	 they	 aren’t	 as	 serious	 (because	 it’s	 free)	 as	 say	 the
people	on	Match.com	or	other	websites,	where	you	have	to	pay	to	be	on	there.
The	 payment	 is	 a	 great	 incentive	 for	 people	 to	 be	 much	 more	 serious	 about
connecting	 with	 others	 and	 going	 out	 on	 dates.	 If	 you	 have	 the	 money,	 I'd
recommend	something	like	Match.

On	a	final	note,	when	you	make	your	online	profile,	present	it	as	you	would
present	yourself	to	a	woman	in	person.	Would	you	be	dull,	boring,	and	all	alone

when	you	go	out?	Well,	you	could,	but	that	wouldn’t	be	very	attractive!	Instead,
what	 works	 in-person	 tends	 to	 work	 online	 as	 well.	 Make	 your	 profile	 fun,
outgoing,	humorous,	and	exciting.	Definitely	use	social	proof	and	pre-selection
in	your	pictures,	with	pictures	of	you	having	a	good	time	with	your	buddies	(and
your	 female	 friends).	 Also,	 be	 doing	 fun	 things:	 playing	 a	 sport,	 going	 to	 an
event,	 going	 to	 a	 party.	 Don’t	 have	 a	 bunch	 of	 selfies	 of	 yourself	 taken	 on	 the
same	 day,	 with	 just	 different	 shirts	 on.	 (I’ve	 done	 this	 myself,	 long,	 long	 ago!
Yeah,	needless	to	say,	it	didn’t	work!)

Just	remember,	online	dating	is	an	extension	to	your	real,	face-to-face	game.
When	you’re	online,	act	as	you	would	in	person.	If	you’re	developing	yourself
and	building	your	great	game,	you	should	have	no	trouble	finding	success	online
and	in	turn	having	more	in-person	success.	Online	dating	really	is	a	great	tool	for
enhancing	your	game,	so	take	advantage	of	it!

"Everyone	has	inside	of	him	a	piece	of	good	news.
The	good	news	is	that	you	don't	know	how	great	you	can	be!
How	much	you	can	love!	What	you	can	accomplish!
And	what	your	potential	is!"

-	Anne	Frank

	Chapter	Twenty

Why	You	Will	Suck	.	.	.	At	First!

You	 will	 suck	 for	 a	 while.	 That’s	 just	 how	 it	 is.	 You'll	 fall	 on	 your	 face.
You'll	look	like	an	idiot.	You'll	feel	like	a	creep.	You'll	get	blown	out.	You'll	get
yelled	at.	You'll	get	threatened.	You'll	feel	like	shit.	You'll	want	to	give	up!

But	you	can’t.

You	 can’t	 give	 up,	 and	 you	 can’t	 quit.	 This	 is	 your	 life	 and	 you	 have	 to
figure	it	out.	You	want	to	find	a	woman,	or	several	women,	someone	to	connect
with	and	spend	the	best	parts	of	your	life	beside.	Nobody	wants	to	be	alone,	and
if	 it	 takes	 going	 through	 everything	 above	 to	 beat	 this	 feeling	 of	 being	 alone,
then	so	be	it!	That’s	a	sacrifice	worth	making.

All	of	the	negative	things	that	can	happen	when	approaching	women	usually
only	 happen	 at	 first.	 They	 are,	 in	 a	 sense,	 just	 temporary.	 They	 eventually
dissipate	 with	 time	 as	 you	 get	 better	 and	 better.	 If	 you	 think	 you'll	 be	 getting
yelled	at,	threatened,	or	blown	out	all	the	time,	you	are	dead	wrong.	These	things
really	 only	 occur	 when	 you	 don’t	 know	 how	 to	 handle	 certain	 situations	 with
certain	women.

Eventually,	 with	 experience,	 you	 learn	 how	 to	 handle	 their	 reactions	 and
figure	out	how	to	fix	things,	or	at	least	de-escalate	them	before	they	get	worse.
Many	 times,	 it’s	 as	 simple	 as	 smiling	 or	 saying	 “I'm	 sorry,”	 and	 you	 can
completely	 change	 the	 tone	 of	 an	 interaction.	 But	 guys	 just	 learning	 how	 to
approach	 women	 don’t	 understand	 this	 concept,	 and	 often	 can’t	 handle	 the
pressure.	They	get	lost	in	the	fray.

Expecting	to	be	great	at	something	when	you	first	start	off	is	foolish.	Sure,
people	 are	 more	 inclined	 to	 certain	 subjects	 than	 others,	 but	 that	 doesn’t	 mean
they'll	automatically	excel.	It	often	takes	much	time	and	practice,	even	for	those
naturals.

Do	 you	 think	 Michael	 Jordan	 could	 dunk	 the	 first	 time	 he	 picked	 up	 a
basketball?	 Do	 you	 think	 Albert	 Einstein	 could	 solve	 complex	 mathematical
algorithms	 when	 he	 was	 still	 learning	 how	 to	 count?	 Do	 you	 think	 George

Harrison	could	instantly	play	exceptionally	awesome-sounding	guitar	riffs	when
he	first	touched	an	instrument?	Of	course	not.	All	of	these	legends	invested	years
upon	years	to	develop	their	craft.	They	practiced	and	practiced,	until	they	slowly
got	better	at	their	skill.

Fortunately,	 approaching	 women	 is	 a	 skill	 that	 can	 be	 learned	 too,	 and
improved	 upon	 in	 time.	 (It’s	 also	 much	 easier	 than	 doing	 anything	 those	 guys
did!)	It	takes	a	lot	of	hard	work	and	dedication,	but	the	more	you	do	it	the	better
you’ll	become.	Think	back	to	the	10,000-hour	rule.	The	closer	you	get	to	hitting
this	number	the	more	of	an	expert	you’ll	be.	The	three	legends	above	went	far
and	away	past	the	10,000-hour	mark,	but	if	you	recall,	you	don’t	have	to	come
anywhere	near	this	number.	Just	striving	toward	it	gets	you	better	and	better.

I	want	you	to	think	back	for	a	second	to	the	time	when	you	first	learned	how
to	drive	a	car.	I	know	every	guy	wants	to	get	behind	the	wheel	of	a	car	when	he's
16,	and	cruise	around	and	pick	up	friends	and	show	off	his	great	driving	skills.
We	 want	 to	 act	 cool	 and	 pretend	 we’re	 Jeff	 Gordon	 for	 a	 while.	 We	 think	 it
looks	easy,	and	that	we’ll	pick	it	up	right	away	and	be	a	cool	high-schooler	with
wheels.	But	it	doesn’t	play	out	like	this.

The	 reality	 of	 the	 situation	 is	 that	 when	 we	 first	 learn	 how	 to	 drive	 we
completely	suck	at	it!	We	practice	in	our	parents’	car	on	secluded	neighborhood
streets,	 and	 we	 do	 absolutely	 horrible.	 We	 jerk	 the	 pedal,	 go	 too	 fast,	 then	 too
slow,	 jam	 on	 the	 brake,	 hold	 the	 steering	 wheel	 awkwardly,	 take	 wide	 turns
around	 corners,	 and	 then	 freak	 out	 and	 get	 yelled	 at	 for	 doing	 dumb,	 obvious
things	like	blowing	stop	signs!	(This	is	just	for	an	automatic	car	too;	don’t	get
me	started	on	a	standard!)	Yes,	it's	a	parent’s	worst	nightmare,	the	day	their	kid
turns	16!

If	you	recall	back	to	when	you	were	learning	how	to	drive,	I’m	sure	all	of
these	things	(at	the	very	least	most	of	them)	happened	to	you.	It’s	easy	to	watch
someone	 drive	 for	 so	 many	 years	 and	 think	 we	 can	 do	 it	 too.	 But	 when	 we
actually	 get	 behind	 the	 wheel,	 and	 try	 to	 do	 everything	 we	 have	 to	 in	 order	 to
successfully	operate	the	vehicle,	it’s	much	harder	than	it	looks.

It	takes	a	month,	two	months,	maybe	three	months	of	practicing	before	most
people	 get	 respectable	 at	 driving.	 For	 some	 it’s	 even	 a	 little	 longer,	 maybe	 six
months	or	even	up	to	a	year	(For	some,	it's	never!).	On	average	though,	two	or
three	months	should	be	expected.

Well,	the	same	thing	goes	for	approaching.

I'd	use	the	exact	same	time-frame	for	approaching	women	and	driving	a	car.
When	you	start	off,	expect	to	suck	for	at	least	a	month,	probably	two	or	three,
and	maybe	even	up	to	a	full	year	before	you	get	decent	at	it!	As	much	as	it	sucks
not	being	good	at	something	like	that,	the	end	result	is	well	worth	it,	just	as	with
driving	a	car.	If	you'd	quit	the	day	your	father	yelled	at	you	and	called	you	an
asshole	for	almost	getting	the	both	of	you	killed,	you	never	would	have	learned
how	to	drive,	and	you	never	would’ve	had	that	great	skill	in	life.

Just	remember,	when	the	going	gets	tough	(as	it	certainly	will	when	you’re
learning	 how	 to	 approach	 women),	 the	 tough	 get	 going!	 Don’t	 quit,	 and	 don’t
give	up.	Expect	to	be	terrible	at	first,	then	appreciate	the	fact	that	you’re	sticking
through	it	and	getting	better	by	doing	so.	The	day	will	come	soon	enough,	when
you	realize	you’ve	gotten	good	at	this	skill,	just	like	all	the	other	things	you’ve
learned	to	master	in	life!

"Intelligence	is	the	ability	to	adapt	to	change."

-	Stephen	Hawking

	Chapter	Twenty-One

Working	With	A	Wingman

One	of	the	easiest	ways	to	improve	your	success	while	approaching	women
is	to	go	with	a	friend.	A	friend	who	wants	to	approach	women	with	you	serves
two	purposes.	Not	only	will	this	“wingman”	push	you	into	opening	more	women
than	 you	 would	 by	 yourself,	 but	 he	 also	 makes	 you	 look	 and	 feel	 better	 while
doing	it!

Let	me	explain	.	.	.

Have	you	ever	gone	out	alone	to	approach	women	on	the	street	or	at	a	bar?	If
you’re	 reading	 this	 book,	 the	 chances	 are	 probably	 50/50	 that	 you	 have.	 You,
like	 me,	 have	 maybe	 gone	 out	 on	 occasion,	 at	 least	 once	 before,	 and	 tried
meeting	women	by	yourself.	(I’m	not	talking	about	going	out	alone	and	meeting
up	with	someone	or	friends	here.	I	mean	actually	going	out	alone	and	continually
approaching	women,	at	night	or	during	the	day.)	If	so,	congratulations,	you	have
a	lot	of	balls!

Whether	 or	 not	 you	 were	 successful	 in	 your	 attempts	 doesn’t	 really	 matter
(more	 likely	 you	 weren’t,	 as	 it’s	 very	 tough	 to	 be).	 The	 fact	 that	 you	 were
willing	 to	 do	 this	 is	 very	 impressive.	 It	 shows	 that	 you're	 very	 committed	 to
learning	how	to	improve	your	dating	life,	and	you're	probably	going	to	succeed
at	this	faster	than	most	guys.

If	you	have	gone	out,	what	you	probably	learned	right	away	was	that	it’s	not
easy,	 not	 easy	 at	 all!	 It’s	 actually	 extremely	 difficult	 to	 approach	 women	 when
you’re	by	yourself.	It’s	tough	for	a	number	of	reasons,	but	the	main	one	is	this:
you	aren’t	in	the	right	mindset.

You	see,	when	you’re	with	someone,	you’re	naturally	going	to	be	talking	to
them	and	having	a	good	time.	You’ll	be	walking	around	already	warmed	up,	just
because	of	this	banter	with	your	friend.	You’ll	be	having	fun,	as	friends	do	when
they’re	with	each	other,	and	in	turn	you'll	be	giving	off	all	sorts	of	great	vibes,
and	women	will	pick	up	on	this	wonderful	energy	fast!

On	 the	 contrary,	 when	 you’re	 by	 yourself,	 you’re	 naturally	 quiet	 and

introverted,	 listening	 to	 the	 voice	 inside	 your	 head,	 having	 no	 dialogue	 with
anyone	else.	This	often	causes	you	to	emit	a	poor	energy	and	send	off	bad	vibes.
Needless	to	say,	this	is	not	the	ideal	mindset	for	meeting	a	new	woman.

You	may	also	feel	a	bit	weird	or	off,	walking	around	by	yourself	and	going
up	to	woman	after	woman.	Personally,	to	this	day,	I'd	even	feel	a	bit	weird	doing
this,	and	I’m	a	dating	coach!	It’s	just	not	natural	to	approach	women	time	after
time	 when	 you’re	 by	 yourself.	 It	 can	 be	 done,	 and	 do	 not	 take	 this	 as
discouragement	 from	 doing	 so,	 all	 I	 mean	 is	 that	 it’s	 so	 much	 easier	 if	 you're
with	someone,	anyone	!

Being	 an	 introvert,	 I	 constantly	 think	 over	 things	 internally,	 and	 this	 keeps
me	from	being	as	outgoing	as	I'd	like	to	be	at	times.	This	constant	chatter	in	my
head	also	gets	me	thinking	negative	thoughts	about	what	I'm	doing.	For	instance,
if	 an	 approach	 hasn’t	 gone	 the	 way	 I	 intended	 it	 to,	 I	 might	 be	 stuck	 thinking
about	 that	 for	 the	 next	 few	 minutes,	 and	 it	 would	 probably	 interfere	 with	 my
upcoming	approaches.	But	if	I	have	someone	with	me,	a	friend,	or	wingman,	my
thoughts	 wouldn’t	 be	 able	 to	 run	 amok.	 In	 fact,	 when	 I’m	 with	 a	 wingman,	 I
have	little	if	any	thoughts	at	all,	because	I’m	usually	in	conversation	with	him.	I
don’t	have	time	to	think	and	analyze	every	little	thing	introverts	like	to	think	and
analyze.	 Instead,	 I’m	 more	 focused	 on	 being	 in	 the	 present	 moment,	 and	 my
success	is	more	evident	this	way.

It’s	almost	like	having	a	safety	net	when	you’re	with	someone	else.	It’s	not
at	all	like	approaching	women	is	dangerous	or	anything,	but	as	humans,	we	feel
more	safe	and	comfortable	surrounded	by	friends	or	in	groups	of	people.	Going
by	yourself	just	naturally	creates	a	little	more	anxiety	than	going	with	a	friend.
It’s	almost	like	you’re	going	into	battle	with	someone	else,	who	can	watch	your
back	 and	 help	 you	 out	 if	 you	 need	 it.	 It’s	 more	 of	 a	 psychological	 boost	 than
anything	else,	but	it's	effective	nonetheless.

No	one	pushes	you	into	opening	more	women	like	a	good	wingman	will.	If
you’re	 by	 yourself	 and	 you	 see	 a	 beautiful	 woman	 nearby	 and	 all	 of	 a	 sudden
you	get	a	rush	of	crazy,	high-voltage	approach	anxiety,	who’s	going	to	force	you
into	walking	over	and	talking	to	her?	Who’s	going	to	say	“Stop	being	a	pussy,
and	get	your	ass	over	there!”?	Nobody.

If	 you’re	 with	 a	 friend,	 though,	 and	 you’re	 both	 approaching	 women,	 your
friend	will	hold	you	accountable	and	make	you	go	over	there.	This	is	one	of	the

most	important	factors.	You	can	keep	each	other	in	check	and	make	sure	you’re
both	going	up	to	women.	No	one	gets	a	chance	to	chicken	out	or	come	up	with
excuses.	Without	a	friend,	 nobody	 would	ever	know	that	that	beautiful	 woman
you	just	passed	up	was	even	alive.	But	with	that	wingman	by	your	side,	you	bet
he	saw	her,	and	you	bet	you’re	going	in	and	talking	to	her	.	.	.	or	he	is!

The	final	thing	that	a	wingman	does	is	give	you	social	proof,	which,	as	we
know,	is	a	huge	asset	in	the	dating	world.	It	gives	credence	where	questions	may
abound.	Social	proof,	the	appearance	of	something	seeming	to	be	more	valued,
incredible	 psychological
in

phenomenon.	 Amazon	 customer	 reviews,	 Wal-Mart	 commercials,	 and	 Nike
advertisements	all	use	social	proof.	They	get	people	to	vouch	for	their	products,
which	in	turn	makes	their	products	seem	more	precious.	Whether	they	like	it	or
not,	people	give	massive	credit	to	the	opinions	of	others.

By	walking	around	with	a	friend,	that	friend	is	granting	you	social	proof.	He
is	saying,	through	body-language	and	mannerisms,	that	you	are	a	good	guy,	and
that	 he	 enjoys	 your	 company.	 When	 people,	 or	 more	 particularly	 women,	 see
this,	 they	 naturally	 think	 more	 highly	 of	 you	 because	 they	 take	 your	 friend’s
review	of	you	and	it	shifts	their	opinion	right	away.

For	example,	picture	yourself	walking	on	a	street	by	yourself	right	now	in	an
ordinary	fashion.	You're	not	abnormally	negative	or	positive,	just	your	average,
usual	self.	You	have	a	normal	look	on,	with	a	normal	facial	expression,	and	you
stop	a	woman	walking	by	whom	you	find	attractive.	Now,	picture	yourself	with
a	friend,	on	the	same	street.	You're	chatting	it	up,	laughing,	and	having	a	great
time,	and	then	you	stop	the	same	woman	you	find	attractive.	Which	guy	do	you
think	has	the	better	chance	at	success?	Yup,	you	guessed	it,	guy	number	two!

The	guy	who's	laughing	and	having	a	great	time,	being	given	a	ton	of	social
proof	 from	 his	 friend,	 is	 the	 guy	 who'll	 have	 a	 much	 greater	 chance	 at	 getting
that	 woman’s	 number.	 She	 instantly	 picks	 up	 on	 all	 the	 favorable	 social	 cues
between	 the	 two	 of	 you	 guys,	 which	 will	 greatly	 help	 your	 chances	 when	 you
talk	to	her.

So	next	time	you	go	out,	go	out	with	a	friend.	Get	yourself	a	good	wingman
today	and	start	getting	more	girls!	(If	you	can’t	find	a	good	wingman	to	go	out
with,	however,	keep	going	out	on	your	own.	It	will	be	a	little	harder,	but	don't
worry,	you'll	still	be	meeting	more	women	than	if	you	stayed	home!)

"Your	time	is	limited,
So	don't	waste	it	living	someone	else's	life.

	Chapter	Twenty-Two

Picking	The	Right	Approach

Deciding	which	way	to	approach	women	can	be	tricky.	There	are	so	many
different	styles	out	there,	and	so	many	different	coaches	to	learn	from.	You	have
the	loud,	outgoing,	direct	guys	like	Adam	LoDolce,	who	insist	that	being	direct
is	the	best	way	to	go.	Then	you	have	guys	like	David	Wygant,	who	use	indirect,
observational	openers	that	work	great	for	him.	And	then	you	have	guys	like	Paul
Janka,	who	say	making	the	approach	short	and	sweet	is	best,	comparing	his	1-2
minute	openers	to	movie	previews.	All	of	these	approaches	are	effective.	And	all
of	these	coaches	are	great.	But	which	approach	will	work	for	you?

Not	 everyone	 is	 going	 to	 be	 loud.	 Not	 everyone	 is	 going	 to	 want	 to	 be
indirect.	Not	everyone	is	going	to	want	to	fly	through	their	approaches,	and	get	a
woman’s	phone	number	in	1-2	minutes.	The	key	is	to	try	them	all	and	find	what
fits	you	best.	Maybe	you’re	more	of	a	LoDolce	type,	loud	and	outgoing.	Maybe
you’re	 more	 indirect,	 like	 Wygant.	 Or	 perhaps	 you	 feel	 the	 best	 way	 to	 get	 a
woman’s	 number	 is	 to	 rush	 the	 interaction	 and	 get	 in	 and	 out	 like	 Janka	 does.
Like	I	said,	all	of	these	methods	work	great,	you	just	need	to	figure	out	which
one	is	best	for	you	and	try	to	perfect	it.

Maybe	you’ll	develop	your	own	little	style	based	off	one	of	these	methods,
and	then	perfect	that.	The	only	way	you’ll	learn	is	by	trying.	It’s	good	to	try	all
sorts	of	methods	from	all	sorts	of	coaches.	There	are	quite	literally	thousands	of
coaches	out	there;	the	guys	listed	above	are	just	a	few	of	the	more	popular	ones.
So	don’t	be	shy.	Give	it	a	try.

It	took	me	a	while	to	figure	out	my	own	style,	but	as	I	mentioned	earlier,	I
like	to	bounce	around	and	switch	things	up	from	time	to	time,	depending	on	my
mood.	 I	 don’t	 pigeon-hole	 myself	 into	 only	 doing	 one	 thing,	 but	 would	 rather
switch	things	up	based	on	how	and	what	I’m	feeling	that	day.	I	am	an	introvert
by	 nature	 but	 throughout	 the	 day	 I	 definitely	 have	 moments	 of	 extroversion.
There	 are	 certainly	 times	 when	 I	 love	 being	 the	 center	 of	 attention	 and	 being
loud,	and	this	undoubtedly	reflects	on	my	approach	game.

Most	guys	can,	however,	rule	out	a	ton	of	methods	right	off	the	bat.	If,	for

example,	 you're	 a	 guy	 who's	 very	 shy	 and	 very	 introverted,	 and	 doesn't	 like
being	the	center	of	attention	(as	I	do	at	times),	it’s	fair	to	say	that	an	incredibly
direct	approach	would	not	be	best	for	you.	Going	indirect	and	being	more	subtle
would	be	far	better.	On	the	other	hand,	if	you're	a	guy	who's	ready	to	learn	game,
and	 are	 naturally	 extroverted	 and	 great	 at	 speaking,	 learning	 how	 to	 be	 more
direct	and	candidly	communicate	your	feelings	to	women	would	be	better.	You
could	 easily	 adapt	 a	 direct	 approach	 to	 meeting	 women	 and	 would	 be	 much
better	off	for	it.

I	 do	 recommend	 those	 guys	 mentioned	 above,	 as	 they	 are	 all	 great	 dating
coaches	and	have	a	long	track-record	of	success.	They’ve	been	around	for	a	very
long	time,	and	have	helped	many	guys	out	in	this	area.	You	have	to	be	careful
when	 new	 coaches	 pop	 up	 and	 spout	 out	 about	 their	 method	 being	 superior	 to
everyone	 else’s.	 I’m	 always	 a	 bit	 wary	 when	 the	 next	 guy	 pops	 up	 and	 starts
making	all	sorts	of	crazy	claims	about	being	the	best	new	coach	around.	You’re
better	 off	 going	 with	 guys	 who've	 been	 around	 for	 years	 and	 years	 and	 have
shown	repeated	success	coaching	their	students.

The	 Dating	 Community	 has	 its	 fair	 share	 of	 smart,	 intelligent,	 proven
coaches.	With	just	a	little	research,	it’s	easy	to	find	them	and	start	learning	from
them.	The	Community	does	have	its	fair	share	of	idiots	though,	like	some	of	the
hyped-up	new	guys	who	claim	to	be	the	best	at	teaching	game.	Again,	do	your
own	due	diligence	and	you	can	find	out	soon	enough	who's	legitimate	and	who's
not.	The	guys	who	are	legitimate	are	the	ones	to	learn	from.	The	others?	Well,
you	can	forget	about	them	because	they	won’t	be	around	for	long.

Be	sure	to	try	out	a	lot	of	the	established	and	interesting	things	from	some	of
the	 top	 experts	 out	 there.	 Everyone	 has	 his	 own	 style;	 what	 may	 work	 for	 you
might	 not	 work	 for	 the	 next	 guy,	 and	 vice-versa.	 Just	 remember	 to	 stay	 away
from	 all	 the	 fluff	 and	 stuff	 that	 seems	 ridiculous.	 I	 have	 a	 saying	 in	 the
Community,	“If	it	looks	ridiculous,	sounds	ridiculous,	and	seems	ridiculous,	then
it’s	complete	bullshit!”	Stay	away	from	all	the	wacky,	weird	shit	out	there;	trust

you,	a	method	that	feels	like	it’s	going	to	work.	Choose	something	that	fits	who
you	are	inside,	as	well	as	your	core	beliefs.	This	can	be	anything,	but	it	must	be

you	 !	 If	 you	 do	 this	 and	 are	 honest	 with	 who	 you	 are,	 you'll	 see	 the	 utmost
success	in	the	quickest	amount	of	time.	There	are	no	boundaries	and	no	limits	to

	Chapter	Twenty-Three

short	nappy	hair,	beady	black	eyes,	and	an	evil	stare.	They	will	look	terrifying
enough,	but	be	even	more	dangerous	in	reality.	They’ll	walk	with	a	limp,	but	be
able	to	reach	speeds	up	to	and	faster	than	most	normal	human-beings	because	of

Just	kidding.	This	is	not	happening,	and	it	never	will.	Zombies	are	a	figment
of	 our	 wildest	 imaginations,	 like	 vampires	 and	 giants.	 They	 do	 not	 exist	 and
there	is	no	way	they	ever	will,	which	is	funny	because	so	many	people	actually

zombies.	 They	 just	 need	 a	 little	 push	 and	 a	 little	 guidance,	 and	 they	 can	 see

When	you	have	great	game,	it	doesn’t	mean	you	sleep	with	a	million	girls;	it

much	more.	It	cheapens	it	to	say	that	game	is	all	about	having	sex	with	women.

enjoyment	 out	 of	 it	 anymore;	 they	 just	 do	 it	 to	 say	 they	 do	 it,	 and	 to	 prove	 to

Please	 listen	 to	 me	 here:	 you	 don’t	 want	 to	 become	 one	 of	 these	 zombies.
It’s	 worse	 than	 death	 in	 my	 opinion.	 It’s	 taking	 the	 fun	 and	 excitement	 and
energy	 out	 of	 living	 and	 replacing	 it	 with	 boring,	 lifeless,	 and	 unanimated

Learn	to	take	breaks	from	approaching	when	you’re	getting	sick	of	it.	Your

their	 social	 lives	 and	 enjoying	 themselves,	 not	 as	 a	 way	 of	 validating	 their

your	 job	 to	 open	 every	 single	 girl	 you	 see.	 Leave	 that	 up	 to	 the	 lifeless	 souls

	Chapter	Twenty-Four

Handling	More	Than	One	At	A	Time

A	lot	of	the	time,	when	you	go	out	to	meet	women,	there	will	be	more	than
one	 you	 have	 to	 talk	 to.	 Ideally,	 you	 could	 go	 up	 to	 women	 alone,	 and	 they
would	be	alone,	and	you	could	easily	talk	to	them	and	spit	your	magical	game.
You	 could	 even	 get	 their	 numbers	 and	 fall	 in	 love	 and	 have	 three	 beautiful
children	and	live	happily	ever	after	.	.	.

But,	that’s	usually	not	how	it	works	out!

Unfortunately,	a	beautiful	woman	you	want	to	approach	is	typically	with	a
friend	 of	 hers.	 And	 so,	 you	 have	 to	 decide	 how	 to	 approach	 her	 while	 dealing
with	this	friend.

With	One	Friend

If	 a	 woman	 is	 with	 one	 friend,	 it	 can	 be	 very	 difficult	 to	 approach	 and	 be
successful	in	this	situation,	just	due	to	the	simple	fact	that	when	you	talk	to	her,
the	friend	will	be	all	alone	and	probably	feel	left	out.	You	must	keep	this	in	mind
when	 you	 go	 in.	 If	 you	 can	 keep	 the	 friend	 busy	 while	 you	 work	 your	 charm,
you’ll	be	much	better	off.

If	 you	 have	 a	 wingman,	 of	 course,	 he	 can	 keep	 the	 friend	 busy.	 However,
we're	assuming	you're	alone	here	and	you've	approached	two	women;	you	want
to	do	your	best	to	be	friendly	to	her	friend,	whilst	still	making	it	clear	you	are
interested	 in	 your	 target.	 You	 could	 even	 say	 that:	 “You	 ladies	 are	 both	 very
pretty,	 but	 you	 (speaking	 to	 the	 one	 you	 like)	 are	 absolutely	 beautiful.	 You’re
like	my	dream	girl!”	Being	nice	and	giving	a	compliment	to	the	friend	is	pretty
important.	That	way,	it	doesn’t	look	like	you're	just	hitting	on	her	friend,	even
though	you	are!

If	you	can	separate	her	from	the	friend,	that’s	ideal.	It	might	take	some	time,
but	at	some	point,	you	should	suggest	that	you,	and	the	woman	you	like,	go	to
some	other	location	nearby.	Tell	the	friend	you'll	be	right	back	and	not	to	worry.
This	of	course	should	come	after	at	least	a	few	minutes	of	chatting	with	both	of
them,	being	as	nice	as	possible	to	the	friend,	so	she	can	feel	okay	with	you	now

being	alone	with	her	friend.	It	might	be	tricky,	but	if	you're	nice	enough	to	her,
and	have	a	strong	enough	belief	that	what	you're	saying	is	true,	both	women	will
pick	up	on	it	and	trust	you.

Once	you	separate	her	from	the	friend,	you'll	be	golden.	You	can	then	talk	to
her	 openly	 and	 proceed	 with	 your	 normal	 game,	 not	 worrying	 so	 much	 about
being	interrupted.

With	Two	Friends

Similar	to	the	last	section,	when	opening	a	large	group	of	women	you	want

to	open	more	than	just	the	one	woman	you’re	most	interested	in.	This	might	not

called	 the	 “Foot	 in	 the	Door	 Effect,”	 where	 by	 doing	 one	 small	 thing,	 you	can
eventually	do	much,	much	more.

great	night	for	many	a	great	men.	A	cock-block	thrives	in	this	role.	She,	or	even

of	 action	 is	 to	 ignore	 it,	 and	 hope	 it	 slowly	 fades	 away	 when	 it	 sees	 you	 not
reacting	 and	 caring	 very	 little	 about	 its	 attempts	 to	 thwart	 your	 every	 move.
Usually	 this	 is	 enough,	 but	 if	 you	 have	 a	 stubborn	 (maybe	 even	 drunk)	 cock-
block,	there	may	come	a	point	where	you	have	to	put	it	in	its	place.	And	this	is

Just	be	bold	and	honest	here.	You	don’t	need	to	be	a	complete	ass	and	start
cursing	and	yelling,	but	if	the	time	comes	where	you	have	to	put	the	cock-block

behaving,	 and	 how	 inappropriate	 she’s	 been	 the	 whole	 time	 in	 talking	 to	 you.
Tell	her	to	leave	you	alone	and	stop	acting	like	a	child.

be	okay.	The	cock-block	will	retreat	and	know	she's	not	dealing	with	someone
who	 can	 easily	 be	 shaken.	 (You	 must	 be	 willing	 to	 stand	 by	 what	 you	 say.	 Be

slay	the	terrible	cock-block	and	victory	shall	be	yours!

Approaching	 a	 woman	 with	 a	 friend,	 or	 a	 few,	 is	 definitely	 more	 difficult

done.	 Just	 remember	 to	 talk	 to	 everyone,	 not	 just	 the	 one	 you	 want—except
when	it	comes	to	those	pesky	cock-blocks,	they	can	be	avoided!

You	can	steer	yourself	in	any	direction	you	choose.
