	Chapter	Twenty-Five

Warm	Approaches

The	core	focus	of	this	entire	book	is	to	emphasize	how	easy	it	can	be	to	meet
women	in	everyday	situations.	No	longer	do	you	have	to	walk	around	aimlessly,
hoping	that	you	stumble	across	a	woman	who	thinks	you’re	“cute.”	Instead,	you
can	go	out	and	start	to	make	things	happen	for	yourself.	If	you	see	a	woman,	and
you	 think	 she's	 cute,	 you	 can	 tell	 her,	 and	 take	 it	 from	 there.	 There	 is	 nothing
stopping	you	from	this!

recommended	 for	 meeting	 more	 women,	 when	 you	 start	 warm-approaching,
you'll	see	just	how	superior	it	really	is.

So	 what	 is	 a	 warm	 approach?	 Well,	 it’s	 definitely	 a	 lot	 milder	 than	 a	 cold
one.	A	warm	approach	is	an	approach	to	a	woman	whom	you	already	know	in
some	 capacity.	 This	 capacity	 can	 vary	 greatly,	 but	 the	 fact	 that	 you	 and	 she
recognize	one	another	makes	the	approach	warm	.

You	might	be	sort-of-friends	with	a	woman,	see	her	out	and	about	one	day
and	decide	you'd	like	to	approach	her	and	get	her	number;	the	fact	that	you	know
her	 would	 make	 it	 a	 warm	 approach.	 Or	 maybe	 you	 see	 a	 woman	 to	 whom
you’ve	 said	 “Hi”	 once	 or	 twice	 in	 class	 or	 at	 work,	 and	 want	 to	 approach	 her
now;	again,	this	would	be	a	warm	approach.	Or	you	might	see	a	hot	friend	of	one
of	your	friends,	someone	you	don’t	know	at	all	but	still	recognize;	again	you'd
be	approaching	her	in	a	warm	manner.	Lastly,	there's	the	woman	you	don’t	know
at	all,	but	you’ve	maybe	at	least	said	“Hi”	to	her	earlier	in	the	night	(assuming
you're	 at	 a	 bar	 or	 in	 a	 similar	 setting);	 if	 you've	 even	 said	 that	 much,	 it	 makes
this	approach	warm	as	well.

For	this	final	example,	you	don’t	know	the	woman	well,	but	you	still	do	to	a
certain	 degree,	 and	 the	 familiarity	 of	 talking	 to	 her	 earlier	 on	 gives	 you	 that
connection,	no	matter	how	minimal	it	is.

Just	 think	 about	 it	 for	 a	 second	 and	 you’ll	 realize	 how	 powerful	 the	 warm
approach	truly	is.	A	woman	at	a	bar	who	has	no	idea	who	you	are	is	much	more
inclined	to	be	hesitant	to	want	to	talk	to	you	when	you	first	approach	her.	Her
guard	is	going	to	be	up	very	high	for	you,	and	for	any	guy	who	tries	to	talk	to
her.

However,	 take	 this	 same	 woman	 and	 change	 the	 approach	 around
completely.	 Instead	 of	 a	 random	 stranger	 walking	 up	 and	 trying	 to	 talk	 to	 her,
she	 sees	 a	 familiar	 face.	 Whether	 you're	 a	 friend,	 an	 acquaintance,	 someone
she’s	only	said	“Hi”	to	or	someone	she	talked	to	briefly	earlier	in	the	night,	your
familiar	 face	 goes	 a	 long	 way	 into	 comforting	 her.	 And	 this	 comfort	 is	 very
important	when	pulling	off	successful	approaches.

As	 humans,	 we	 like	 familiarity:	 familiar	 faces,	 similar	 individuals,	 they
allow	 us	 to	 let	 our	 guards	 down.	 We	 innately	 carry	 a	 sort	 of	 repressed	 fear	 of
strangers,	not	a	deathly	or	panic-stricken	fear,	but	a	fear	nonetheless.	We	don’t
know	what	potential	harm	someone	could	bring	if	we	don't	know	who	they	are.
(This	is	why	it's	so	important	to	try	to	elicit	comfort	when	approaching	a	woman
from	 the	 get-go,	 through	 things	 like	 smiling,	 laughing,	 introducing	 yourself,
mirroring,	 etc.)	 It’s	 always	 a	 thought	 in	 the	 backs	 of	 our	 minds,	 and	 a	 tool	 we
use	 as	 a	 defense	 mechanism.	 With	 a	 warm	 approach,	 however,	 this	 defense
mechanism	is	at	least	partly	shut	off.

Right	 off	 the	 bat	 she'll	 be	 much	 more	 at	 ease	 with	 you	 because	 of	 your
acquaintance,	and	she'll	trust	you	more—what	you	say,	what	you	do,	what	you
suggest,	and	what	you	present	to	her.	She'll	have	a	trust	that	resonates	from	her
subconscious	and	it	will	make	things	much	easier	for	you	initially	.	.	.	and	then,
of	course,	later	on.

Another	truly	great	thing	about	warm	approaches	is	that	it’s	so	much	easier
to	have	a	connection	and	start	a	good	conversation	this	way.	You	won’t	have	to
stumble	for	things	to	say	or	subjects	to	talk	about,	as	you	normally	would	when
you	first	approach	a	woman.	Instead,	you	have	a	commonality	already	in	place,
whether	it’s	a	mutual	friend,	a	class	you	took	together,	a	“How’s	the	night	been
going	since	I	saw	you	last?”	question,	or	the	fact	that	you	actually	are	friends,	in
which	 case	 you	 have	 a	 million	 things	 to	 talk	 about!	 The	 warm-approach
conversations	 are	 so	 much	 smoother	 initially,	 because	 there's	 that	 connection
already	in	place.

How	do	you	maximize	your	efforts	and	get	more	warm	approaches,	you	ask?
Simple;	 start	 putting	 yourself	 in	 situations	 where	 women	 abound.	 That	 means
getting	more	social!	This	is	the	best	way	to	maximize	your	warm	approaches	and
improve	your	dating	life.

Start	 going	 out	 and	 becoming	 more	 active.	 Go	 to	 the	 gym,	 join	 a	 club,
participate	in	a	group,	sign	up	for	a	sport,	join	a	charity,	take	a	class.	All	of	these
things	will	open	the	doors	for	you	to	meet	more	people,	and	this	is	the	name	of
the	 game.	 There	 are	 always	 plenty	 of	 quality	 women	 who	 go	 to	 these	 things,
usually,	some	of	the	best	women	in	fact.	Even	if	you	don’t	“pick	up”	a	woman	at
whatever	activity	or	place	you	two	meet,	you	can	always	pick	her	up	later	on;	it's
inevitable	(especially	if	you	live	in	the	same	general	area)	that	you'll	bump	into
her,	at	the	bar	or	the	grocery	store,	etc.	Then	the	“warm	approach”	comes	into
play.

If	you	don’t	want	to	leave	it	up	to	chance,	however	(I	usually	don’t),	you	can
always	 talk	 to	 a	 woman	 after	 class	 or	 whatever	 activity	 you’re	 doing	 together.
Maybe	it's	not	the	first	day	you	show	up,	if	you	don’t	want	to	make	it	seem	so
much	 like	 you're	 trying	 to	 hit	 on	 her.	 (It	 really	 depends	 on	 the	 situation,	 and
whether	you	know	you'll	be	seeing	her	frequently.)	You	can	always	just	talk	to
her	one	day,	after	a	few	classes.

By	 this	 point,	 it	 will	 again	 be	 a	 warm	 approach,	 because	 of	 the	 familiarity
factor.	 She	 might	 not	 talk	 to	 you	 during	 class,	 and	 she	 might	 not	 even	 really
notice	you	much.	However,	if	you	go	to	the	same	class	(or	whatever	it	is),	and
have	 been	 doing	 so	 for	 some	 time,	 I	 guarantee	 she	 will	 have	 seen	 you	 at	 least
once,	if	not	several	times.	This	alone	will	make	it	a	warm	approach,	and	make
things	so	much	easier	for	you!

Even	 if	 you	 don’t	 meet	 gorgeous	 women	 in	 all	 of	 these	 places	 right	 away,
becoming	more	social	and	making	new	connections	will	open	up	doors	later	on.
The	 more	 friends	 you	 make	 doing	 various	 activities	 like	 the	 ones	 above,	 the
more	chances	you	create	of	being	introduced	to	friends	of	these	friends.

Those	introductions	will	be	some	of	the	very	best	ways	to	meet	women.	If	a
friend	 of	 yours	 (most	 likely	 female)	 introduces	 you	 to	 her	 hot	 friend,	 that	 hot
friend	is	definitely	going	to	be	very	inclined	to	want	to	get	to	know	you.	Your
friend	(and	hers)	is	giving	you	tremendous	social	proof	here,	basically	handing
you	the	keys	to	her	friend’s	vagina!

So	don’t	be	shy	about	befriending	women	to	whom	you’re	not	attracted.	Just
remember	to	keep	it	friendly,	and	not	so	much	sexual.	Don't	give	them	the	wrong
impression	or	lead	them	on;	this	is	just	not	morally	right.	Being	friendly,	though,
and	 actually	 and	 genuinely	 making	 connections	 and	 true	 friendships,	 is
absolutely	worth	it.	It	can	have	more	benefits	than	you	might	think.	Just	be	smart
about	it	and	be	honest	with	them	and	with	yourself.

Use	 these	 tips	 and	 you'll	 take	 your	 game	 to	 a	 whole	 new	 level.	 There	 is
nothing	like	approaching	women,	but	meeting	them	through	warm	approaches	is
literally	 the	 best	 way	 possible!	 Is	 it	 getting	 warm	 in	 here	 .	 .	 .	 or	 is	 it	 just	 your
approach?

"The	true	sign	of	intelligence	is	not	knowledge	but	imagination."

-	Albert	Einstein

	Chapter	Twenty-Six

Mastering	The	Approach

Men	initiating	an	interaction	with	women	has	always	been	(and	always	will
be)	a	fundamental	part	of	courtship.	From	the	ancient	days	until	now,	it’s	been
primarily	up	to	a	man	to	commence	a	possible	connection	between	two	people.

But	 this	 is	 no	 burden	 on	 men	 who	 know	 what	 to	 do.	 In	 fact,	 it’s	 quite	 the
reward	 for	 these	 guys,	 who	 have	 a	 skill	 that	 can	 be	 taught	 and	 harnessed,	 and
one	that’s	being	refined	by	men	all	over	the	world.	What	a	blessing	indeed!

I	 hope	 by	 now	 you	 have	 a	 good	 idea	 about	 what	 it	 takes	 to	 harness	 this
ability	for	meeting	women.	It’s	such	a	valued	skill	to	have.	To	say	it’s	one	of	the
most	important	things	a	man	could	learn	in	life	would	be	an	understatement	in
my	 view.	 It’s	 THE	 most	 important	 skill	 we	 can	 learn.	 It’s	 a	 craft	 of	 true
intelligence:	social	intelligence.

Any	 man	 who	 can	 conquer	 the	 fear	 of	 being	 utterly	 rejected	 by	 another
woman	 (a	 man’s	 number-one	 worst	 fear)	 has	 essentially	 conquered	 life.	 He’s
taken	 the	 worst	 possible	 dread	 and	 instead	 of	 hiding	 from	 it,	 perfected	 it,	 and
used	it	to	his	advantage.

And	what	advantage	is	this?	The	advantage	of	finding	love,	often	considered

the	sole	purpose	for	being	alive!

By	perfecting	approaching,	a	man	is	taking	ahold	of	his	life	and	deciding	to
be	the	controller	of	it.	He	gets	to	choose	what	he	wants	in	life	and	obtain	things
he	desires,	instead	of	waiting	back	and	hoping	or	aimlessly	praying	for	things	to
fall	into	his	lap.	Yes,	approaching	enables	him	and	empowers	him	to	make	his
own	destiny.

It’s	 not	 going	 to	 be	 easy,	 as	 nothing	 in	 life	 worth	 getting	 is.	 It	 will	 take	 a
long	time	to	see	results,	and	a	lot	of	failures	and	hurt	before	you	get	good	at	it.
But	by	now	you	know	that.	And	you	also	know	that	it’s	worth	it.

Falling	or	your	face	at	first	and	struggling	and	getting	rejected	is	all	going	to
happen.	 Remember	 the	 10,000-hour	 rule	 here.	 But	 it’s	 not	 the	 guys	 who	 never

get	rejected	who	do	the	best.	It’s	the	ones	who	get	rejected	over	and	over	again,
who	learn	how	to	deal	with	this,	and	learn	from	their	mistakes.	The	Masters	of
Rejection	is	what	I	like	to	call	them.

Become	a	master	of	rejection	if	you	really	want	to	be	great.	Learn	to	be	okay
with	failing	and	making	mistakes—not	just	in	approaching	women,	but	in	life	in
general.	 Too	 many	 people	 strive	 to	 be	 perfect	 in	 life.	 Worse	 yet,	 too	 many
people	strive	not	to	fail,	and	thus	don't	take	any	chances.	They	sit	back	and	let
life	 pass	 them	 by,	 because	 they're	 too	 worried	 to	 put	 themselves	 out	 there.
Everyone	 has	 this	 mask	 and	 is	 afraid	 to	 take	 it	 off	 and	 show	 the	 world	 what’s
behind	it.	These	are	the	same	people	who	become	saddened	or	depressed	later	in
life,	 because	 they've	 grown	 so	 accustomed	 to	 being	 someone	 they’re	 not.	 How
can	 anyone	 be	 happy	 with	 who	 they	 are,	 if	 who	 they	 are	 really	 isn’t	 who	 they
are?

Take	this	book	and	realize	that	it’s	okay	to	stop	and	talk	to	a	random	woman,
on	the	street	or	at	a	bar,	or	whenever	you	feel	the	urge	to.	Don’t	be	afraid	to	put
yourself	out	there	and	make	things	happen	for	yourself.

Society	has	grown	more	and	more	into	a	legion	of	anti-social	creatures.	It’s
almost	as	if	we’ve	become	sheep	who	line	up	and	silently	go	about	doing	daily
tasks,	 then	 go	 home	 to	 sleep,	 and	 wake	 up	 to	 do	 more	 of	 the	 same.	 Life’s	 so
repetitive	 for	 most	 people.	 Most	 of	 them	 have	 no	 idea	 they’ve	 even	 become
these	sheep-like	creatures,	oblivious	to	what’s	going	on.	God	forbid	if	you	want
to	spice	things	up,	stop	a	woman,	and	actually	be	social;	all	the	other	sheep	will
be	 stunned	 by	 this	 unaccustomed	 action	 from	 what	 they	 perceived	 to	 be	 just
another	sheep!

Well,	don’t	be	just	another	sheep!	Be	someone	who	takes	life	the	way	it	was
intended	to	be	taken:	with	happiness	and	fun.	Enjoy	what	you	do,	and	have	fun
doing	it.	Don’t	fall	in	line	with	all	the	other	sheep	and	get	sucked	into	thinking
as	they	do.	If	normal	was	crazy,	would	you	still	want	to	be	normal?	Of	course
not!

Well,	normal	is	not	really	crazy,	but	it	certainly	is	boring;	do	you	want	to	be
this?	Of	course	you	don’t!	Be	bold,	stand	out,	and	try	your	damnedest	not	to	fit
in.	It’s	good	to	be	unique	in	life—for	society’s	sake,	and	certainly	for	your	own	!

I	can	remember	way	back	when,	many	years	ago,	I’d	been	rejected	by	a	girl
I	really	liked.	Having	absolutely	no	iota	of	'game'	at	the	time,	and	suffering	from

years	 of	 heartache,	 I	 decided	 enough	 was	 enough,	 and	 became	 determined	 to
make	 a	 change.	 I	 didn’t	 know	 how	 at	 the	 time,	 but	 I	 just	 knew	 that	 I'd	 do
something	to	change	the	course	of	my	sad,	lonely,	depressed	life.

That	same	night	I	researched	everything.	Fortunately,	I	was	able	to	stumble
across	 the	 Dating	 Community	 and	 begin	 to	 find	 all	 the	 great	 dating	 coaches
within	 it.	 Devouring	 all	 their	 knowledge,	 and	 realizing	 the	 mistakes	 I’d	 been
making	for	years	and	years,	the	course	of	my	life	was	forever	changed.

I	 remember	 going	 on	 my	 first	 approach	 a	 short	 while	 after	 that,	 and	 being
nervous	as	hell.	Outwardly,	of	course,	I	pretended	to	be	cocky	and	confident,	but
inside	 I	 was	 terrified,	 and	 for	 good	 reason.	 Just	 a	 short	 time	 before,	 I’d	 been
totally	oblivious	to	talking	to	women	and	had	no	idea	what	to	say	or	do.	For	my
whole	 life	 prior	 to	 this,	 talking	 with	 women	 had	 been	 an	 awkward,	 painful
example	 of	 human	 communication.	 Now,	 I	 was	 actually	 pushing	 myself	 into
meeting	 women	 head-on,	 taking	 up	 the	 challenge	 of	 trying	 to	 get	 them	 to	 be
attracted	to	me.

Even	back	then,	I	knew	it	would	be	tough.	I	could	sense	that	it	would	take	a
while	to	get	good	at	and	feel	comfortable	with.	Even	though	I	felt	confident	that
I	could	do	it,	I	just	knew	that	it	wasn’t	going	to	be	easy.	And	it	wasn’t.

That	 first	approach	 I	ever	made	 went	awfully.	I	got	blown	 out	 completely;
the	 rest	 of	 the	 day,	 although	 productive,	 yielded	 little	 to	 no	 positive	 results,
either.	The	next	few	times	after	that	were	no	different.	I	had	failure	after	failure
after	failure.	But	I	also	had	determination,	and	I	never	gave	in.	And	I’m	so	glad	I
didn’t.

Approaching	gave	me	confidence,	both	with	women	and	in	life.	It’s	a	skill
that	 teaches	 you	 how	 to	 communicate	 more	 effectively	 in	 all	 areas.	 It	 teaches
you	 how	 to	 speak	 and	 control	 your	 tone	 of	 voice,	 perfecting	 your	 mannerisms
and	 your	 body	 language.	 More	 importantly,	 though,	 it	 develops	 your	 liveliness
and	energy.

Whenever	you	have	a	good	approach	with	a	woman	you	feel	energized.	Like
a	battery	getting	charged	up,	you	feel	invigorated.	Humans	long	for	this	strong
connection	with	one	another,	and	approaching	women	brings	this	connection	to
life.	It’s	quite	amazing.

Approaching	women	develops	your	overall	character.	It	makes	you	think	in

different	 ways	 and	 be	 more	 attuned	 to	 thinking	 on	 your	 feet	 and	 being	 witty.
You	become	more	fun	and	more	enlightened	through	approaching.	Believe	it	or
not,	you	actually	learn	more	about	yourself	by	talking	with	other	people.	You	get
a	feel	for	who	you	really	are,	without	your	mask	on	and	your	guard	up.	You	find
out	(as	I’ve	seen	in	so	many	guys	I’ve	coached	and	in	myself)	that	you’re	a	lot
more	 complex	 than	 you	 think.	 By	 this	 I	 mean	 there's	 a	 lot	 more	 to	 you:	 skills,
attributes,	qualities,	traits,	and	behaviors	you	have,	that	you	don’t	even	realize.

It’s	 only	 through	 pushing	 yourself,	 uncovering	 some	 of	 these	 layers	 of
“protection,”	that	you	find	things	that	are	truly	amazing	about	yourself.	This	is
why	I	love	approaching.	It	has	given	me	so	much,	and	allowed	me	to	discover	so
much	more	about	myself.

Next	time	you	see	someone	to	whom	you’re	attracted,	don’t	hesitate.

You	see	a	sexy	woman	walking	down	the	street,	and	you	get	that	knee-jerk
reaction	to	stop	in	your	tracks	and	just	admire	another	beauty	walking	by.	You
know	you	don’t	have	a	chance	with	her	so	instead	you	decide	to	just	watch	her
pass	 by	 .	 .	 .	 No,	 not	 this	 time!	 This	 time,	 you	 say	 fuck	 that	 ,	 and	 tell	 yourself
you’re	going	for	it!

You	rush	up	to	her,	as	by	now	she’s	quite	far	away,	and	then	stop	her	mid-
stride.	 You	 deliver	 a	 direct	 line	 about	 how	 you	 feel,	 and	 why	 you	 really
approached	her.	To	your	initial	amazement,	she	loves	it!	She	smiles	and	tells	you
her	 name,	 and	 you	 chat	 for	 a	 few	 minutes,	 actually	 making	 a	 really	 great
connection	 with	 her.	 You	 exchange	 numbers	 and	 make	 plans	 to	 meet	 up	 in	 a
couple	of	days.	You've	taken	hold	of	what	you	want	and	made	it	happen,	instead
of	just	letting	it	happen	for	you.

Choosing	to	live	your	life	this	way	is	choosing	to	live	it	with	happiness	as
the	prime	objective.	You	now	make	things	happen,	and	take	hold	of	your	desires.
You	live	for	you	and	you	alone,	and	you	find	that	people	love	you	for	this!

"Success	is	not	final,	failure	is	not	fatal:
It	is	the	courage	to	continue	that	counts."

-	Winston	Churchill

	Chapter	Twenty-Seven

Not	Trying	In	Life

By	 now	 I	 hope	 you	 realize	 that	 approaching	 women	 is	 not	 just	 about
approaching	women.	It’s	so	much	more	than	going	up	to	a	random	woman	and
deciding	 you’re	 going	 to	 strike	 up	 a	 conversation	 and	 then	 maybe	 seduce	 her.
It’s	about	developing	a	new	mindset	and	perspective	on	life.

You	 see,	 it	 takes	 a	 lot	 of	 courage	 to	 do	 this	 thing	 called	 “approaching.”	 It
takes	guts	that	not	many	guys	have,	or	have	the	nerve	to	acquire.	But	by	doing
this,	you	feel	incredible	about	yourself.	Even	if	you	fail,	you	still	succeed!

Even	if	you	approach	100	women	and	have	absolutely	no	success	at	all	with
them	(which	would	be	nearly	impossible,	even	if	you	tried	to	fail!),	you	still	gain
something	profoundly	important.	You	still	gain	something	so	incredible	and	so
rewarding:	the	feeling	of	being	alive!

Yes,	by	taking	these	chances	in	life—actually	going	out	and	making	things
happen—you	 will	 be	 infinitely	 more	 happy	 than	 if	 you'd	 decided	 to	 stay	 back
and	do	nothing.	Even	if	you	fail!	You	still	feel	amazing,	because	of	the	thrill	and
excitement	 you	 are	 creating.	 This	 is	 what	 life	 is	 all	 about.	 It’s	 all	 about	 being
proactive	and	choosing	to	push	yourself	and	challenge	yourself	in	ways	you've
only	dreamed	of.

Life	is	so	rewarding	when	we	finally	do	things	we	always	wanted	to	do,	but
never	got	the	chance	to.	When	we	overcome	our	fears	and	just	go	for	something,
an	invigorating	euphoria	sweeps	through	our	bodies.	This	doesn’t	just	apply	to
meeting	women,	but	anything	in	life.

No	matter	if	it’s	a	job	you	always	wanted,	a	relationship	you	always	desired,
a	 skill	 you’ve	 always	 had	 the	 urge	 to	 learn	 .	 .	 .	 we	 all	 hold	 back	 from	 doing
different	 things	 in	 our	 lives,	 mostly	 because	 we	 fear	 putting	 in	 the	 necessary
effort	 it	 takes	 to	 accomplish	 said	 task.	 But	 this	 needs	 to	 change.	 This
procrastination	on	life	needs	to	stop	now!

I	truly	believe	we	are	all	here	for	one	reason	or	another.	Every	single	person
on	 this	 planet,	 all	 7	 billion	 of	 us,	 has	 some	 purpose.	 By	 idly	 sitting	 back	 and

letting	time	pass,	watching	the	world	spin	around	without	us	in	it,	we	are	really
just	wasting	our	lives.	We	might	as	well	be	dead,	or	starring	in	some	badly	acted
horror	 movie	 about	 monsters,	 because	 that’s	 what	 we’ve	 become:	 unenergetic,
lifeless	corpses,	breathing	in	oxygen	and	blinking	our	eyes.

For	 some	 reason	 this	 has	 become	 an	 epidemic	 in	 our	 society.	 People	 have
given	 up	 the	 desire	 to	 learn,	 to	 grow,	 and	 to	 push	 themselves	 into	 all	 sorts	 of
new,	exciting	endeavors.	Children	in	schools	care	more	about	looking	cool	than
learning	and	expanding	their	minds.	Men	in	the	workplace	care	more	about	their
paychecks	 than	 actually	 doing	 something	 they	 enjoy.	 Couples	 in	 relationships
care	 more	 about	 being	 not	 being	 single	 than	 finding	 and	 being	 with	 someone
they	truly	love	and	with	whom	they	are	happy.

Friendships	 also	 mean	 little	 nowadays.	 You	 can	 only	 count	 on	 family,	 and
maybe—maybe—	one	best	friend.	So	many	of	our	friends	 now	are	too	busy	to
really	 be	 there	 when	 we	 need	 them.	 This	 is	 not	 to	 say	 they’re	 not	 your	 true
friends,	or	that	they're	not	good	friends	or	great	people,	but	in	our	society	as	it’s
been	shaped	over	the	last	few	decades,	“friendship”	has	taken	on	a	whole	new
meaning.	 (When	 was	 the	 last	 time	 anyone	 had	 over	 500	 friends	 in	 real	 life?
These	days,	everyone	has	at	least	this	many	virtual	ones	online.)

Living	in	this	microwave	world,	where	we	all	want	things	to	be	done	in	30
seconds,	 we	 text	 and	 message	 people	 on	 social	 media,	 thinking	 this	 passes	 for
real-life	interaction.	We	get	up	each	and	every	day	to	check	our	Instagrams	and
Facebooks	and	Twitters.	We	Like,	Comment,	and	Tweet	about	all	sorts	of	things
that	 happen	 throughout	 the	 day:	 all	 the	 boring,	 uninteresting	 occurrences	 from
the	times	between	sleep	get	posted	there.

Nobody	really	cares	about	our	dog	wearing	sunglasses.	Nobody	really	wants
to	know,	“I’m	at	the	doctors	bored	out	of	my	mind!!!”	Nobody	gives	a	shit	about
how	badly	you're	craving	that	extra	large	Mochaccino	from	Dunkin	Donuts	right
now!	And	nobody,	except	maybe	your	spouse	one	day,	ever	will!

Yet	 we	 feel	 compelled	 to	 live	 online,	 rather	 than	 the	 real	 world.	 We	 feel
compelled	to	read	everybody	else’s	stories,	and	stalk	everyone	else’s	pictures	to
see	 what	 everyone	 else	 is	 doing.	 We	 do	 all	 this	 and	 get	 bored	 doing	 it.	 We
actually	 secretly	 despise	 it	 all,	 and	 tell	 everyone	 how	 boring	 and	 stupid	 social
media	 is—yet	 we	 stay	 on	 it.	 We	 can’t	 get	 rid	 of	 it.	 Even	 if	 we	 delete	 our
Facebook	accounts,	we	either	re-activate	it	a	month	later,	or	just	switch	channels

and	hop	onto	Instagram	or	some	other	virtual	platform.	We	cannot	live	without
this	 means	 of	 communication!	 We	 now	 love	 to	 live	 our	 lives	 by	 seeing	 what
everyone	else	is	doing	in	theirs.

We	have	it	completely	backwards.	We	should	be	living	life	the	way	we	want
to,	 not	 how	 everyone	 else	 is.	 We	 should	 start	 focusing	 more	 on	 our	 goals,
experiences,	and	desires,	and	not	give	two	shits	about	those	“friends”	from	our
high-school	who	we’ll	never	really	come	in	contact	with	again.

Why	 waste	 your	 time	 looking	 at	 pictures	 and	 posts	 from	 Bob	 who	 had	 the
same	Spanish	class	as	you,	back	in	junior	year?	Is	Bob	going	to	benefit	you	or
your	life	in	any	way?	No.	Absolutely	not.	I	really	truly	think	it’s	time	we	got	off
the	 social	 media	 drug	 and	 replaced	 it	 with	 real-world	 treatment	 and	 activity.
There's	really	nothing	better	than	living	your	life	in	the	moment	and	taking	in	all
the	beauty	and	splendor	that	it	has	to	offer.

I’m	not	even	a	social	media	nut.	I	just	truly	believe	that	for	many	people	it
takes	up	such	a	huge	amount	of	valuable	time.	Instead	of	wasting	2-4	hours	of
your	 day,	 checking	 and	 commenting	 on	 statuses,	 videos	 and	 pictures,	 why	 not
just	spend	10	minutes	a	day	(at	the	most),	briefly	checking	to	see	if	you	have	any
important	notifications	or	updates	you	need	to	take	care	of,	and	then	calling	it	a
social	 media	 wrap?	 This	 way,	 you	 could	 still	 get	 your	 virtual	 “fix”	 and	 leave
enough	time	to	enjoy	and	actually	participate	in	“real”	life.

It’s	 this	 position	 of	 being	 lazy	 that	 is	 holding	 our	 society	 back	 as	 a	 whole.
It’s	so	much	easier	to	just	mindlessly	scroll	through	Facebook	and	read	statuses
than	it	is	to	read	a	book,	learn	a	new	skill,	or	actually	go	out	and	socialize	with
people.	It’s	so	convenient	and	time-consuming	this	way.	Nobody	wants	to	put	in
the	work	and	make	an	effort.	After	all,	this	isn’t	fun	and	it	isn’t	easy.

But	 it	 must	 be	 done.	 We	 have	 to	 make	 a	 change,	 and	 start	 living	 life	 as	 it
should	 be.	 We	 have	 to	 start	 experiencing	 and	 undertaking	 new	 and	 exciting
activities.	These	endeavors	reward	our	spirits.	They	keep	us	young,	they	keep	us
alive,	and	they	make	life	worth	living!

"Never	let	the	fear	of	striking	out	get	in	your	way."

-	Babe	Ruth

	Chapter	Twenty-Eight

What	To	Say	After	The	Approach

A	 book	 about	 approaching	 women	 wouldn’t	 quite	 be	 complete	 without	 a
chapter	dedicated	to	the	part	immediately	following	the	approach.	A	lot	of	times
guys	get	stuck	after	the	opener,	and	have	absolutely	no	idea	what	to	say.	They
know,	and	have	often	perfected,	that	initial	opening	line,	but	then	they	frequently
crash	and	burn,	stumbling	to	articulate	any	bit	of	known	phonetic	sound.

A	 few	 mumbled	 words	 and	 a	 few	 indiscernible	 auditory	 effects	 later,	 the
woman	 awkwardly	 excuses	 herself	 and	 resumes	 her	 journey.	 All	 too	 often,	 the
guy	 is	 left	 speechless	 (and	 numberless),	 because	 of	 his	 inability	 to	 shift	 away
from	this	initial	approach.

It’s	important	to	know	how	to	transition	away	from	your	opening	lines,	and
get	into	and	maintain	a	good	conversation.	To	know	how	to	do	this,	you	have	to
first	 decide	 which	 approach	 you're	 going	 to	 use.	 For	 example,	 if	 you’re	 going
direct,	 you	 can	 easily	 transition	 from	 your	 opening	 line	 and	 automatically	 get
into	 a	 flirty,	 fun	 sort	 of	 vibe	 with	 the	 woman.	 (Assuming	 of	 course	 that	 she's
receptive	to	your	approach.)

The	transition	from	a	good	direct	opener	is	fairly	easy,	and	requires	only	that
you	know	how	to	start	and	keep	a	good	conversation	flowing,	which	I'll	discuss
shortly.	By	going	direct,	you	let	a	woman	know	you're	into	her,	and	you	can	use
this	to	your	advantage.	That’s	the	beauty	of	going	direct:	you	know	right	away
whether	 or	 not	 a	 woman	 is	 feeling	 you.	 And	 if	 she	 is,	 you	 don't	 need	 to	 waste
time	 dilly-dallying;	 if	 she's	 not,	 you	 can	 just	 move	 on	 to	 the	 next	 woman.
However,	 transitioning	 away	 from	 an	 indirect	 opener	 (I	 should	 say	 doing	 it
successfully)	requires	a	bit	more	finesse.

When	 you	 go	 indirect,	 as	 we’ve	 learned	 earlier,	 you	 surrender	 your	 honest
intentions	 for	 a	 brief	 period	 of	 time.	 Instead	 of	 the	 woman	 knowing	 you’re
approaching	her	because	you	like	her,	you	have	to	actually	feign	interest	in	her
for	a	short	time,	to	keep	up	with	your	justification	for	talking	to	her.	(I	know	it
doesn’t	sound	great,	but	that’s	the	reality	of	the	situation,	and	in	many	cases,	it’s
your	only	chance	at	success.)

Transitioning	 away	 from	 your	 opener,	 whatever	 you	 indirectly	 come	 up
with,	 you	 must	 do	 basically	 one	 of	 two	 things:	 a)	 end	 the	 well-intentioned-
charade	and	come	clean,	telling	her	that	you	think	she’s	attractive;	or	b)	keep	up
with	the	act	for	a	short	while	longer.	(I’ll	be	quite	honest:	the	faster	you	can	get
away	from	your	act,	the	better	off	you're	going	to	be!)

Most	 women	 intuitively	 know	 what	 your	 intentions	 are.	 They	 don’t	 mind
playing	along	with	your	game	for	a	minute	or	so,	and	in	many	cases	they	may
even	applaud	you	for	having	the	guts	to	actually	go	up	to	them	and	chat.	But	if
you	keep	dodging	the	elephant	in	the	room,	the	fact	that	both	of	you	know	why
you're	really	speaking	to	her,	she'll	quickly	lose	all	respect	for	you!	(This	goes
especially	for	boring,	serious,	and	non-playful	guys.)

So	what	can	you	do	to	successfully	get	from	your	indirect	stance	to	a	direct
one,	if	you	can’t	quite	tell	her	right	away	that	you	find	her	attractive?	What	can
you	 say,	 other	 than	 come	 right	 out	 and	 tell	 her	 you	 think	 she’s	 cute?	 What
actually	works	and	is	effective?

Well,	a	few	things	actually	work	quite	well.

Keeping	 the	 conversation	 going	 by	 asking	 her	 another	 indirect	 question	 is
one	way	to	do	it.	If	you	stopped	her	initially	by	asking	some	question,	and	she
answered,	but	you	can’t	quite	muster	the	courage	yet	to	just	tell	her	you	like	her,
ask	 her	 something	 else.	 “Where	 are	 you	 from?”	 can	 work,	 as	 you're	 trying	 to
place	her	local	accent.	Or	ask	her	what	time	she	has,	glancing	at	her	watch,	or
what	 she’s	 been	 up	 to	 that	 day.	 Any	 of	 these	 is	 actually	 quite	 awful	 as	 a
conversation	builder,	but	each	is	effective	for	buying	you	more	precious	time	to
come	up	with	something	better	to	say.

What	might	be	a	little	more	effective	is	telling	her	something	about	herself.
If	you're	stumbling	for	things	to	say	after	opening	her	up,	make	an	observation
about	 something	 you	 see	 on	 her:	 a	 compliment	 on	 her	 outfit,	 an	 assumption
about	 her	 style,	 a	 remark	 on	 her	 energy	 or	 mood	 .	 .	 .	 anything	 related	 to	 these
things.	 Making	 statements	 like	 this	 can	 be	 pretty	 effective	 in	 starting	 a
conversation,	and	oftentimes	it's	enough	to	get	the	ball	rolling.

Making	a	joke	or	making	her	laugh	by	doing	something	goofy	is	perhaps	the
best	way	to	transition	away	from	your	opening	indirect	line.	You	always	want	to
be	 non-threatening	 and	 playful	 when	 approaching	 women	 (and	 when	 hanging
around	women	in	general).	The	best	way	to	convey	this	is	by	making	her	laugh.

This	 can	 be	 a	 little	 difficult	 to	 do,	 but	 in	 the	 next	 chapter	 I’ll	 give	 you	 some
specific	tips	on	how	you	can	be	funnier	and	make	women	laugh.	Just	know	this:
by	making	her	laugh,	you	really	open	up	the	doors	for	great	conversation.

Making	her	smile	is	so	important.	In	fact,	it’s	essential	to	success.	If	you	can
get	 her	 to	 open	 up	 to	 you	 by	 smiling	 (or	 better	 yet	 laughing	 with	 you)	 you're
golden.	 That’s	 why	 this	 means	 of	 transitioning	 away	 from	 your	 opener	 is	 so
damn	effective.	Like	I	said,	it’s	challenging	to	get	down,	but	so	effective	when
you	do!

You	have	to	be	able	to	move	on	effectively	from	your	opening	line,	whether
it’s	direct	or	indirect.	You	need	to	bridge	the	gap	between	you	as	a	stranger,	to
whom	she	doesn’t	feel	comfortable	talking,	to	you	being	a	pleasant	person	she’s
just	met,	with	whom	she	already	feels	at	ease.	It’s	challenging,	of	course,	but	by
practicing	the	aforementioned	transitions	and	learning	the	specific	tips	to	having
a	good	conversation	in	the	following	chapter,	you	can	get	this	down.

Soon	enough,	you	won’t	be	stumbling	for	things	to	say	when	you	meet	new
women.	 You'll	 learn	 how	 to	 converse	 easily	 with	 them	 and	 start	 building
attraction	right	away.	It	will	be	fun	and	easy,	and	you'll	come	to	enjoy	the	gift	of
effectively	communicating	with	the	opposite	sex.

"Every	time	I	see	an	adult	on	a	bicycle,
I	no	longer	despair	for	the	future	of	the	human	race."

-	H.	G.	Wells

	Chapter	Twenty-Nine

Having	Good	Conversations	With	Women

What	do	I	say	next?	I’m	running	out	of	shit	to	say!	I	hope	this	doesn’t	get
awkward	in	a	minute.	If	only	I	could	make	her	laugh	and	be	funny	like	some	of
those	 guys	 on	 T.V.!	 Damn,	 this	 really	 sucks!	 Any	 second	 now,	 she’s	 going	 to
think	I’m	boring	and	walk	away.	.	.	.

These	 are	 just	 some	 of	 the	 thoughts	 that	 go	 through	 the	 heads	 of	 so	 many
guys	when	they're	running	out	of	things	to	say	in	conversations	with	women.	It
typically	goes	great	for	a	little	while:	guys	can	make	women	laugh,	they	can	be
interesting	for	a	brief	time,	and	they	can	even	be	engaging	for	a	moment.	They
have	a	woman	clinging	to	every	word,	like	a	fat	school-boy	clinging	to	his	last
piece	of	cake.

However,	something	inevitably	happens	after	a	short	while.	Like	all	people,
men	do	get	boring.	Their	jokes	dry	up;	the	initial	novel	interest	fades,	and	their
ability	to	be	fun	and	engaging	crashes	faster	than	a	Malaysian	airplane!

If	only	there	was	some	way	to	keep	their	spirits	up,	and	keep	the	vibe	with
the	 woman	 alive.	 If	 only	 there	 was	 a	 way	 to	 build	 and	 maintain	 good
conversations	 with	 women!	 Ah,	 but	 there	 is.	 There	 is	 such	 a	 way,	 and	 I	 will
show	you!

Having	great	conversations	(or	at	least	having	a	woman	think	she's	having	a
great	 conversation)	 comes	 down	 to	 one	 basic	 thing:	 making	 her	 feel	 like	 she's
interesting.	 She	 may	 be	 as	 boring	 as	 a	 bag	 of	 bricks,	 but	 if	 you	 can	 somehow
make	her	feel	like	she’s	the	most	interesting	woman	in	the	world,	she	will	in	turn
feel	like	she’s	had	an	incredible	conversation	with	you.

So	how	do	you	do	this?	How	can	you	make	a	boring	woman,	or	any	woman
for	 that	 matter,	 feel	 like	 she's	 intriguing	 you	 with	 her	 words?	 (After	 all,	 most
women—and	most	men	for	that	matter—actually	are	quite	interesting,	once	you
get	them	talking.	Everyone	has	a	unique	story	to	tell.).

There	are	a	few	things	you	can	do.	For	one,	you	can	be	engaging	yourself.
By	 being	 exciting	 and	 saying	 things	 with	 passion	 and	 energy,	 she	 will	 tend	 to

want	 to	 reciprocate	 and	 match	 your	 energy	 levels.	 Easy	 enough,	 right?	 Yes,	 of
course.

Next	time	you	find	yourself	in	a	conversation	with	someone	else,	whether	a
man	or	a	woman,	observe	the	type	of	energy	and	passion	that	you	have	in	your
responses	or	questions.	Most	of	the	time	we	have	little	to	no	energy,	as	we	like
to	naturally	conserve	it	for	other	things	that	might	pop	up	in	our	lives.

As	 an	 experiment,	 however,	 try	 being	 more	 animated,	 talking	 with	 more
liveliness	to	everyone	you	come	across	today.	Put	an	optimistic	spin	on	whatever
you’re	saying,	and	try	to	inspire	whoever	you	are	speaking	to	with	your	words.
Speak	as	though	you	just	won	$1,000	on	a	scratch	ticket,	and	see	how	the	other
person	responds.

My	 guess	 is	 you'll	 start	 having	 a	 livelier,	 more	 enthusiastic	 dialogue	 with
anyone	 to	 whom	 you're	 speaking.	 You	 can	 then	 translate	 this	 $1,000	 idea	 onto
your	conversations	with	women.	When	they	see	how	much	spirit	you	have	when
you	talk	to	them,	they	will	in	turn	want	to	speak	to	you	the	same	way.	This	is	a
great	first	step	to	boosting	your	conversational	skills.

Another	good	trick	you	can	use	is	to	just	listen	more.	I	know,	sometimes	it’s
tough	 for	 guys	 to	 really	 listen	 to	 women	 and	 what	 they're	 saying.	 This	 is	 why
men	 bond	 better	 with	 other	 men	 when	 they're	 doing	 some	 sort	 of	 activity
together:	 grabbing	 a	 beer,	 shooting	 some	 pool,	 or	 playing	 video	 games.	 We're
not	the	most	social	of	creatures,	and	we	therefore	aren’t	as	socially	adept	as	our
better	halves	are.

Women,	 on	 the	 other	 hand,	 are	 great	 listeners	 and	 easily	 bond	 with	 other
women	by	talking	to	them.	They're	much	better	at	communicating	their	thoughts
and	feelings	and	sharing	their	emotions	than	guys.	Women	are	therefore	a	little
offended	when	guys	have	a	tougher	time	keeping	up	with	what	they're	saying	in
their	 conversations	 and	 really	 connecting	 with	 them.	 That's	 not	 to	 say	 it’s	 not
possible,	but	it	does	require	a	little	more	effort	for	men	to	keep	up	with	women
socially.

One	 way	 to	 have	 a	 better	 conversation	 and	 become	 a	 better	 listener	 is	 to
actually	 let	 the	 woman	 do	 the	 leading	 in	 the	 conversation.	 As	 we	 all	 know,
women	love	talking,	so	why	not	let	them?	It	takes	the	pressure	off	us	to	come	up
with	things	to	say,	and	it	also	plays	into	what	they	naturally	love	doing	anyway.
By	letting	them	do	most	of	the	talking,	and	just	sort	of	standing	back	and	letting

them	go	on,	we	really	kill	two	birds	with	one	stone!

There's	nothing	more	effective	for	great	conversations	than	letting	the	other
person	 speak.	 It’s	 not	 just	 women	 here,	 but	 all	 of	 us	 human	 beings,	 who	 love
hearing	 ourselves	 speak	 and	 passing	 our	 thoughts	 onto	 others.	 It’s	 just	 human
nature.

As	far	as	actually	listening	to	women,	the	best	way	is	to	try	to	pick	certain
things	 out	 of	 what	 they're	 saying.	 Hopefully,	 different	 things	 that	 seem
interesting	 or	 somewhat	 appealing	 to	 you	 will	 jump	 out	 when	 she's	 talking.
When	this	happens,	learn	to	hold	on	to	them,	and	keep	them	ready	for	when	she
finishes	whatever	she	is	saying.	Rather	than	having	a	blank,	empty	pause	in	the
conversation,	casually	bring	up	one	of	the	things	she	spoke	about.	It’s	really	that
easy.

In	fact,	this	is	how	all	good	conversations	operate.	Someone	says	something,
and	 during	 that	 person’s	 speech	 all	 sorts	 of	 possible	 topics	 pop	 up.	 The	 other
person	then	responds,	either	with	a	statement	or	a	question,	related	to	something
just	said.	That’s	it.

One	 final	 technique	 for	 keeping	 conversations	 alive	 and	 healthy	 is	 to	 ask
open-ended	 questions,	 and	 make	 open-ended	 statements	 about	 things	 that	 are
being	said.	Rather	than	just	asking	a	yes-no	question,	you	want	to	ask	a	woman
questions	 requiring	 some	 thought,	 and	 make	 her	 dig	 into	 different	 parts	 of	 her
brain.	This	way,	you	really	have	her	thinking	about	things	and	sharing	this	time,
thinking	and	being	creative	with	you.

In	fact,	let	me	make	it	even	less	complicated	than	that.	Here’s	an	example:	A

man	tells	a	woman	she's	cute	and	asks	her	name.

“Thanks.	I'm	Julianne.”

“Cool.	I'm	Bob,	nice	to	meet	you.”

“Thanks!”	She	walks	off,	never	to	be	heard	from	again.

A	second	man	also	tells	the	woman	she's	cute	but	instead	of	asking	for	her
name,	 he	 tells	 her	 he	 wants	 to	 guess	 it.	 She	 laughs	 and	 says,	 “Okay!”	 He	 then
rattles	 off	 three	 or	 four	 different,	 very	 girly,	 feminine	 names.	 She	 smiles	 and
laughs,	and	says	“You’re	way	off!”

“Don't	tell	me,”	he	says,	“Just	give	me	a	hint!”	She	obliges,	and	after	a	few

minutes	of	more	hints	(and	laughs	and	smiles),	he	finally	guesses	her	name.	Of
course	by	now	the	name	doesn’t	even	matter;	he	has	this	woman	totally	craving
more	of	him.	He	can	say	anything	at	this	point	and	be	well	off.

Do	 you	 see	 the	 difference?	 The	 first	 guy	 didn’t	 leave	 any	 opening	 for	 the
conversation	 to	 go	 on.	 He	 asked	 a	 question,	 the	 woman	 answered,	 and	 the
discussion	was	over.	But	the	second	guy	actually	does	a	few	really	great	things.
Not	 only	 does	 he	 leave	 himself	 an	 opening	 in	 the	 beginning	 to	 continue	 the
conversation	by	making	an	open-ended	statement,	he	also	gets	her	talking	right
away.	He	takes	things	she	says	and	goes	with	them,	and	builds	the	conversation
from	there.

He	also	does	one	more	really	important	thing:	he	flirts	with	her,	and	makes
her	laugh.	This,	above	anything	else,	will	make	any	conversation	with	a	woman
awesome!	Being	funny	and	flirty	is	perhaps	the	greatest	tool	in	all	conversations
with	women.	You	don’t	have	to	be	super	charismatic	or	super	funny	by	nature	to
be	 able	 to	 make	 women	 laugh,	 or	 to	 flirt	 with	 them	 either.	 This	 is	 a
misconception.	Not	everyone	can	be	as	funny	as	Chris	Rock	or	Robin	Williams.
These	 guys	 are	 just	 naturally	 funny	 people.	 But	 everyone,	 and	 I	 do	 mean
everyone,	can	make	a	woman	laugh.

Being	funny	is	actually	fairly	easy	when	you	have	the	right	attitude:	a	fun,
playfully	teasing	approach.	You	want	to	tease	her	a	little	about	all	sorts	of	things,
just	 as	 grade	 school	 boys	 and	 girls	 do.	 Even	 when	 they	 grow	 up	 from	 being
grade	school	girls,	women	still	love	this	sort	of	teasing	behavior	that	was	done	to
them	 when	 they	 were	 little.	 And	 guys	 still	 love	 being	 that	 teasing	 young	 boy
they	used	to	be;	they	oftentimes	just	forget	how	fun	it	actually	was.	By	bringing
this	attitude	back,	though,	you	can	make	women	laugh	again.

Being	 sarcastic	 is	 at	 times	 really	 good	 for	 lightening	 the	 mood.	 Grossly
exaggerating	different,	obvious	things	is	also	great.	Coming	up	with	a	blatantly
obvious	fib,	about	something	you	both	know	isn't	true,	is	also	great.	All	of	these
things	 can	 be	 awesome	 for	 making	 a	 woman	 laugh	 and	 keeping	 conversations
animated.

It’s	 important	 to	 note	 that	 most,	 if	 not	 all	 of	 your	 teasing,	 or	 your	 other
techniques	 for	 being	 humorous,	 should	 almost	 always	 come	 with	 a	 smile	 or
smirk	 on	 your	 face.	 This	 lets	 the	 woman	 know	 that	 you're	 just	 kidding	 and
messing	 around,	 and	 that	 you	 should	 not	 be	 taken	 seriously.	 They	 should	 also

always	be	done	with	a	“playful	voice”	instead	of	your	normal	speaking	voice,	or
this	might	not	come	across	the	way	you	intend	it	to.

With	 that	 said,	 use	 all	 of	 these	 things	 freely.	 Women	 love	 to	 laugh	 and	 it
keeps	them	engaged	in	the	interaction.	By	combining	all	of	these	tips,	your	next
conversation	 with	 women	 should	 be	 exceptionally	 fun	 and	 engaging,	 and	 you
should	never,	ever,	run	out	of	things	to	say!

"Nothing	can	stop	the	man
With	the	right	mental	attitude	from	achieving	his	goal;
Nothing	on	earth	can	help	the	man	with	the	wrong	mental	attitude."

-	Thomas	Jefferson

	Chapter	Thirty

Catcalls	vs.	Approaches

Catcalls	are	for	assholes.	It’s	really	as	simple	as	that.	If	you	make	catcalls	at
women,	you're	a	douchebag.	You	should	be	locked	in	a	guillotine	and	publicly
smacked	by	as	many	women	as	possible	for	48	straight	hours.

What’s	 wrong	 with	 catcalls,	 you	 ask?	 Everything.	 They're	 offensive	 to	 the
women	for	whom	they	are	intended.	They're	obnoxious	to	the	rest	of	the	public
who	hears	them.	They're	not	amusing	to	anyone	but	the	catcaller	(and	maybe	his
obnoxious	 friends).	 And	 lastly,	 they	 ruin	 the	 chances	 for	 good,	 respectable,
quality	men	who	actually	want	to	talk	to	this	woman	at	a	future	time.

There	was	this	young	woman	who	recently	filmed	herself	in	New	York	City
after	 constantly	 being	 harassed	 by	 men	 just	 for	 walking	 down	 the	 street.	 She
decided	she	wanted	everyone	to	know	the	daily	harassment	she	endured,	from	all
sorts	of	assholes	who	had	nothing	tangible	to	say	other	than	things	like	“Damn,
Mami!”	and	“You’re	hot,	girl!”	and	“What’s	your	name,	sexy?”

Any	one	of	these	things	could	be	said	to	a	woman	in	conversation	under	the
right	circumstance	(except	maybe	the	“Mami”	one;	I	don’t	think	that	would	ever
really	work,	at	least	not	for	me).	The	problem	with	all	of	these	things	is	that	not
one	of	them	was	actually	done	in	a	respectable,	polite	fashion.

Just	because	you	want	to	appear	confident	when	you	“spit”	game	to	a	girl,	it
doesn’t	 mean	 you	 have	 to	 be	 rude.	 Not	 one	 of	 the	 guys	 in	 the	 video	 actually
approached	 the	 woman	 with	 any	 respect.	 They	 all	 in	 one	 way	 or	 another	 just
shouted	things	out	to	her	as	she'd	already	passed	them,	or	even	from	behind	her.
Not	one	person	ever	said	“Excuse	me!”	“Sorry	to	bother	you”	or	“Hi,	my	name
is	.	.	.”	or	anything	resembling	the	sort.

None	of	these	men	even	approached	her	from	in	front.	They	all	seemed	like
creeps	in	her	peripheral,	and	a	lot	of	them	then	got	really	offended	when	she	paid
them	no	mind.	But	can	you	really	blame	her?	This	woman	filmed	something	like
10	 hours	 worth	 of	 herself	 walking	 around	 NYC	 all	 alone,	 and	 got	 over	 100
catcalls	 from	 men.	 And	 (from	 what	 we	 can	 see	 in	 the	 video)	 not	 one	 of	 these

men	actually	showed	her	any	respect	or	decency,	and	actually	looked	her	in	the
eye	and	from	the	front.

Now	 I’m	 sure	 there	 were	 a	 lot	 of	 decent	 guys	 in	 the	 video	 who	 where
misrepresented	as	being	jerks	or	douches.	I’m	sure	out	of	the	100	guys,	at	least
half	of	them	are	really	good	guys	deep	down.	But	the	fact	of	the	matter	is,	all	of
them	failed	to	show	it.	Their	approach	to	going	up	to	this	attractive	woman	was
way	off.	And	somebody	has	to	let	them	know.

This	woman,	who	wasn’t	even	dressed	up	or	wearing	much	make-up	at	all,
got	 over	 100	 catcalls.	 That’s	 one	 man	 being	 disrespectful	 to	 her	 every	 six
minutes.	 That’s	 pretty	 bad.	 She	 wasn’t	 wearing	 anything	 incredibly	 sexy,	 and
she	 certainly	 wasn’t	 a	 super-model,	 just	 a	 pretty	 average-looking	 woman.
Imagine	how	many	other	women	have	to	go	through	this	same	thing.	My	guess
is	almost	every	single	woman	out	there	faces	something	similar	on	a	day-today
basis.	This	is	why	it's	so	hard	for	decent	guys	to	go	up	and	approach	other	decent
women.	These	catcalling	idiots	are	ruining	it	for	the	rest	of	us!

If	you	really	want	to	approach	a	woman,	then	really	approach	her!	Walk	up
to	her	from	in	front,	where	she	can	see	you,	and	where	she'll	feel	less	threatened.
Then,	actually	say	something	substantial.	Don’t	shout	some	wiseass	thing	from
behind	 her,	 after	 she	 passes	 you.	 These	 off-hand	 comments,	 and	 attempts	 at
being	slick	and	bold,	are	futile	and	they	make	you	look	like	an	imbecile.	They'll
never	work	for	wooing	a	woman.	No	woman	in	the	history	of	mankind	has	ever
been	 seduced	 by	 someone	 who	 shouted,	 “Damn,	 Mami!”	 from	 50	 feet	 behind
her!	It	just	doesn’t	work.	And	it	never	will.

I	 read	 a	 comment	 online	 from	 one	 of	 the	 people	 who	 agreed	 with	 this
woman.	She	said	that	for	any	guy	wondering	how	this	woman,	and	other	women
like	 her,	 feel	 when	 guys	 catcall	 at	 them,	 it’s	 like	 the	 guy	 who	 tries	 to	 sell	 you
stuff	 on	 the	 street.	 Usually	 it’s	 something	 like	 a	 mix-tape	 or	 some	 other	 shitty
work	 of	 art	 you’re	 not	 interested	 in.	 This	 guy,	 who	 just	 bothers	 person	 after
person	 without	 any	 regard	 for	 personal	 boundaries	 and	 without	 thinking	 about
their	respect,	just	blindly	tries	to	push	his	shit	onto	you.

“No,	I	don’t	want	your	shitty	mix-tape,	and	I	never	will.	Stop	trying	to	sell
me	that	crap.	Leave	me	alone!”	This	is	exactly	the	sentiment	brought	to	women,
by	these	guys	who	blindly	try	hitting	on	them	in	the	street.	“Stop	trying	to	sell
sex	 to	 these	 women	 this	 way.	 They	 don’t	 want	 it	 and	 they	 never	 will.”	 Your

approach	is	way	off	if	you	do	this,	so	stop	doing	it!

Approaching	is	one	thing.	It's	a	great	way	to	meet	women	for	quality	guys.	It
is	 respectable	 and	 enjoyable,	 and	 oftentimes	 leads	 to	 something	 special.	 Many
great	 guys	 meet	 many	 great	 women	 by	 going	 up	 and	 talking	 to	 them—on	 the
street	during	the	day,	at	the	bar	at	night,	or	at	some	sort	of	function	or	party.

Men	 going	 up	 to	 women,	 introducing	 themselves	 and	 getting	 to	 know
women	 is	 customary	 in	 our	 society.	 It’s	 been	 done	 for	 thousands	 of	 years	 and
will	be	done	for	many	thousands	more,	if	not	forever.	Meeting	women	this	way
is	perfectly	acceptable.	I	recommend	it,	as	a	dating	coach,	an	author,	and	a	man
who	knows	firsthand	what	it	takes	to	approach	women.

Catcalling,	 on	 the	 other	 hand,	 must	 end.	 It's	 a	 stain	 on	 the	 respectable
practice	 of	 approaching	 women	 and	 it	 gives	 a	 lot	 of	 good	 men	 a	 bad	 name.
Catcallers	everywhere:	Do	everyone	a	favor	and	stop	being	a	dick!

"I	have	been	impressed	with	the	urgency	of	doing.
Knowing	is	not	enough;	we	must	apply.
Being	willing	is	not	enough;	we	must	do."

-	Leonardo	da	Vinci

	Chapter	Thirty-One

Beyond	The	Numbers

When	I	first	began	writing	this	book,	the	ending	was	originally	intended	to
be	 a	 brief	 overview	 of	 everything	 we	 covered	 earlier.	 However,	 this	 has
changed.

I	 didn’t	 want	 the	 finality	 to	 be	 some	 hashed-up,	 ordinary,	 feel-good
conclusion.	I	think	those	shitty	end-of-the-book	chapters	suck	royally,	and	take
away	from	the	rest	of	the	story.	Not	to	mention,	when	I	initially	wrote	the	first,
incredibly	 rough	 and	 rugged	 draft	 to	 this	 book,	 I	 was	 still	 single	 and	 meeting
women	regularly.

My	views,	like	that	of	all	people,	have	somewhat	changed,	and	even	evolved
from	that	time.	My	main	points	have	stayed	the	same,	and	they	always	will	for
that	 matter,	 but	 in	 general	 a	 lot	 of	 my	 positions	 and	 perspectives	 have	 shifted.
How	 could	 they	 not?	 I'm	 no	 longer	 going	 out	 on	 multiple	 dates	 a	 week	 and
sleeping	 with	 a	 ton	 of	 women.	 I	 now	 have	 one	 woman,	 so	 I	 can’t	 really	 speak
from	that	standpoint	anymore.

With	that	said,	I	had	to	fix	and	reshape	a	lot	of	this	book	to	make	it	fit	my
current	outlook	on	life.	What	you’ve	read	is	the	best	of	both	worlds.	It	gives	you
the	 perspective	 of	 my	 single,	 approaching	 life,	 and	 the	 best	 parts	 of	 that,	 and
now	 my	 committed	 life,	 and	 my	 take	 on	 approaching,	 and	 how	 it	 led	 to	 my
happily	dedicated	life	as	it	is	today.

It	really	couldn’t	get	any	better.

Ultimately,	 the	 only	 thing	 anyone	 actually	 wants	 in	 life	 is	 to	 love	 and	 be
loved	 .	 That’s	 it.	 Approaching	 gives	 you	 the	 tool	 to	 obtain	 this.	 I	 used	 what	 I
learned	from	approaching	and	was	able	to	transform	my	entire	life!	That’s	why	I
believe	in	 it	so	 much.	I	never	loved	failing	or	going	up	to	a	woman	and	being
rejected;	however,	I	did	love	the	feeling	I	got	knowing	that	I	was	getting	better
and	 better	 each	 time	 I	 did	 it.	 I	 loved	 watching	 myself	 get	 more	 confident,	 and
feeling	more	and	more	women	being	attracted	to	me,	each	and	every	day.

Finally,	I	love	that	it’s	been	able	to	find	me	someone	I	love,	and	who	loves

me	 back.	 I	 now	 have	 life’s	 greatest	 gift:	 unconditional	 love	 for	 someone	 who
unconditionally	loves	me	back.	That’s	the	only	thing	that	really,	truly	matters	in
life!

So	without	further	ado,	here’s	my	better	ending:

It’s	10:30	a.m.	on	a	Sunday,	and	I	can’t	sleep.	My	thoughts	keep	racing,	with
a	million	ideas	shooting	off	like	fire-crackers	in	my	head.	That’s	customary	for
me	 and	 I	 recognize	 this	 familiar	 feeling.	 I	 get	 it	 every	 so	 often,	 and	 by	 now	 I
know	exactly	what	it	means.

“But	Goddammit,	I’m	so	tired	and	I	just	want	to	go	to	sleep!	Fuck	my	life!”
I	say	in	my	head.	I	don’t	feel	like	doing	what	I	know	I	have	to.	I	roll	around	a
few	times	and	try	to	induce	myself	into	a	subconscious	coma.

After	 a	 few	 minutes	 of	 ultimate	 struggle	 I	 give	 in	 and	 say	 aloud,	 “Fuck	 it!

I’ll	do	it!”	I	slowly	roll	over	and	reluctantly	drag	myself	out	of	bed.

I	 walk	 over	 to	 my	 livelihood,	 my	 HP	 Pavilion	 laptop,	 and	 open	 it	 up.	 My
entire	business	runs	on	this	little	machine,	and	it’s	through	this	device	that	I’ve
been	able	to	capture	all	of	my	brilliant	and	not-so-brilliant	ideas!

As	much	as	I	love	this	instrument,	I	currently	loathe	the	hell	out	of	it!	I	sit
down	 and	 open	 up	 Microsoft	 Word	 and	 briefly	 scroll	 through	 my	 writing.	 I
shake	my	head	in	dismay,	not	necessarily	because	of	any	disdain	for	what	I've
written,	but	because	of	what	I	know	I'll	do	next.

And	then	I	do	it.	As	much	as	it	pains	me,	I	do	it.

I	hit	the	“Control”	key	.	.	.	the	letter	“A”	.	.	.	and	finally	.	.	.	the	“Backspace”
button,	 and	 in	 an	 instant	 all	 of	 my	 2,264	 words	 vanish.	 Gone	 forever.	 Nothing
remains	but	a	blank,	untouched,	New	Word	Document.	A	shiver	courses	through
my	spine,	but	I	know	it’s	for	the	better.	The	final	chapter	was	okay,	but	I	didn’t
love	it,	and	I	knew	I'd	been	awoken	by	this	intermittent	insomnia	for	a	reason.

As	much	as	I	hate	it,	my	sleepless-mind	was	telling	me	something.	And	that

something	was	a	better	ending.	.	.	.

I	begin	etching	out	the	new	conclusion,	words	seamlessly	pouring	from	my
neurons	to	my	fingers	to	my	computer	screen.	I	rattle	off	sentence	after	sentence
and	paragraph	after	paragraph,	and	I’m	delighted	with	what	I	see.	I	can	tell	how
much	better	this	is,	and	I’m	getting	excited	just	thinking	about	it.

Some	 time	 later,	 hearing	 a	 rustling	 sound,	 I	 glance	 over	 my	 shoulder	 onto
the	bed	I’d	departed	before.	I	see	a	beautiful	blonde	woman	rolling	onto	the	side
I‘d	 occupied	 earlier.	 She's	 unbelievably	 sexy,	 even	 as	 she	 lies	 there,	 her	 long
blonde	hair	draping	down	over	her	silky	soft	skin.	Her	facial	features,	perfect	in
symmetry	 and	 splendor,	 glisten	 from	 the	 glow	 of	 my	 screen.	 She	 seems	 to	 be
smiling	even	though	she’s	asleep,	reminding	me	of	how	funny	and	attractive	her
personality	is.	I	admire	the	beauty	in	her	as	I	stare	at	this	woman	for	what	seems
like	hours.	My	girlfriend,	my	absolute	dream	girl!

Ironically,	 as	 I	 write	 of	 how	 amazing	 she	 is,	 as	 if	 reading	 my	 mind,	 she
awakes	and	looks	over	at	me.	She	smiles	and	tells	me	to	finish	up	soon,	because
she	 wants	 to	 snuggle.	 But	 then	 she	 adds,	 “Take	 your	 time	 though,	 Babe,	 you
know	 I’m	 just	 kidding;	 I	 don’t	 want	 you	 to	 rush	 at	 all!	 But	 make	 sure	 you
snuggle	with	me	when	you	finish!”	And	she	smiles	and	rolls	back	onto	her	side
and	into	slumber.

“I’ll	be	right	over,	Sexy!”	I	say	softly,	knowing	full-well	that	only	I	can	hear
myself	at	this	point.	I	briefly	think	of	the	conclusion	to	my	life’s	journey	up	until
this	 moment.	 This	 is	 one	 approach	 I	 don’t	 have	 to	 worry	 about.	 This	 woman
loves	me	to	death,	and	I'm	so	grateful	for	it.

I	conclude	my	tale	by	snuggling	up	with	her	warm,	smooth,	flawless	body.
We're	both	naked	and	I	can	feel	her	skin	caress	against	my	own.	Her	body	is	so
comforting	and	relaxing	as	I	embrace	it.	It’s	amazing.

I	dream	about	being	alone,	about	being	depressed,	about	having	no	friends,
about	 having	 no	 girlfriends,	 and	 about	 being	 awful	 with	 women.	 It	 must	 be
because	of	my	brain’s	stimulation	from	my	earlier	writing.	These	thoughts	pop
back	up	in	the	form	of	dreams.

I'm	back	in	school,	walking	down	a	long	dark	hall.	The	lights	are	flickering
and	it	seems	eerily	quiet.	There’s	no	one	around	but	me.	I	keep	walking,	hoping
to	 get	 to	 class,	 but	 then	 I	 see	 a	 pretty	 girl	 with	 long	 dark	 hair.	 She’s	 very
beautiful,	and	I	go	up	to	her	to	say	hi.	As	I	get	closer	and	closer,	I	realize	that
this	 girl	 is	 very	 pretty,	 but	 there's	 something	 about	 her	 that’s	 not	 right.	 I	 don’t
know	what	it	is,	but	something	is	just	off.	It’s	only	after	I	get	close	enough	to	say
“Hi”	that	I	realize	this	girl	is	not	what	she	seemed	from	afar.

tells	me	she	does	not	mean	well.	I	actually	get	pretty	frightened	for	a	moment	as
I	see	the	crazed	look	on	her	face!

She	doesn’t	say	anything	more	after	I	say	“Hi,”	instead,	she	just	laughs.	She
has	a	loud,	devilish,	and	terrifying	laugh,	one	that	scares	me	to	death!	I	quickly
turn	around	and	bolt	down	the	hall,	fear	running	through	every	part	of	my	veins.
This	woman	is	no	woman	at	all,	but	some	sort	of	demon	or	monster!	I	turn	down
all	 sorts	 of	 different	 corridors,	 slamming	 the	 doors	 shut	 behind	 me	 as	 I	 pass
them,	trying	desperately	to	get	as	far	away	from	this	wicked	creature	as	possible!

I	 run	 until	 I'm	 out	 of	 breath,	 and	 bend	 over	 to	 catch	 myself	 for	 a	 moment.
Exhausted,	I	have	little	energy	left	to	do	more	trekking.	When	I	look	up,	I'm	in	a
huge	city	with	towering	buildings	and	skyscrapers	all	around	me.	I	look	over	to
my	left	and	see	a	woman	only	a	few	yards	away.	I	walk	over	and	say	something
to	her.	I	don’t	know	what	it	is,	but	apparently	I've	said	something	she	likes.	She
starts	laughing	and	smiling	and	enjoying	herself	with	me.

We	have	a	great	conversation	about	something	and	are	both	vibing	with	one
another.	We	seem	to	have	known	each	other	for	years	because	we	keep	naturally
talking	about	more	and	more	interesting	topics.

And	then,	I	look	at	her,	and	I	realize	just	how	beautiful	this	woman	actually

is!

She	 has	 the	 face	 of	 an	 angel,	 with	 beautiful,	 blue,	 mystifying	 eyes,	 long,
blonde	Goldilocks-hair,	and	a	smile	which	shows	her	perfectly	pearly	white	teeth
and	accentuates	the	rest	of	her	pretty	face.

I	am	immediately	in	love	with	this	woman.	And	she	is	in	love	with	me.

The	next	thing	I	know	I	go	in	to	kiss	her,	and	am	greeted	with	her	sexy,	soft
lips	on	mine.	The	feeling	is	magnetic,	and	it	seems	to	invigorate	every	bone	in
my	 body.	 This	 kiss	 sends	 electricity	 throughout	 my	 entire	 frame.	 My	 heart
pumps	like	never	before.

I	kiss	her	more	and	more,	and	I	seem	to	be	filled	with	more	and	more	love.	I

continue	for	a	moment	.	.	.	until	.	.	.	suddenly	.	.	.

I'm	hit	by	a	blinding	light,	and	I	realize	I'm	in	a	completely	different	place.
My	lips	have	just	been	on	my	girlfriend’s,	and	she	smiles	at	me	as	she	kisses	me

again.	I'm	back	in	my	room	with	my	beautiful	girl!

It	takes	me	a	few	seconds	to	come	to	my	senses	and	return	to	the	present.

“It’s	so	good	to	be	back	from	that	dream	,”	I	think	to	myself.	“So	good	to	be
back	in	reality	.	”	Then	I	realize	it:	I’ve	never	really	left	reality.	This	is	my	life
now.	I’ve	learned	to	overcome	so	much	in	life,	and	I've	ended	up	finding	heaven
on	earth.

I	 learned	 how	 to	 approach,	 and	 ended	 up	 meeting	 my	 very	 own	 beautiful

angel!	I	love	my	life,	my	girlfriend,	and	everything	I	do.

Is	 approaching	 women	 everything?	 Of	 course	 not!	 But	 is	 it	 pretty	 fucking

awesome?	I'd	say	so!

“There	is	always	someone	or	something	better	out	there
If	we’re	not	accepted	or	wanted	by	someone	or	something.
Life	is	perfect	in	this	way.
It	weeds	out	the	things	that	are	not	meant	to	be,
And	gives	us	something	better	in	the	end.”

-	Justin	Stenstrom
